88.	Wa qa_la mu_sa_ rabbana_ innaka a_taita fir'auna wa mala'ahu_ zinataw wa amwa_lan fil haya_tid dunya_, rabbana_ liyudillu_ 'an sabilik(a), rabbana-tmis 'ala_ amwa_lihim wa-sydud 'ala_ qulu_bihim fala_ yu'minu_ hatta_ yarawul 'aza_bal alim(a).
89.	Qa_la qad ujibad da'watukuma_ fa-staqima_ wa la_ tattabi'a_nni sabilal lazina la_ ya'lamu_n(a).
90.	Wa ja_wazna_ bi bani isra_'ilal bahra fa atba'ahum fir'aunu wa junu_dahu_ bagyaw wa'adwa_(n), hatta_ iza_  adrakahul garaqu qa_la a_mantu annahu_ la_ ila_ha illal lazi  a_manat bihi banu_ isra_'ila wa ana minal muslimin(a).
91.	_l'a_na wa qad 'asaita qablu wa kunta minal mufsidin(a).
92.	Fal yauma nunajjika bi badanika litaku_na liman khalfaka a_yah(tan), wa inna kasiram minan na_si 'an a_ya_tina_ laga_filu_n(a).
93.	Wa laqad bawwa'na_ bani isra_'ila mubawwa'a sidqiw wa razaqna_hum minat tayyiba_t(i), fama-khtalafu_ hatta_ ja_'ahumul 'ilm(u), inna rabbaka yaqdi bainahum yaumal qiya_mati fima_ ka_nu_  fihi yakhtalifu_n(a).
94.	Fa in kunta fi syakkim mimma_ anzalna_ ilaika fas'alil lazina yaqra'u_nal kita_ba min qablik(a), laqad ja_'akal haqqu mir rabbika fala_ taku_nanna minal mumtarin(a).
95.	Wa la_ taku_nanna minal lazina kazzabu_ bi a_ya_tilla_hi fa taku_na minal kha_sirin(a).
96.	Innal lazina haqqat 'alaihim kalimatu rabbika la_ yu'minu_n(a).
97.	Wa lau ja_'athum kullu a_yatin hatta_ yarawul 'aza_bal alim(a).
98.	Fa lau la_ ka_nat qaryatun a_manat fa nafa'aha_ ima_nuha_ illa_ qauma yu_nus(a), lamma_ a_manu_ kasyafna_ 'anhum 'aza_bal khizyi fil haya_tid dunya_ wa matta'na_hum ila_ hin(in).
99.	Wa lau sya_'a rabbuka la'a_mana man fil ardi kulluhum jami'a_(n), afa anta tukrihun na_sa hatta_ yaku_nu_ mu'minin(a).
100.	Wa ma_ ka_na li nafsin an tu'mina illa_ bi iznilla_h(i), wa yaj'alur rijsa 'alal lazina la_ ya'qilu_n(a).
101.	Qul-inzuru_ ma_za_ fis  sama_wa_ti wal ard(i), wa ma_ tugnil a_ya_tu wan nuzuru 'an qaumil la_ yu'minu_n(a).
102.	Fa hal yantaziru_na illa_ misla ayya_mil lazina khalau min qablihim, qul fantaziru_ inni ma'akum minal muntazirin(a).
103.	Summa nunajji rusulana_ wallazina a_manu_ kaza_lik(a), haqqan 'alaina_ nunjil mu'minin(a).
104.	Qul ya_ ayyuhan na_su in kuntum fi syakkim min dini fala_ a'budul lazina ta'budu_na min du_nilla_hi wa la_kin a'budulla_hal lazi yatawaffa_kum, wa umirtu an aku_na minal mu'minin(a).
105.	Wa an aqim wajhaka lid dini hanifa_(n), wa la_ taku_nanna minal musyrikin(a).
106.	Wa la_ tad'u_na min du_nilla_hi  ma_ la_ yanfa'uka wa la_ yadurruk(a), fa in fa'alta fa innaka izam minaz za_limin(a).
107.	Wa iy yamsaskalla_hu bi durrin fala_ ka_syifa lahu_ illa_ huw(a), wa iy yuridka  bi khairin fala_ ra_dda lifadlih(i), yusibu bihi may yasya_'u min 'iba_dih(i), wa huwal gafu_rur rahim(u).
108.	Qul ya_ ayyuhan na_su qad ja_'akumul haqqu mir rabbikum, faman-ihtada_ fa innama_ yahtadi li nafsih(i), wa man dalla fa innama_ yadillu 'alaiha_, wa ma_ ana 'alaikum bi wakil(in).
109.	Wa-ttabi' ma_ yu_ha_ ilaika wa-sbir hatta_ yahkumalla_h(u), wa huwa khairul ha_kimin(a).
.EndTopic
;___________________
.Topic qsHud " 11. Hud"
1.	Alif La_m Ra_, kita_bun uhkimat  a_ya_tuhu_ summa fussilat mil ladun hakimin khabir(in).
2.	Alla_ ta'budu_ illalla_h(a), innani lakum minhu naziruw wa  basyir(uw),-
3.	Wa an-istagfiru_ rabbakum summa tu_bu_ ilaihi yumatti'kum mata_'an hasanan ila_ ajalim musammaw wa yu'ti kulla zi fadlin fadlah(u_), wa in tawallau fa inni akha_fu 'alaikum 'aza_ba yamin  kabir(in).
4.	Ilalla_hi marji'ukum, wa huwa  'ala_ kulli syai'in qadir(un).
5.	Ala_ innahum yasnu_na sudu_rahum  liyastakhfu_ minh(u), ala_ hina yastagsyu_na siya_bahum, ya'lamu ma_ yusirru_na wa ma_  yu'linu_n(a), innahu_ 'alimum bi za_tis sudu_r(i).
6.	Wa ma_ min da_bbatin fil ardi illa_ 'alalla_hi rizquha_ wa ya'lamu mustaqarraha_ wa mustauda'aha_, kullun fi kita_bim mubin(in).
7.	Wa huwal lazi khalaqas sama_wa_ti wal arda fi sittati ayya_miw wa ka_na 'arsyuhu_ 'alal ma_'i liyabluwakum ayyukum ahsanu 'amala_(n), wa la'in qulta innakum mabu'u_su_na mim ba'dil mauti layaqu_lannal lazina kafaru_ in ha_za_ illa_ sihrum mubin(un).
8.	Wa la'in akhkharna_ 'anhumul'aza_ba ila_ ummatin ma'du_datil layaqu_lunna ma_ yahbisuh(u_), ala_ yauma ya'tihim laisa masru_fan 'anhum wa ha_qa bihim ma_ ka_nu_ bihi yastahzi'u_n(a).
9.	Wa la'in azaqnal insa_na minna_ rahmatan summa naza'na_ka minh(u), innahu_ laya'u_sun kafu_r(un).
10.	Wa la'in azaqna_hu na'ma_'a ba'da darra_'a massathu layaqu_lanna zahabas sayyia 'a_tu 'anni, innahu_ lafarihun fakhu_r(un),
11.	Illal lazina sabaru_ wa 'amilus sa_liha_t(i), ula_'ika lahum magfiratuw wa ajrun kabir(un).
12.	Fa la'allaka ta_rikum ba'da ma_ yu_hu_ ilaika da_'iqum bihi sadruka ay yaqu_lu_ lau la_ unzila 'alaihi kanzun au ja_'a ma'ahu_ malak(un), innama_ anta nazir(un), walla_hu 'ala_ kulli syai'iw wakil(un).
13.	Am yaqu_lu_na-ftara_h(u), qul fa'tu_ bi 'asyri suwarim mislihi muftaraya_ tiw wa-d'u_ man-istata'tum min du_nilla_hi in kuntum sa_diqin(a).
14.	Fa illam yastajibu_ lakum fa'lamu_ annama_ unzila bi 'ilmilla_hi wa alla_ ila_ha illa_ huw(a), fahal antum muslimu_n(a).
15.	Man ka_na yuridul haya_tad dunya_ wa zinataha_ nuwaffi ilaihim a'ma_lahum fiha_ wa hum fiha_ la_ yubkhasu_n(a).
16.	Ula_'ikal lazina laisa lahum fil a_khirati illan na_r(u), wa habita ma_ sana'u_ fiha_ wa ba_tilum ma_ ka_nu_ ya'malu_n(a).
17.	Afaman ka_na 'ala_ bayyinatim mir rabbihi wa yatlu_hu sya_hidum minhu wa min qablihi kita_bu mu_sa_ ima_maw wa rahmah(tan), ula_'ika yu'minu_na bih(i), wa may yakfur bihi minal ahza_bi fan na_ru mau'iduhu_ fala_ taku fi miryatim minhu innahul haqqu mir rabbika wa la_kinna aksaran na_si la_ yu'minu_n(a).
18.	Wa man azlamu mim man-iftara_ 'alalla_hi kaziba_(n), ulu_'ika yu'radu_na 'ala_ rabbihim wa yaqu_lul asyha_du ha_'ula_'il lazina kazabu_ 'ala_ rabbihim, ala_ la'natulla_hi 'alaz za_limin(a),
19.	Allazina yasuddu_na 'an sabililla_hi wa yabgu_naha_ 'iwaja_(n), wa hum bil a_khirati hum ka_firu_n(a).
20.	Ula_'ika lam yaku_nu_ mu'jizina fil ardi wa ma_ ka_na lahum min du_nilla_hi min auliya_'(a), yuda_'afu laumul 'aza_b(u), ma_ ka_nu_ yastati'u_nas sam'a wa ma_ ka_nu_ yubsiru_n(a).
21.	Ula_'ikal lazina khasiru_ anfusahum wa dalla 'anhum ma_ ka_nu_ yaftaru_n(a).
22.	La_ jarama annahum fila a_khirati humul akhsaru_n(a).
23.	Innal lazina a_manu_ wa 'amilus sa_liha_ti wa akhbatu_ ila_ rabbihim, ula_'ika asha_bul jannah(ti), hum fiha_ kha_lidu_n(a).
24.	Masalul fariqaini kal a'ma_ wal asammi wal basiri was sami'(i), hal yastawiya_ni masala_(n), afala_ tazakkaru_n(a).
25.	Wa laqad arsalna_ nu_han ila_ qaumihi inni lakum nazirum mubin(un),
26.	Alla_ ta'budu_ illalla_h(a), inni akha_fu 'alaikum 'aza_ba yaumin alim(in).
27.	Fa qa_lal mala'ul lazina kafaru_ min qaumihi ma_ nara_ka illa_ basyaram mislana_ wa ma_ nara_ka-ttaba'aka illal lazina hum ara_ziluna_ ba_diyar ra'y(i), wa ma_ nara_ lakum 'alaina_ min fadlim bal nazunnukum ka_zibin(a).
28.	Qa_la ya_ qaumi ara'aitum in kuntu 'ala_ bayyinatim mir rabbi wa a_ta_ni rahmatam min 'indihi fa 'ummiyat 'alaikum, anulzimukumu_ha_ wa antum lahu_ ka_rihu_n(a).
29.	Wa ya_ qaumi la_ as'alukum 'alaihi ma_la_(n), in ajriya illa_ 'alalla_hi wa ma_ ana bita_ridil lazina a_manu_, innahum mula_qu_ rabbihim wa la_kinni ara_kum qauman tajhalu_n(a).
30.	Wa ya_ qaumi may yansuruni minalla_hi in tarattuhum, afala_ tazakkaru_n(a).
31.	Wa la_ aqu_lu lakum 'indi khaza_'inulla_hi wa la_ a'lamul gaiba wa la_ aqu_lu inni malakuw wa la_ aqu_lu lillazina tazdari a'yunukum lay yu'tiyahumulla_hu khaira_(n), alla_hu a'lamu bima_ fi anfusihim, inni izal laminaz za_limin(a).
32.	Qa_lu_ ya_ nu_hu qad ja_daltana_ fa aksarta jida_lana_ fa'tina_ bima_ ta'iduna_ in kunta minas sa_diqin(a).
33.	Qa_la innama_ ya'tikum bihilla_hu in sya_'a wa ma_ antum bi mu'jizin(a).
34.	Wa la_ yanfa'ukum nushi in arattu an ansaha lakum in ka_nalla_hu yuridu ay yugwiyakum, huwa rabbukum, wa ilaihi turja'u_n(a).
35.	Am yaqu_lu_na-ftara_h(u), qul in-iftaraituhu_ fa 'alayya ijra_mi wa ana bari'um mimma_ tujrimu_n(a).
36.	Wa u_hiya ila_ nu_hin annahu_ lay yu'mina min qaumika illa_  man qad a_mana fala_ tabta'is bima_ ka_nu_ yaf'alu_n(a).
37.	Wa-sna'il fulka bi a'yunina_ wa wahyina_ wa la_ tukha_tibni fil lazina zalamu_ innahum mugraqu_n(a).
38.	Wa yasna'ul fulk(a), wa kullama_ marra 'alaihi mala'um min qaumihi sakhiru_ minh(u), qa_la in taskharu_ minna_ fa inna_ naskharu minkum kama_ taskharu_n(a).
39.	Fa saufa ta'lamu_n(a), may ya'tihi 'aza_buy yukhzihi wa yahillu 'alaihi 'aza_bum muqim(un).
40.	Hatta_ iza_ ja_'a amruna_ wafa_rat tannu_r(u), qulna-hmil fiha_ min kullin zaujaini-snaini wa ahlaka illa_ man sabaqa 'alaihil qaulu wa man a_man(a), wa ma_ a_mana ma'ahu_ illa_ qalil(un).
41.	Wa qa_la_rkabu_ fiha_ bismilla_hi majreha_ wa mursa_ha_, inna rabbi lagafu_rur rahim(un).
42.	Wa hiya tajri bihim fi maujin kal jiba_l(i), wa nu_da_ nu_hun-ibnahu_ wa ka_na fi ma'ziliy ya_ bunayya-rkam ma'ana_ wa la_ takum ma'al ka_firin(a).
43.	Qa_la sa a_wi ila_ jabaliy ya'simuni minal ma_'(i), qa_la la_ 'a_simal yauma min amrilla_hi illa_ mar rahim(a), wa ha_la bainahumal mauju faka_na minal mugraqin(a).
44.	Wa qila ya_ ardu_bla'i ma_'aki wa ya_ sama_'u aqli'i wa gidal ma_'u wa qudiyal amru wa-stawat 'alal ju_diyyi wa qila bu'dal lil qaumiz za_limin(a).
45.	Wa na_da_ nu_hur rabbahu_ faqa_la rabbi inna_bni min ahli, wa inna wa'dakal haqqu wa anta ahkamul ha_kimin(a).
46.	Qa_la ya_ nu_hu innahu_ laisa min ahlik(a), innahu_ 'amalun gairu sa_lihin fala_ tas'alni ma_ laisa laka bihi 'ilm(un), inni a'izuka an taku_na minal ja_hilin(a).
47.	Qa_la rabbi inni a'u_zu bika an as'alaka ma_ laisa li bihi 'ilm(un), wa illa_ tagfir li wa tarhamni akum minal kha_sirin(a).
48.	Qila ya_ nu_hu-hbit bi sala_mim minna_ wa baraka_tin 'alaika wa 'ala_ umamim mimmam ma'ak(a), wa umamun sanumatti'uhum summa yamassuhum minna_ 'aza_bun alim(un).
49.	Tilka min amba_'il gaibi nu_hiha_ ilaik(a), ma_ kunta ta'lamuha_ anta wa la_ qaumuka min qabli ha_za_, fa-sbir, innal 'a_qibata lil muttaqin(a).
50.	Wa ila_ 'a_din akha_hum hu_da_(n), qa_la ya_ qaumi'budulla_ha ma_ lakum min ila_hin gairuh(u_), in antumilla_ muftaru_n(a).
51.	Ya_ qaumi la_ as'alukum 'alaihi ajra_(n), in ajriya illa_ 'alal lazi fatarani, afala_ ta'qilu_n(a).
52.	Wa ya_ qaumi-stagfiru_ rabbakum summa tu_bu_ ilaihi yursilis sama_'a 'alaikum midra_raw wa yazidkum quwwatan ila_ quwwatikum wa la_ tatawallau mujrimin(a).
53.	Qa_lu_ ya_ hu_du ma_ ji'tana_ bi bayyinatiw wa ma_ nahnu bi ta_riki a_lihatina_ 'an qaulika wa ma_ nahnu laka bi mu'minin(a).
54.	In naqu_lu illa-'tara_ka ba'du a_lihatina_ bi su_'(in), qa_la inni usyhidulla_ha wa-syhadu_ anni bari'um mimma_ tusyriku_n(a).
55.	Min du_nihi fa kidu_ni jami'an summa la_ tunziru_n(i).
56.	Inni tawakkaltu 'alalla_hi rabbi wa rabbikum, ma_ min da_bbatin illa_ huwa a_khizum bi na_siyatiha_, inna rabbi 'ala_ sira_tim mustaqim(in).
57.	Fa in tawallau faqad ablagtukum ma_ ursiltu bihi ilaikum, wa yastakhlifu rabbi qauman gairakum, wa la_ tadurru_nahu_ syaia'a_(n), inna rabbi 'ala_ kulli syai'in hafiz(un).
58.	Wa lamma_ ja_'a amruna_ najjaina_ hu_daw wallazina a_manu_ ma'ahu_ bi rahmatim minna_, wa najjaina_hum min 'aza_bin galiz(in).
59.	Wa tilka 'a_d(un), jahadu_ bi a_ya_ti rabbihim wa 'asau rusulahu_ wa-ttaba'u_ amra kulli jabba_rin 'anid(in).
60.	Wa utbi'u_ fi ha_zihid dunya_ la'nataw wa yaumal qiya_mah(ti), ala_ inna 'a_dan kafaru_ rabbahum, ala_ bu'dal li 'a_din qaumi hu_d(in).
61.	Wa ila_ samu_da akha_hum sa_liha_(n), qa_la ya_ qaumi-'budulla_ha ma_ lakum min ila_hin gairuh(u_), huwa ansya'akum minal ardi wa-sta'marakum fiha_ fa-stagfiru_hu summa tu_bu_ ilaih(i), inna rabbi qaribum mujib(un).
62.	Qa_lu_ ya_ sa_lihu qad kunta fina_ marjuwwan qabla ha_za_ atanha_na_ an na'buda ma_  ya'budu a_ba_'una_ wa innana_ lafi syakkim mimma_ tad'u_na_ ilaihi murib(in).
63.	Qa_la ya_ qaumi ara'aitum in kuntu 'ala_ bayyinatim mir rabbi, wa a_ta_ni minhu rahmatan famay yansuruni minalla_hi in 'asaituh(u_), fama_ tazidu_nani gaira takhsir(in).
64.	Wa ya_ qaumi ha_zihi na_qatulla_hi lakum a_yatan fazaru_ha_ ta'kul fi ardilla_hi wa la_ tamassu_ha_ bi su_'in faya'khuzakum 'aza_bun qarib(un).
65.	Fa 'aqaru_ha_ fa qa_la tamatta'u_ fi da_rikum sala_sata ayya_m(in), za_lika wa'dun gaira makzu_b(in).
66.	Falamma_ ja_'a amruna_ najjaina_ sa_lihaw wallazina a_manu_ ma'ahu_ birahmatim minnu_ wa min khizyi yaumi'iz(in), inna rabbaka huwal qawiyyul 'aziz(u).
67.	Wa akhazal lazina zalamus saihatu fa asbahu_ fi diya_rihim ja_simin(a),
68.	Ka allam yagnau fiha_, ala_ inna samu_da kafaru_ rabbahum, ala_ bu'dal lisamu_d(a).
69.	Wa laqad ja_'at rusuluna_ ibra_hima bil busyra_ qa_lu_  sala_ma_(n), qa_la sala_mun fama_ labisa an ja_'a bi 'ijlin haniz(in).
70.	Falamma_ ra'a_ aidiyahum la_ tasilu ilaihi nakirahum wa aujasa minhum khifah(tan), qa_lu_ la_ takhaf inna_ ursilna_ ila_ qaumi lu_t(in).
71.	Wa-mra'atuhu_ qa_'imatun fa dahikat fa basysyarna_ha_ bi isha_q(a), wa miw wara_'i isha_qa ya'qu_b(a).
72.	Qa_lat ya_ wailata_ a'alidu wa ana 'aju_zuw wa ha_za_ ba'li syaikha_(n), inna ha_za_ lasyai'un 'ajib(un).
73.	Qa_lu_ ata'jabina min amrilla_hi rahmatulla_hi wa baraka_tuh(u_), 'alaikum ahlal  bait(i), innahu_ hamidum majid(un).
74.	Falamma_ zahaba 'an ibra_himar rau'u wa ja_'athul busyra_  yuja_diluna_ fi qaumi lu_t(in).
75.	Inna ibra_hima lahalimun awwa_hum munib(un).
76.	Ya_ ibra_himu a'rid 'an ha_za_, innahu_ qad ja_'a amru rabbik(a), wa innahum a_tihim 'aza_bun gairu mardu_d(in).
77.	Wa lamma_ ja_'at rusuluna_ lu_tan si'a bihim wa da_qa bihim zar'aw wa qa_la ha_za_  yaumun 'asib(un).
78.	Wa ja_'ahu_ qaumuhu_ yuhra'u_na ilaih(i), wa min qablu ka_nu_  ya'malu_ nas sayyi'a_t(i), qa_la ya_ qaumi ha_'ula_'i bana_ti hunna atharu lakum fa-ttaqulla_ha wa la_ tukhzu_ni fi daifi, alaisa minkum rajulur rasyid(un).
79.	Qa_lu_ laqad 'alimta ma_ lana_ fi bana_tika min haqq(in), wa innaka lata'lamu ma_ nurid(u).
80.	Qa_la lau anna li bikum quwwatan au a_wi ila_ ruknin syadid(in).
81.	Qa_lu_ ya_ lu_tu inna_ rusulu rabbika lay yasilu_ ilaika fa asri bi ahlika bi qit'im minal laili wa la_ yaltafit minkum ahadun illa-mra'atak(a), innahu_ musibuha_ ma_ asa_bahum, inna mau'idahumus subh(u), alaisas subhu bi qarib(in).
82.	Falamma_ ja_'a amruna_ ja'alna_ 'a_liyaha_ sa_filaha_ wa amtarna_ 'alaiha_ hija_ratam min  sijjilim mandu_d(in).
83.	Musawwamatan 'inda rabbik(a), wa ma_ hiya minaz za_limina bi ba'id(in).
84.	Wa ila_ madyana akha_hum syu'aiba_(n), qa_la ya_ qaumi-'budulla_ha ma_ lakum min ila_hin gairuh(u_), wa la_ tanqusul mikya_la wal miza_na inni ara_kum bi khairiw wa inni akha_fu 'alaikum 'aza_ba yaumim muhit(in).
85.	Wa ya_ qaumi auful mikya_la wal miza_na bil qisti wa la_ tabkhasun na_sa asy-ya_'ahum wa la_ ta'sau fil ardi mufsidin(a).
86.	Baqiyyatulla_hi khairul lakum in kuntum mu'minin(a), wa ma_ ana 'alaikum bi hafiz(in).
87.	Qa_lu_ ya_ syu'aibu asala_tuka ta'muruka an natruka ma_  ya'budu a_ba_'una_ au an naf'ala fi amwa_lina_ ma_ nasyu_'(u), innaka la antal halimur rasyid(u).
88.	Qa_la ya_ qaumi ara'aitum in kuntu 'ala_ bayyinatim mir rabbi wa razaqani minhu rizqan hasanaw wa ma_ uridu an ukha_lifakum ila_ ma_ anha_kum 'anh(u), in uridu illal isla_ha ma-stata't(u), wa ma_ taufiqi illa_ billa_h(i), 'alaihi tawakkaltu wa ilaihi unib(u).
89.	Wa ya_ qaumi la_ yajrimannakum syiqa_qi ay yusibakum mislu ma_ asa_ba qauma nu_hin au qauma hu_din au qauma sa_lih(in), wa ma_ qaumu lu_tim minkum bi ba'id(in).
90.	Wa-stagfiru_ rabbakum summa tu_bu_ ilaih(i), inna rabbi rahimuw wadu_d(un).
91.	Qa_lu_ ya_ syu'aibu ma_ nafqahu kasiram mimma_ taqu_lu wa inna_ lanara_ka fina_ da'ifa_(n), wa lau la_ rahtuka larajamna_k(a), wa ma_ anta 'alaina_ bi 'aziz(in).
92.	Qa_la ya_ qaumi arahti a'azzu 'alaikum minalla_h(i), wa-ttakhaztumu_hu wara_'akum zihriyya_(n), inna rabbi bima_  ta'malu_na muhit)un).
93.	Wa ya_ qaumi-'malu_ 'ala_ maka_natikum inni 'a_mil(un), saufa ta'lamu_n(a), may ya'tihi 'aza_buy yukhzihi wa man huwa ka_zib(un), wa-rtaqibu_ inni ma'akum raqib(un).
94.	Wa lamma_ ja_'a amruna_ najjaina_ syu'aibaw wallazina a_manu_ ma'ahu_ birahmatim minna_, wa akhazatil lazina zalamus saihatu fa asbahu_ fi diya_rihim ja_simin(a).
95.	Ka allam yagnau fiha_, ala_  bu'dal li madyana kama_ ba'idat samu_d(u).
96.	Wa laqad arsalna_ mu_sa_ bi a_ya_tina_ wa sulta_nim mubin(in),
97.	Ila_ fir'auna wa mala'ihi fa- ttaba'u_ amra fir'aun(a), wa ma_ amru fir'auna bi rasyid(in).
98.	Yaqdumu qaumahu_ yaumal qiya_mati fa auradahumun na_r(a), wa bi'sal wirdul mauru_d(u).
99.	Wa utbi'u_ fi ha_zihi la'natau wa yaumal qiya_mah(ti), bi'sar rifdul marfu_d(u).
100.	Za_lika min amba_'il qura_ naqussuhu_ 'alaika minha_ qa_'imuw wa hasid(un).
101.	Wa ma_ zalamna_hum wa la_kin zalamu_ anfusahum fama_ agnat a_lihatuhumul lati yad'u_na min du_nilla_hi min syai'il lamma_ ja_'a amru rabbik(a), wa ma_ za_du_hum gaira tatbib(in).
102.	Wa kaza_lika akhzu rabbika iza_ akhazal qura_ wa hiya za_limah(tun), inna akhzahu_ alimun syadid(un).
103.	Inna fi za_lika la a_yatal liman kha_fa 'aza_bal a_khirah(ti), za_lika yaumum majmu_'(ul), lahun na_su wa  za_lika yaumum masyhu_d(un).
104.	Wa ma_ nu'akhkhiruhu_ illa_ li ajalim ma'du_d(in).
105.	Yauma ya'ti la_ takallamu nafsun illa_ bi iznih(i), fa minhum syaqiyyuw wa sa'id(un).
106.	Fa ammal lazina syaqu_ fa fin na_ri lahum fiha_ zafiruw wa syahiq(un),
107.	Kha_lidina fiha_ ma_ da_matis sama_wa_tu wal ardu illa_ ma_ sya_'a rabbuk(a), inna rabbaka fa''a_lul lima_ yurid(u).
108.	Wa ammal lazina su'idu_ fa fil jannati kha_lidina fiha_ ma_ da_matis sama_wa_tu wal ardu illa_ ma_ sya_'a rabbuk(a), 'ata_'an gaira majzu_z(in).
109.	Fala_ taku fi miryatim mimma_ ya'budu ha_'ula_'(i), ma_ ya'budu_na illa_ kama_ ya'budu a_ba_'uhum min qabl(au), wa inna_ lamuwaffu_hum nasibahum gaira manqu_s(in).
110.	Wa laqad a_taina_ mu_sal kita_ba fa-khtulifa fih(i), wa lau la_ kalimatun sabaqat mir rabbika laqudiya bainahum, wa innahum lafi syakkim minhu murib(in).
111.	Wa inna kullal lamma_ layuwaffiyannahum rabbuka a'ma_lahum, innahu_ bima_ ya'malu_na khabir(un).
112.	Fa-staqim kama_ umirta wa man ta_ba ma'aka wa la_  tatgau, innahu_ bima_ ta'malu_na basir(un).
113.	Wa la_ tarkanu_ ilal lazina zalamu_ fatamassakumun na_r(u), wa ma_ lakum min du_nilla_hi min auliya_'a  summa la_ tunsaru_n(a).
114.	Wa aqimis sala_ta tarafayin naha_ri wa zulafam minal lail(i), innal hasana_ti yuzhibnas sayyi'a_t(i), za_lika zikra_ liz  za_kirin(a).
115.	Wa-sbir fa innalla_ha la_ yudi'u ajral muhsinin(a).
116.	Fa lau la_ ka_na minal quru_ni min qablikum ulu_ baqiyyatiy yanhauna 'anil fasa_di fil ardi illa_ qalilam mimman anjaina_ minhum, wa-ttaba'al  lazina zalamu_ ma_ utrifu_ fihi wa ka_nu_ mujrimin(a).
117.	W a ma_ ka_na rabbuka liyuhlikal qura_ bi zulmiw wa ahluha_ muslihu_n(a).
118.	Wa lau sya_'a rabbuka laja'alan na_sa ummataw wa_hidataw wa la_ yaza_lu_na  mukhtalifin(a),
119.	Illa_ mar rahima rabbuk(a), wa liza_lika khalaqahum, wa tammat kalimatu rabbika la'amla'anna jahannama minal jinnati wan na_si ajma'in(a).
120.	Wa kullan naqussu 'alaika min amba_'ir rusuli ma_ nusabbitu bihi fu'a_daka wa ja_'aka fi ha_zihil haqqu wa  mau'izatuw wa zikra lil mu'minin(a).
121.	Wa qul lillazina la_ yu'mina_na-'malu_ 'ala_ maka_natikum, inna_ 'a_miulu_n(a).
122.	Wa-ntaziru_, inna_  muntaziru_n(a).
123.	Wa lilla_hi gaibus sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa ilaihi yurja'ul amru kulluhu_ fa-'budhu wa tawakkal 'alaih(i), wa ma_ rabbuka bi ga_filin 'amma_ ta'malu_n(a).
.EndTopic
;______________________
.Topic qsYusuf " 12. Yusuf"
1.	Alif La_m Ra_, tilka a_ya_tul kita_bil mubin(i).
2.	Inna_ anzalna_hu qur'a_nan 'arabiyyal la'allakum ta'qila_n(a).
3.	Nahnu naqussu 'alaika ahsanal qasasi bima_ auhaina_ ilaika ha_zal qur'a_n(a), wa in kunta min qablihi laminal ga_filin(a).
4.	Iz qa_la ya_sufu li abihi ya_ abati inni ra'aitu ahada'asyara kaukabaw wasy syamsa wal qamara ra'aituhum li sa_jidin(a).
5.	Qa_la ya_ bunayya la_ taqsus ru'ya_ka 'ala_ ikhwatika fa yakidu laka kaida_(n), innasy syaita_na lil insa_ni 'aduwwum  mubin(un).
6.	Wa kaza_lika yajtabika rabbuka wa yu'allimuka min ta'wilil aha_disi wa yutimmu ni'matahu_'alaika wa 'ala_ a_li ya'qu_ba kama_ atammaha_ 'ala_ abawaika min qablu ibra_hima wa isha_q(a), inna ibra_hima 'alimun hakim(un).
7.	Laqad ka_na fi yu_sufa wa  ikhwatihi a_ya_tul lis sa_'ilin(a).
8.	Iz qa_lu_ layu_sufu wa akhu_hu ahabbu ila_ abina_ wa nahnu 'usbah(tun), inna aba_na_ lafi dala_lim mubin(in),
9.	Uqtulu_ yu_sufa aw-itrahu_hu arday yakhlu lakum wajhu abikum wa taku_nu_ mim ba'dihi qauman sa_lihin(a).
10.	Qa_la qa_'ilum minhum la_ taqtulu_ yu_sufa wa alqu_hu fi  gaya_batil jubbi yaltaqithu ba'dus sayya_rati in kuntum  fa_'ilin(a).
11.	Qa_lu_ ya_ aba_na_ ma_ laka la_  ta'manna_ 'ala_ yu_sufa wa inna_  lahu_ lana_sihu_n(a).
12.	Arsilhu ma'ana_ gaday yarta' wa yal'ab wa inna_ lahu_  laha_fizu_n(a).
13.	Qa_la inni layahzununi an tazhabu_ bihi wa akha_fu ay  ya'kulahuz zi'bu wa antum 'anhu ga_filu_n(a).
14.	Qa_lu_ la'in akalahuz zi'bu wa nahnu 'usbatun inna_ izal  lakhaa_siru_n(a).
15.	Falamma_ zahabu_ bihi wa ajma'u_ ay yaj'alu_hu fi gaya_batil jubb(i), wa auhaina_ ilaihi latunabbi'annahum bi amrihim ha_za_ wa hum la_ yasy'uru_n(a).
16.	Wa ja_'u_ aba_hum 'isya_'ay yabku_n(a).
17.	Qa_lu_ ya_ aba_na_ inna_ zahabna_  nastabiqu wa tarakna_ yu_sufa 'inda mata_'ina_ fa akalahuz  zi'b(u), wa ma_ anta bimu'minil lana_ wa lau kunna_  sa_diqin(a).
18.	Wa ja_'u_ 'ala_ qamisihi bi  damin kazib(in), qa_la bal sawwalat lakum anfusukum amra_(n), fa sabrun jamil(un), walla_hul  musta'a_nu 'ala_ ma_ tasifu_n(a).
19.	Wa ja_'at sayya_ratun fa arsal_a wa_ridahum fa adla_ dalwah(a_), qa_la ya_ busyra_ ha_za_ gula_m(un), wa asarru_hu bida_'ah(tan), walla_hu  'alimum bima_ ya'malu_n(a).
20.	Wa syarauhu bi samanim bakhsin dara_hima  ma'du_dah(tin), wa ka_na_ fihi  minaz za_hidin(a).
21.	Wa qa_lal lazi-sytara_hu mim misra li-mra'atihi akrimi maswa_hu 'asa_ ay yanfa'ana_ au nattakhizahu_ walada_(n), wa  kaza_lika makkanna_ liyu_sufa fil ard(i), wa linu'allimahu_  min ta'wilil aha_dis(i), walla_hu ga_libun 'ala_ amrihi wa la_kinna aksaran na_si la_ ya'lamu_n(a).
22.	Wa lamma_ balaga asyuddahu_ a_taina_hu hukmaw wa 'ilma_(n), wa kaza_lika najzil muhsinin(a).
23.	Wa ra_wadathul lati huwa fi baitiha_ 'an nafsihi wa gallaqatil abwa_ba wa qa_lat haita lak(a), qa_la ma'a_zalla_hi innahu_ rabbi  ahsana maswa_y(a), innahu_ la_  yuflihuz za_limu_n(a).
24.	Wa laqad hammat bihi wa hamma biha_, lau la_ ar ra'a_ burha_na rabbih(i), kaza_lika linasrifa 'anhus su_'a wal fahsya_'(a), innahu_ min 'iba_dinal mukhlasin(a).
25.	Wa-stabaqal ba_ba wa qaddat  qamisahu_ min duburiw wa alfaya_ sayyidaha_ ladal ba_b(i), qa_lat ma_ jaza_'u man ara_da bi ahlika su_'an illaa_  ay yusjana au 'aza_bun alim(un).
26.	Qa_la hiya ra_wadatni 'an nafsi wa syahida sya_hidum  min ahliha_, in ka_na qamisuha_ qudda min qubulin fa sadaqat wa huwa minal ka_zibin(a).
27.	Wa in ka_na qamisuhu_ qudda min duburin fa kazabat wa huwa minas sa_diqin(a).
28.	Falamma_ ra'a_ qamisahu_ qudda min duburin qa_la innahu_ min kaidikunn(a), inna   kaidakunna 'azim(un).
29.	Yu_sufu a'rid 'an ha_za_ wa-stagfiri lizambik(i), innaki kunti minal  kha_ti'in(a).
30.	Wa qa_la niswatun fil  madinati-mra'atul 'azizi tura_widu fata_ha_ 'an nafsih(i), qad syagafaha_ hubba_(n), inna_ lanara_ha fi dala_lim mubin(in).
31.	Falamma_ sami'at bi makrihinna arsalat ilaihinna wa a'tadat lahunna muttaka'aw wa a_tat kullawa_hidatim minhunna sikkinaw wa qa_at-ikhruj 'alaihinn(a), falamma_ ra'ainahu_ akbarnahu_ wa qatta'na aidiyahunn(a), wa qulna ha_sya lilla_hi ma_ ha_za_ basyara_(n), in ha_za_ illa_  malakun karim(un).
32.	Qa_lat faza_likunnal lazi  lumtunnani fih(i), wa laqad ra_wattuhu_ 'an nafsihi fa-sta'sam(a), wa la'il lam yaf'al ma_ a_muruhu_ layusjananna wa layaku_nam minas sa_girin(a).
33.	Qa_la rabbis sijnu ahabbu ilayya mimma_ yad'u_nani  ilaih(i), wa illa_ tasrif 'anni kaidahunna asbu ilaihinna wa akum minal ja_hilin(a).
34.	Fa-staja_ba lahu_ rabbuhu_  fasarafa 'anhu kaidahunn(a), innahu_ huwas sami'ul 'alim(u).
35.	Summa bada_ lahum mim ba'di ma_ ra'awul a_ya_ti  layasjununnahu_ hatta_ hin(in).
36.	Wa dakhala ma'ahus sijna fataya_n(i), qa_la ahaduhuma_ inni ara_ni a'siru khamra_(n), wa qa_lal a_kharu inni ara_ni ahmilu fauqa ra'si khubzan ta'kulut tairu minh(u), nabbi'na_ bita'wilih(i), inna_ nara_ka minal muhsinin(a).
37.	Qa_la la_ ya'tikuma_ ta'a_mun turzaqa_nihi illa_ nabba'tukuma_ bi ta'wilihi  qabla ay ya'tiyakuma_, za_likuma_ mimma_ 'allamani rabbi, inni taraktu millata qaumil la_ yu'minu_na billa_hi  wa hum bil a_khirati hum ka_firu_n(a)
38.	Wa-ttaba'tu millata a_ba_'i ibra_hima wa isha_qa wa ya'qu_b(a), ma_ ka_na lana_ an nusyrika billa_hi min syai'(in), za_lika min fadlilla_hi 'alaina_ wa 'alan na_si wa la_kinna aksaran na_si la_ yasykuru_n(a).
39.	Ya_ sa_hibayis sijni a'arba_bum mutafarriqu_na khairun amilla_hul wa_hidul qahha_r(u). 
40.	Ma_ ta'budu_na min du_nihi illa_ asma_'an sammaitumu_ha_ antum wa a_ba_'ukum ma_ anzalalla_hu biha_ min sulta_n(in), inil hukmu illa_ lilla_h(i), amara alla_ ta'budu_ illa_ iyya_h(u), za_likad dinul qayyimu wa la_kinna aksaran na_si la_ ya'lamu_n(a). 41.Ya_ sa_hibayis sijni amma_ ahadukuma_ fayasqi rabbahu_ khamra_(n), wa ammal a_kharu fa yuslabu fa ta'kulut tairu mir ra'sih(i), qudiyal amrul lazi fihi tastaftiya_n(i).
42.	Wa qa_la lillazi zanna annahu_ na_jim minhuma-zkurni 'inda rabbik(a), fa ansa_husy  syaita_nu zikra rabbihi fa labisa fis sijni bid'a  sinin(a).
43.	Wa qa_lal maliku inni ara_ sab'a baqara_tin sima_niy ya'kuluhunna sab'un 'ija_fuw wa sab'a sumbula_tin khudriw wa ukhara ya_bisa_t(in), ya_ ayyuhal mala'u aftu_ni fi ru'ya_ya in kuntum lir ru'ya_  ta'buru_n(a).
44.	Qa_lu_ adga_su ahla_m(in), wa ma_ nahnu bi ta'wilil ahla_mi bi  'a_limin(a).
45.	Wa qa_lal lazi naja_ minhuma_ waddakara ba'da ummatin ana  unabbi'ukum bita'wilihi fa arsilu_n(i).
46.	Yu_sufu ayyuhas siddiqu aftina_ fi sab'i baqara_tin sima_niy ya'kuluhunna sab'un'ija_fuw wa sab'i sumbula_tin khudriw wa ukhara ya_bisa_t(il), la'alli arji'u  ilan na_si la'allahum  ya'lamu_n(a).
47.	Qa_la tazra'u_na sab'a sinina  da'aba_(n), fama_ hasattum fazaru_hu fi sumbulihi illa_  qalilam mimma_ ta'kulu_n(a).
48.	Summa ya'ti mim ba'di za_lika sab'un syida_duy ya'kulna ma_ qaddamtum lahunna illa_ qalilam mimma_ tuhsinu_n(a).
49.	Summa ya'ti mim ba'di za_lika'a_mun fihi yuga_sun na_su wa fihi ya'siru_n(a).
50.	Wa qa_lal maliku'tu_ni bih(i), falamma_ ja_'ahur rasu_lu qa_la-rji' ila_ rabbika fas'alhu ma_ ba_lun niswatilla_ti qatta'na  aidiyahunn(a), inna rabbi bi  kaidihinna 'alim(un).
51.	Qa_la ma_ khatbukunna iz ra_wattunna yu_sufa 'an nafsih(i), qulna ha_sya lilla_hi ma_ 'alimna_ 'alaihi min su_'(in), qa_lat-imra'atul 'azizil a_na hashasal haqq(u), ana ra_wattuhu_ 'an nafsihi wa innahu_ laminassa_diqin(a).
52.	Za_lika liya'lama anni lam akhunhu bil gaibi wa  annalla_ha la_ yahdi kaidal kha_'inin(a).
53.	Wa ma_ ubarri'u nafsi, innan nafsa la'amma_ratum bis su_'iilla_ ma_ rahima rabbi, inna rabbi gafu_rur rahim(un).
54.	Wa qa_lal maliku'tu_ni bihi astakhlishu linafsi, falamma_kallamahu_ qa_la innakal yauma ladaina_ makinun amin(un).
55.	Qa_la-j'alni 'ala_ khaza_'inil ard(i), inni hafizun'alim(un).
56.	Wa kaza_lika makkanna_liyu_sufa fil ardi yatabawwa'u minha_ haisu yasya_'(u), nusibu bi  rahmatina_ man nasya_'u wa la_ nudi'u ajral muhsinin(a).
57.	Wa la'ajrul a_khirati khairul lillazina a_manu_ wa ka_nu_ yattaqu_n(a).
58.	Wa ja_'a ikhwatu yu_sufa fadakhalu_ 'alaihi fa'arafahum wa hum lahu_ munkiru_n(a).
59.	Wa lamma_ jahhazahum bi jaha_zihim qa_la'tu_ni bi akhil lakum min abikum, ala_ tarauna anni u_fil kaila wa ana khairul munzilin(a).
60.	Fa illam ta'tu_ni bihi fala_ kaila lakum 'indi wa la_ ,taqrabu_n(i).
61.	Qa_lu_ sanura_widu 'anhu aba_hu wa inna_ lafa_'ilu_n(a).
62.	Wa qa_la lifitya_nihi-j'alu_ bida_'atahum fi riha_lihim la'allahum ya'rifu_naha_ iza-nqalabu_ ila_ ahlihim   la'allahum yarji'u_n(a).
63.	Falamma_ raja'u_ ila_ abihim qa_lu_ ya_ aba_na_ muni'a minnal kailu fa arsil ma'ana_ akha_na_ naktal wa inna_ lahu_ laha_fizu_n(a).
64.	Qa_la hal a_manukum 'alaihi illa_ kama_ amintukum 'ala_ akhihi min qabl(u), falla_hu khairun ha_fizaw wa huwa arhamur ra_himin(a).
65.	Wa lamma_ fatahu_ mata_'ahum wajadu_ bida_'atahum ruddat ilaihim, qa_lu_ ya_ aba_na_ ma_ nabgi, ha_zihi bida_'atuna_ ruddat ilaina_ wa namiru ahlana_ wa nahfazu akha_na_ wa nazda_du kaila ba'ir(in), za_lika kailuy yasir(un).
66.	Qa_la lan ursilahu_ ma'akum hatta_ tu'ta_ni mausiqam minalla_hi lata'tunnani bihi  illa_ ay yuha_ta bikum, falamma_ a_tauhu mausiqahum qa_lalla_hu 'ala_ ma_ naqu_lu wakil(un).
67.	Wa qa_la ya_ baniyya la_ tadkhulu_ mim ba_biw wa_hidiw wa-dkhulu_ min abwa_bim  mutafarriqah(tin), wa ma_ ugni 'ankum minalla_hi min syai'(in), inil hukmu illa_ lilla_h(i), 'alaihi   tawakkaltu wa 'alaihi falyatawakkalil mutawakkilu_n(a).
68.	Wa lamma_ dakhalu_ min haisu amarahum abu_hum, ma_ ka_na yugni 'anhum minalla_hi min syai'in illa_ ha_jatan fi nafsi ya'qu_ba qada_ha_, wa innahu_ lazu_ nilmil lima_ 'allamna_hu wa la_kinna aksaran na_si la_ ya'lamu_n(a).
69.	Wa lamma_ dakhalu_ 'ala_ yu_sufa a_wa_ ilaihi akhu_hu qa_la inni ana akhu_ka fala_ tabta'is bima_ ka_nu_ ya'malu_n(a).
70.	Falamma_ jahhazahumm bi jaha_zihim ja'alas siqa_yata fi rahli akhihi summa azzana mu'azzinun ayyatuhal 'iru innakum lasa_riqu_n(a).
71.	Qa_lu_ wa aqbalu_ 'alaihim ma_za_ tafqidu_n(a).
72.	Qa_lu_ nafqidu suwa_'al maliki wa liman ja_'a bihi himlu ba'iriw wa ana bihi za'im(un).
73.	Qa_lu_ talla_hi laqad 'alimtum ma_ ji'na_ linufsida fil ardi wa ma_ kunna_ sa_riqin(a).
74.	Qa_lu_ fama_ jaza_'uhu_ in kuntum ka_zibin(a).
75.	Qa_lu_ jaza_'uhu_ maw wujida fi rahlihi fa huwa jaza_'uh(_), kaza_lika najziz za_limin(a).
76.	Fabada'a bi au'iyatihim qabla wi'a_'i akhihi summa-stakhrajaha_ miw wi'a_'i akhih(i), kaza_lika  kidna_ liyu_suf(a), ma_ ka_na liya'khuza akha_hu fi dinil maliki illa_ ay yasya_'alla_h(u), narfa'u daraja_tim man nasya_'(u), wa fauqa kulli zi 'ilmin 'alim(un).
77.	Qa_lu_ iy yasriq fa qad saraqa akhul lahu_ min qabl(u), fa asarraha_ yu_sufu fi nafsihi wa lam yubdiha_ lahum, qa_la antum syarrum maka_na_(n), walla_hu a'lamu bima_ tasifu_n(a).
78.	Qa_lu_ ya_ ayyuhal 'azizu inna lahu_ aban syaikhan kabiran fa khuz ahadana_ maka_nah(a_), inna_ nara_ka minal muhsinin(a).
79.	Qa_la ma'a_zalla_hi an na'khuza illa_ maw wajadna_ mata_'ana_ 'indah(u_), inna_ izal laza_limu_n(a).
80.	Falamma-stai'asu_ minhu khalasu_ najiyya_(n), qa_la kabiruhum alam ta'lamu_ anna aba_kum qad akhaza 'alaikum mausiqam minalla_hi wa min qablu ma_ farrattum fi yu_sufa falan abrahal arda hatta_ ya'zana li abi au  yahkumalla_hu li, wa huwa khairul ha_kimin(a).
81.	Irji'u_ ila_ abikum fa qu_lu_ ya_ aba_na_ inna-bnaka saraq(a), wa ma_ syahidna_ illa_ bima_ 'alimna_ wa ma_ kunna_ lil gaibi ha_fizin(a).
82.	Wa-s'alil qaryatal lati kunna_ fiha_ wal 'iral lati aqbalna_ fiha_, wa inna_ lasa_diqu_n(a).
83.	Qa_la bal sawwalat lakum anfusukum amra_(n), fa sabrun jamil(un), 'asallaa_hu ay ya'tiyani bihim jami'a_(n), innahu_ huwal 'alimul hakim(u). 
84.	Wa tawalla_ 'anhum wa qa_la ya_ asafa_ 'ala_ yu_sufa wa-byaddat aina_hu minal huzni fahuwa  kazim(un).
85.	Qa_la_ talla_hi tafta'u tazkuru yu_sufa hatta_ taku_na haradan au taku_na minal ha_likin(a).
86.	Qa_la innama_ asyku_ bassi wa huzni ilalla_hi wa a'lamu minalla_hi ma_ la_ ta'lamu_n(a).
87.	Ya_ baniyya-zhabu_ fatahassasu_  miy yu_sufa wa akhihi wa la_ tai'asu_ mir rauhilla_h(i), innahu_ la_ yai'asu mir rauhilla_hi illal qaumul ka_firu_n(a).
88.	Falamma_ dakhalu_ 'alaihi qa_lu_ ya_ ayyuhal 'azizu massana_ wa ahlanad durru wa ji'na_ bi bida_'atim muzja_tin fa aufi lanal kaila wa tasaddaq 'alaina_, innalla_ha yajzil mutasaddiqin(a).
89.	Qa_la hal 'alimtum ma_ fa'altum biya_sufa wa akhihi iz antum ja_hilu_n(a).
90.	Qa_lu_ a'innaka la'anta yu_suf(u), qa_la ana yu_sufu wa ha_za_ akhi qad mannalla_hu 'alaina_, innahu_ may yattaqi wa yasbir fa innalla_ha la_  yudi'u ajral muhsinin(a).
91.	Qa_lu_ talla_hi laqad a_sarakalla_hu 'alaina_ wa in kunna_ lakha_ti'in(a).
92.	Qa_la la_ tasriba 'alaikumul yaum(a), yagfirulla_hu lakum, wa huwa arhamur ra_himin(a).
93.	Izhabu_ bi qamisi ha_za_ fa alquhu 'alu_ wajhi abi ya'ti basira_(n), wa'tu_ni bi ahlikum ajma'in(a).
94.	Wa lamma_ fasalatil 'iru qa_la abu_hum inni la'ajidu riha yu_sufa lau la_ an tufannidu_n(i).
95.	Qa_lu_ tallu_hi innaka lafi dala_likal qadim(i).
96.	Falamma_ an ja_'al basyiru alqa_hu 'ala_ wajhihi fa-rtadda basira_(n), qa_la alam aqul lakum, inni a'lamu minalla_hi ma_ la_ ta'lamu_n(a).
97.	Qa_lu_ ya_ aba_na-stagfir lana_  zunu_bana_ inna_ kunna_ kha_ti'in(a).
98.	Qa_la saufa astagfiru lakum rabbi, innahu_ huwal gafu_rur rahim(u).
99.	Falamma_ dakhalu_ 'ala_ yu_sufa a_wa_ ilaihi abawaihi wa qa_la-dkhulu_ misra in sya_'alla_hua_minin(a).
100.	Wa rafa'a abawaihi 'alal 'arsyi wa kharru_ lahu_ sujjada_(n), wa qa_la ya_ abati ha_za_ ta'wilu ru'ya_yamin qabl(u), qad ja'alaha_  rabbi haqqa_(n), wa qad ahsana bi iz akhrajani minas sijni wa ja_'a bikum minal badwi mim ba'di an nazagasy syaita_nu baini wa baina ikhwati, inna rabbi latiful lima_ yasya_'(u), innahu_ huwal 'alimul hakim(u).
101.	Rabbi qad a_taitani minal  mulki wa 'allamtani min ta'wilil aha_dis(i), fa_tiras sama_wa_ti wal ard(i), anta waliyyi fid dunya_ wal a_khirah(ti), tawaffani muslimaw wa alhiqni bis sa_lihin(a).
102.	Za_lika min amba_'il gaibi nu_hihi ilaik(a), wa ma_ kunta ladaihim iz ajma'u_ amrahum wa hum yamkuru_n(a).
103.	Wa ma_ aksarun na_si wa lau harasta bi mu'minin(a).
104.	Wa ma_ tas'aluhum 'alaihi min ajr(in), in huwa illa_ zikrul lil 'a_lamin(a).
105.	Wa ka'ayyim min a_yatin fis sama_wa_ti wal ardi yamurru_na 'alaiha_ wa hum 'anha_ mu'ridu_n(a).
106.	Wa ma_ yu'minu aksaruhum  billa_hi illa_ wa hum musyriku_n(a).
107.	Afa'aminu_ an ta'tiyahum ga_syiyatum min 'aza_billa_hi au ta'tiyahumus sa_'atu bagtataw wa hum la_ yasy'uru_n(a).
108.	Qul ha_zihi sabili ad'u_ ilalla_h(i), 'ala_ basiratin ana wa man-ittaba'ani, wa subha_nalla_hi wa ma_ ana minal musyrikin(a).
109.	Wa ma_ arsalna_ min qablika illa_ rija_lan nu_hi ilaihim min ahlil qura_, afalam yasiru fil ardi fayanzuru_ kaifa ka_na 'a_qibatul lazina min qablihim, wa lada_rul a_khirati khairul lil lazina-ttaqau, afala_ ta'qilu_n(a).
110.	Hatta_ iza-stai'asar rusulu wa zannu_ annahum qad kuzibu_ ja_'ahum nasruna, fanujjiya man nasya_'(u), wa la_  yuraddu ba'suna_ 'anil qaumil mujrimin(a).
111.	Laqad ka_na fi qasasihim 'ibratul li'ulil alba_b(i), ma_ ka_na hadisay yuftara_ wa la_kin tasdiqal lazi baina yadaihi wa tafsila kulli syai'iw wa hudaw wa rahmatal liqaumiy yu'minu_n(a).
.EndTopic
;_________________________
.Topic qsAr-Ra'd " 13. Ar-Ra'd"
1.	Alif La_m Ra_, tilka a_ya_tul kita_b(i), wallazi unzila ilaika mir rabbikal haqqu wa la_kinna aksaran na_si la_ yu'minu_n(a).
2.	Alla_hul lazi rafa'as sama_wa_ti bi gairi 'amadin taraunaha_ summa-stawa_ 'alal 'arsyi wa sakhkharasy syamsa wal qamar(a), kulluy yajri li ajalim musamma_(n), yudabbirul amra yufassilul a_ya_ti la'allakum biliqa_'i rabbikum tu_qinu_n(a).
3.	Wa huwal lazi maddal arda wa ja'ala fiha_ rawa_siya wa anha_ra_(n), wa min kullis samara_ti ja'ala fiha_ zaujaini-snaini yugsyil lailan naha_r(a), inna fi za_lika la a_ya_til liqaumiy yatafakkaru_n(a).
4.	Wa fil ardi qita'um mutaja_wira_tuw wa janna_tum min a'na_biw wa zar'uw wa nakhilun sinwa_nuw wa gairu sinwa_niy yusqa_ bi ma_'iw wa_hid(in), wa nufaddilu ba'daha_ 'ala_ ba'din  fil ukul(i), inna fi za_likala a_ya_til liqaumiy ya'qilu_n(a).
5.	Wa in ta'jab fa 'ajabun qauluhum a'iza_ kunna_ tura_ban ainna_ lafi khalqin jadid(in), ula_'ikal lazina kafaru_ bi rabbihim, wa ula_'ikal agla_lu fi a'na_qihim, wa ula_'ika asha_bun na_r(i), hum fiha_ kha_lidu_n(a).
6.	Wa yasta'jilu_naka bis sayyi'ati qablal hasanati wa qad khalat min qablihimul masula_t(u), wa inna rabbaka lazu_ magfiratil lin na_si 'ala_  zulmihim, wa inna rabbaka lasyadidul 'iqa_b(i).
7.	Wa yaqu_lul lazina kafaru_ lau la_ unzila 'alaihi a_yatum mir rabbih(i), innama_ anta munziruw wa likulli qaumin ha_d(in).
8.	Alla_hu ya'lamu ma_ tahmilu kullu unsa_ wa ma_ tagidul arha_mu wa ma_ tazda_d(u), wa kullu syai'in bi miqda_r(in).
9.	'A_limul gaibi wasy syaha_datil kabirul muta'a_l(i).
10.	Sawa_'um minkum man asarral qaula wa man jahara bihi wa man huwa mustakhfim bil laili wa sa_ribum bin  naha_r(i).
11.	Lahu_ mu'aqqiba_tum mim baini yadaihi wa min khalfihi yahfazu_nahu_ min amrilla_h(i), innalla_ha la_ yugayyiru ma_ bi qaumin hatta_ yugayyiru_ ma_ bi anfusihim, wa iza_ ara_dalla_hu bi qaumin sa_'an fala_ maradda lah(u_), wa ma_ lahum min du_nihi miw wa_l(in).
12.	Huwal lazi yurikumul barqa khaufaw wa tama'aw wa yunsyi'us saha_bas siqa_l(a).
13.	Wa yusabbihur ra'du bi hamdihi wal mala_'ikatu min khifatih(i), wa yursilus sawa_'iqa fa yusibu biha_ may yasya_'u wa hum yuja_dilu_na filla_h(i), wa huwa syadidul miha_l(i).
14.	Lahu_ da'watul haqq(i), wallazina yad'u_na min du_nihi la_ yastajibu_na lahum bi syai'in illa_ ka ba_siti kaffaihi ilal ma_'i liyabluga fa_hu wa ma_ huwa bi ba_ligih(i), wa ma_ du'a_'ul ka_firina illa_ fi dala_l(in).
15.	Wa lilla_hi yasjudu man fis sama_wa_ti wal ardi tau'aw wa karhaw wa zila_luhum bil guduwwi wala a_sa_l(i).
16.	Qul mar rabbus sama_wa_ti wal ard(i), qulilla_h(u), qul afa-ttakhaztum min du_nihi auliya_'a la_ yamliku_na li anfusihim naf'aw wa la_ darra_(n), qul hal yastawil a'ma_ wal basir(u), am hal tastawiz zuluma_tu wan nu_r(u), am ja'ala_ lilla_hi syuraka_'a khalaqa_ ka khalqihi fa tasya_bahal khalqu 'alaihim, qulilla_hu kha_liqu kulli syai'iw wa huwal wa_hidul qahha_r(u).
17.	Anzala minas sama_'i ma_'an fa sa_lat audiyatum bi qadariha_ fa-htamalas sailu zabadar ra_biya_(n), wa mimma_ yu_qidu_na 'alaihi fin na_ri-btiga_'a hilyatin au mata_'in zabadum misluh(u_), kaza_lika yadribull_hul haqqa wal ba_til(a), fa ammaz zabadu fa yazhabu jufa_'a(n), wa amma_ ma_ yanfa'un na_sa fa yamkusu fil ard(i), kaza_lika yadribulla_hul amsa_l(a).
18.	Lillazina-staja_bu_  lirabbihimul husna_, wallazina lam yastajibu_ lahu_ lau anna lahum ma_ fil ardi jami'aw wa mislahu_ ma'ahu_ la-ftadau bih(i), ula_'ika lahum su_'ul hisa_b(i), wa ma'wa_hum jahannam(u), wa bi'sal miha_d(u).
19.	Afamay ya'lamu annama_ unzila ilaika mir rabbikal haqqu ka man huwa a'ma_, innama_ yatazakkaru ulul alba_b(i),
20.	Allazina yu_fu_na bi 'ahdilla_hi wa la_ yanqudu_nal misa_q(a),
21.	Wallazina yasilu_na ma_ amaralla_hu bihi ay yu_sala wa yakhsyauna rabbahum wa yakha_fu_na su_'al hisa_b(i).
22.	Wallazina sabaru-btiga_'a wajhi rabbihim wa aqa_mus sala_ta wa anfaqu_ mimma_ razaqna_hum sirraw wa  'ala_niyataw wa yadra'u_na bil hasana_tis sayyi'ata ula_'ika lahum 'uqbad da_r(i), 
23.	Janna_tu 'adniy yadkhulu_naha_ wa man salaha mina a_ba_'ihim wa azwa_jihim wa zurriyya_tihim wal mala_'ikatu yadkhulu_na 'alaihim min kulli ba_b(in).
24.	Sala_mun 'alaikum bima_  sabartum fa ni'ma 'uqbad da_r(i).
25.	Wallazina yanquduu_na 'ahdalla_hi mim ba'di  misa_qihi wa yaqta'u_na ma_ amaralla_hu bihi ay yu_sala wa yufsidu_na fil ard(i), ula_'ika lahumul la'natu wa lahum su_'ud da_r(i).
26.	Alla_hu yabsutur rizqa limay yasya_'u wa yaqdir(u), wa farihu_ bil haya_tid dunyu_, wa mal haya_tud dunya_ fil a_khirati illa_ mata_'(un).
27.	Wa yaqu_lul lazina kafaru_ lau la_ unzila 'alaihi a_yatum mir rabbih(i), qul innallu_ha yudillu may yasya_'u wa yahdi ilaihi man ana_b(a).
28.	Allazina a_manu_ wa tatma'innu qulu_buhum bi zikrilla_h(i), ala_ bi zikrilla_hi tatma'innul qulu_b(u).
29.	Allazina a_manu_ wa 'amilus sa_liha_ti tu_ba_ lahum wa husnu ma'a_b(in).
30.	Kaza_lika arsalna_ka fi ummatin qad khalat min qabliha_ umamul litatluwa  'alaihimul lazi auhaina_ ilaika wa hum yakfuru_na bir rahma_n(i), qul huwa rabbi la_ ila_ha illa_ huw(a), 'alaihi tawakkaltu wa ilaihi mata_b(i).
31.	Wa lau anna qur'a_nan suyyirat bihil jiba_lu au qutti'at bihil ardu au kullima bihil mauta_, bal lilla_hil amru jami'a_(n), afalam yay'asil lazina a_manu_ allau yasya_'ulla_hu lahadan na_sa jami'a_(n), wa la_ yaza_lul lazina kafaru_ tusibuhum bima_ sana'u_ qa_ri'atun au tahullu qaribam min da_rihim hatta_ ya'tiya wa'dulla_h(i), innalla_ha la_ yukhliful mi'a_d(a).
32.	Wa laqad-istuhzi'a bi rusulim min qablika fa amlaitu lillazina kafaru_ summa akhaztuhum fa kaifa ka_na 'iqa_b(i).
33.	Afaman huwa qa_'imun 'ala_ kulli nafsim bima_ kasabat, wa ja'ala_ lilla_hi syuraka_'(a), qul sammu_hum, am tunabbi'u_nahu_ bima_ la_ ya'lamu fil ardi am bi za_hirim minal qaul(i), bal zuyyina lillazina kafaru_ makruhum wa suddu_ 'anis sabil(i), wa may  yudlilillu_hu famu_ laha_ min ha_d(in).
34.	Lahum 'aza_bun fil haya_tid dunya_ wa la'aza_bul a_khirati asyaqq(u), wa ma_ lahum minall_hi miw wa_q(in).
35.	Masalul jannatil lati wu'idal muttaqu_n(a), tajri min tahtihal anha_r(u), ukuluha_ da_'imuw wa zilluha_, tilka 'uqbal lazina-ttaqaw, wa 'uqbal ka_firinan na_r(u).
36.	Wallazina a_taina_humul kita_ba yafrahu_na bima_ unzila ilaika wa minal ahza_bi may yunkiru ba'dah(u_), qul innama_ umirtu an a'budalla_ha wa la_ usyrika bih(i), ilaihi ad'u_ wa ilaihi ma'a_b(i).
37.	Wa kaza_lika anzalna_hu hukman 'arabiyya_(n), wa la'in-ittaba'ta ahwa_'ahum ba'da ma_ ja_'aka minal 'ilm(i), ma_ laka minalla_hi miw waliyyiw wa la_ wa_q(in).
38.	Wa laqad arsalna_ rusulam min qablika wa ja'alna_ lahum azwa_jaw wa zurriyyah(tan), wa ma_ ka_na li rasu_lin ay ya'tiya bi a_yatin illa_ bi iznilla_h(i), likulli ajalin kita_b(un).
39.	Yamhulla_hu ma_ yasya_'u wa yusbit(u), wa 'indahu_ ummul kita_b(i).
40.	Wa imma_ nuriyannaka ba'dal lazi na'iduhum au natawaffayannaka fa innama_ 'alaikal bala_gu wa 'alainal hisa_b(u).
41.	Awalam yarau anna_ na'til arda nanqusuha_ min atra_fiha_, walla_hu yahkumu la_ mu'aqqiba li hukmih(i), wa huwa sari'ul hisa_b(i).
42.	Wa qad makaral lazina min qablihim fa lilla_hil makru jami'a_(n), ya'lamu ma_ taksibu kullu nafs(in), wa saya'lamul kuffa_ru liman 'uqbad da_r(i).
44.	Wa yaqu_lul lazina kafaru_ lasta mursala_(n), qul kafu_  billa_hi syahidam baini wa  bainakum, wa man 'indahu_ 'ilmul kita_b(i).
.EndTopic
;________________________
.Topic qsIbrahim " 14. Ibrahim"
1.	Alif La_m Ra_, kitabun anzalna_hu ilaika litukhrijan na_sa minaz zuluma_ti ilan nu_r(i), bi izni rabbihim ila_ sira_til 'azizil hamid(i),
2.	Alla_hil lazi lahu_ ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ard(i), wa wailul lil ka_firina min 'aza_bin syadid(in),
3.	Allazina yastajibu_nal haya_tad dunya_ 'alala a_khirati wa yasuddu_na 'an sabililla_hi wa yabgu_naha_ 'iwaja_(n), ula_'ika  fi dala_lim ba'id(in).
4.	Wa ma_ arsalna_ mir rasu_lin illa_ bi lisa_ni qaumihi liyubayyina lahum, fa yudillulla_hu may yasya_'u wa yahdi may yasya_'(u), wa huwal 'azizul hakim(u).
5.	Wa laqad arsalna_ mu_sa_ bi a_ya_tina_ an akhrij qaumaka minaz zuluma_ti ilan nu_r(i), wa zakkirhum bi ayya_milla_h(i), inna fi za_lika la a_ya_til likulli sabba_rin syaku_r(in).
6.	Wa iza qa_la mu_sa_ li qaumihi-zkuru_ ni'matalla_hi 'alaikm iz anja_kum min a_li fir'auna yasu_mu_nakum su_'al 'aza_bi wa yuzabbihu_na abna_'akum wa yastahyu_na nisa_'akum, wa fi za_likum bala_'um mir rabbikum 'azim(un).
7.	Wa iz ta'azzana rabbukum la'in syakartum  la'azidannakum wa la'in kafartum inna 'azaa_bi lasyadid(un).
8.	Wa qa_la mu_sa_ in takfuru_ antum wa man fil ardi jami'a_(n), fa innalla_ha laganiyyun hamid(un).
9.	Alam ya'tikum naba'ul lazina min qablikum qaumi nu_hiw wa 'a_diw wa samu_d(a), wallazina mim ba'dihim, la_ ya'lamuhum illalla_h(u), ja_'athum rusuluhum bil bayyina_ti fa raddu_ aidiyahum fi afwa_hihim wa qa_lu_ inna_ kafarna_ bima_ ursiltum bihi wa inna_ lafi syakkim mimma_ tad'u_nana_  ilaihi murib(in).
10.	Qa_lat rusuluhum afailla_hi syakkun fa_tiris sama_wa_ti wal ard(i), yad'u_kum liyagfira lakum min zunu_bikum wa yu'akhkhirakum ila_ ajalim musamma_(n), qa_lu_ in antum illa_ basyarum misluna_, turidu_na an tasuddu_na_ 'amma_ ka_na yanbudu a_ba_'una_ fa'tu_na_ bi sulta_nim mubin(in).
11.	Qa_lat lahum rusuluhum in nahnu illa_ basyarum mislukum wa la_kinnalla_ha yamunnu 'ala_ may yasya_'u min 'iba_dih(i), wa ma_ ka_na lana_ an na'tiyakum bi sulta_nin illa_ bi iznilla_h(i), wa 'alalla_hi falyatawakkalil mu'minu_n(a).
12.	Wa ma_ lana_ alla_ natawakkala 'alalla_hi wa qad hada_na_  subulana_, wa lanasbiranna 'ala_ ma_ a_zaitumu_na_, wa 'alalla_hi fal yatawakkalil mutawakkilu_n(a).
13.	Wa qa_lal lazina kafaru_ li rusulihim lanukhrijannakum min ardina_ au lata'u_dunna fi millatina_, fa auha_ ilaihim rabbuhum lanuhlikannaz za_limin(a).
14.	Wa lanuskinannakumul arda mim ba'dihim, za_lika liman kha_fa maqa_mi wa kha_fa wa'id(i). 
15.	Wa-staftahu_ wa kha_ba kullu jabba_rin 'anid(im),
16.	Miw wara_'ihi jahannamu wa yusqa_ mim ma_'in sadid(iy),
17.	Yatajarra'uhu_ wa la_ yaka_du yusiguhu_ wa ya'tihil mautu min kulli maka_niw wa ma_ huwa bi mayyit(in), wa miw wara_'ihi 'aza_bun galiz(un).
18.	Masalul lazina kafaru_ bi rabbihim a'ma_luhum ka rama_din-isytaddat bihir rihu fi yaumin 'a_sif(in), la_ yaqdiru_na mimma_ kasabu_ 'ala_ syai'(in), za_lika huwad dala_lul ba'id(u).
19.	Alam tara annalla_ha khalaqas sama_wa_ti wal arda bil haqq(i), iy yasya' yuzhibkum wa ya'ti bi khalqin jadid(iw),
20.	Wa ma_ za_lika 'alalla_hi bi  'aziz(in).
21.	Wa barazu_ lilla_hi jami'an faqa_lad du'afa_'u lil lazina-stakbaru_ inna_ kunna_ lakum taba'an fahal antum mugna_na 'anna_ min 'aza_billa_hi min syai'(in), qa_lu_ lau had_nalla_hu lahadaina_kum, sawa_'un 'alaina_ ajazi'na_ am sabarna_ ma_ lana_ mim mahis(in).
22.	Wa qa_lasy syaita_nu lamma qudiyal amru innalla_ha wa'adakum wa'dal haqqi wa wa'attukum fa akhlaftukum, wa ma_ ka_na liya 'alaikum min sulta_nin illa_ an da'autukum fa-stajabtum li, fala_ talu_mu_ni wa lu_mu_ anfusakum, ma_ ana bi musrikhikum wa ma_ antum bi musrikhiyy(a), inni kafartu bima_ asyraktumu_ni min qabl(u), innaz za_limina lahum 'aza_bun alim(un).
23.	Wa udkhilal lazina a_manu_ wa 'amilus sa_liha_ti janna_tin tajri min tahtihal anha_ru kha_lidina fiha_ bi izni rabbihim, tahiyyatuhum fiha_ sala_m(un).
24.	Alam tara kaifa daraballa_hu masalan kalimatan tayyibatan ka syajaratin tayyibatin asluha_ sa_bituw wa far'uha_ fis sama_'(i),
25.	Tu'ti ukulaha_ kulla hinim bi izni rabbiha_, wa yadribulla_hul amsa_la lin na_si la'allahum yatazakkaru_n(a).
26.	Wa masalu kalimatin khabisatin ka syajaratin khabisatin-ijtussat min fauqil ardi ma_ laha_ minqara_r(in).
27.	Yusabbitulla_hul lazina a_manu_  bil qaulis sa_biti fil haya_tid dunya_ wa fil a_khirah(ti), wa yudillulla_huz za_limin(a), wa yaf'alulla_hu ma_ yasya_'(u).
28.	Alam tara ilal lazina baddalu_ ni'matalla_hi kufraw wa ahallu_ qaumahum da_ral bawa_r(i),
29.	Jahannam(a), yaslaunaha_, wa bi'sal qara_r(u).
30.	Wa ja'alu_ lilla_hi anda_dal liyudillu_ 'an sabilih(i), qul tamatta'u_ fa inna masirakum ilan na_r(i).
31.	Qul li'iba_diyal lazina a_manu_ yuqimus sala_ta wa yunfiqu_ mimma_ razaqna_hum sirraw wa'ala_niyatam min qabli ay ya'tiya yaumul la_ bai'un fihi wa la_ khila_l(un).
32.	Alla_hul lazi khalaqas sama_wa_ti wal arda wa anzala minas sama_'i ma_'an fa akhraja bihi minas samara_ti rizqal lakum, wa sakhkhara lakumul fulka litajriya fil bahri bi amrih(i), wa sakhkhara lakumul anha_r(a).
33.	Wa sakhkhara lakumusy syamsa wal qamara da_'ibain(i), wa sakhkhara lakumul laila wan naha_r(a).
34.	Wa a_ta_kum min kulli ma_ sa'altumu_h(u), wa in ta'uddu_ ni'matalla_hi la_ tuhsa_ha_, innal insa_na lazalu_mun kaffa_r(un).
35.	Wa iz qa_la ibra_himu rabbi-j'al ha_zal balada a_minaw wa-jnubni wa baniyya an na'budal asna_m(a).
36.	Rabbi innahunna adlalna kasiram minan na_s(i), faman tabi'ani fa innahu_ minni, wa man 'asa_ni fa innaka gafu_rur rahim(un).
37.	Rabbana_ inni askantu min zurriyyati bi wa_din gairi zi zar'in 'inda baitikal muharram(i), rabbana_ liyuqimus sala_ta fa-j'al af'idatam minan na_si tahwi ilaihim wa-rzuqhum minas samara_ti la'allahum yasykuru_n(a).
38.	Rabbana_ innaka ta'lamu ma_ nukhfi wa ma_ nu'lin(u), wa ma_ yakhfa_ 'alalla_hi min syai'in fil ardi wa la_ fis sama_'(i).
39.	Al hamdu lilla_hil lazi wahaba li 'alal kibari isma_'ila wa isha_q(a), inna rabbi lasami'ud du'a_'(i).
40.	Rabbi-j'alni muqimas sala_ti wa min zurriyyati, rabbana_ wa taqabbal du'a_'(i).
41.	Rabbana-gfir li wa liwa_lidayya wa lil mu'minina yauma yaqu_mul hisa_b(u).
42.	Wa la_ tahsabannalla_ha ga_filan 'amma_ ya'maluz za_limu_n(a), innama_ yu'akhkhiruhum liyaumin tasykhasu fihil absa_r(u),
43.	Muhti'ina muqni'i ru'u_sihim la_ yartaddu ilaihim tarfuhum, wa af'idatuhum hawa_'(un).
44.	Wa anzirin na_sa yauma ya'tihimul 'aza_b(u), fa yaqu_lul lazina zalamu_ rabbana_ akhkhirna_ ila_ ajalin qarib(in), nujib da'wataka wa nattabi'ir rusul(a), awalam taku_nu_ aqsamtum min qablu ma_ lakum min zawa_l(iw),
45.	Wa sakantum fi masa_kinil lazina zalamu_ anfusahum wa tabayyana lakum kaifa fa'alna_ bihim wa darabna_ lakumul amsa_l(a).
46.	Wa qad makaru_ makrahum wa 'indalla_hi makruhum, wa in ka_na makruhum litazu_la minhul jiba_l(u).
47.	Fala_ tahsabannalla_ha mukhlifa wa'dihi rusulah(a_), innalla_ha 'azizun zu-ntiqa_m(in).
48.	Yauma tubaddalul ardu gairal ardi was sama_wa_tu wa barazu_ lilla_hil wa_hidil qahha_r(i).
49.	Wa taral mujrimina yauma'izim muqarranina fil asfa_d(i).
50.	Sara_biluhum min qatira_niw wa tagsya_ wuju_hahumun na_r(u),
51.	Liyajziyalla_hu kulla nafsim ma_ kasabat, innalla_ha sari'ul hisa_b(i).
52.	Ha_za_ bala_gul lin na_si wa liyunzaru_ bihi wa liya'lamu_ annama_ huwa ila_huw wa_hiduw wa liyazzakkara ulul alba_b(i).
.EndTopic
;______________________
.Topic qsAl-Hijr " 15. Al-Hijr"
1.	Alif La_m Ra_, tilka a_ya_tul kita_bi wa qur'a_nim mubin(in).
2.	Rubama_ yawaddul lazina kafaru_ lau ka_nu_ muslimin(a).
3.	Zarhum ya'kulu_ wa yatamatta'u_ wa yulhihimul amalu fa saufa  ya'lamu_n(a).
4.	Wa ma_ ahlakna_ min qaryatin illa_ wa laha_ kita_bum ma'lu_m(un).
5.	Ma_ tasbiqu min ummatin ajalaha_ wa ma_ yasta'khiru_n(a).
6.	Wa qa_lu_ ya_ ayyuhal lazi nuzzila 'alaihiz zikru innaka  lamajnu_n(un).
7.	Lau ma_ ta'tina_ bil mala_'ikati in kunta minas sa_diqin(a).
8.	Ma_ nunazzilul mala_'ikata illa_ bil haqqi wa ma_ ka_nu_ izam munzarin(a).
9.	Inna_ nahnu nazzalnaz zikra wa inna_ lahu_ laha_fizu_n(a).
10.	Wa laqad arsalna_ min qablika fi syiya'il awwalin(a).
11.	Wa ma_ ya'tihim mir rasu_lin illa_ ka_nu_ bihi  yastahzi'u_n(a).
12.	Kaza_lika naslukuhu_ fi qulu_bil mujrimin(a),
13.	La_ yu'minu_na bihi wa qad khalat sunnatul awwalin(a).
14.	Wa lau fatahna_ 'alaihim ba_bam minas sama_'i fazallu_ fihi ya'ruju_n(a),
15.	Laqa_lu_ innama_ sukkirat absa_runa_ bal nahnu qaumum mashu_ru_n(a).
16.	Wa laqad ja'alna_ fis sama_'i buru_jaw wa zayyanna_ha_ lin  na_zirin(a),
17.	Wa hafizna_ha_ min kulli  syaita_nir rajim(in),
18.	Illa_ man-istaraqas sam'a fa atba'ahu_ syiha_bum mubin(un).
19.	Wal arda madadna_ha_ wa alqaina_ fiha_ rawa_siya wa ambatna_ fiha_ min kulli syai'im mauzu_n(in).
20.	Wa ja'alna_ lakum fiha_  ma'a_yisya wa mal lastum lahu_ bi ra_ziqin(a).
21.	Wa im min syai'in illa_ 'indana_ khaza_'inuhu_ wa ma_ nunazziluhu_ illa_ bi qadarim ma'lu_m(in).
22.	Wa arsalnar riya_ha lawa_qiha fa anzalna_ minas sama_'i ma_'an fa asqaina_kuma_h(u), wa ma_ antum lahu_ bi kha_zinin(a).
23.	Wa inna_ lanahnu nuhyi wa numitu wa nahnul wa_risin(a).
24.	Wa laqad 'alimnal mustaqdimina minkum wa laqad 'alimnal musta'khirin(a).
25.	Wa inna rabbaka huwa yahsyuruhum, innahu_ hakimun 'alim(un).
26.	Wa laqad khalaqnal insa_na min salsa_lim min hama'im  masnu_n(in).
27.	Wal ja_nna khalaqna_hu min qablu min na_ris samu_m(i).
28.	Wa iz qa_la rabbuka lil mala_'ikati inni kha_liqum basyaram min salsa_lim min hama'im masnu_n(in).
29.	Fa iza-stawaituhu_ wa nafakhtu fihi mir ru_hi fa  qa'u_ lahu_ sa_jidin(a).
30.	Fasajadal mala_'ikatu  kulluhum ajma'u_n(a),
31.	Illa_ iblis(a), aba_ ay yaku_na ma'as sa_jidin(a).
32.	Qa_la ya_ iblisu ma_ laka alla_ taku_na ma'as sa_jidin(a).
33.	Qa_la lam akul li'asjuda li basyarin khalaqtahu_ min salsa_lim min hama'im masnu_n(in).
34.	Qa_la fa-khruj minha_ fa innaka rajim(uw),
35.	Wa inna 'alaikal la'nata ila_ yaumid din(i).
36.	Qa_la rabbi fa anzirni ila_ yaumi yub'asu_n(a).
37.	Qa_la fa innaka minal  munzarin(a),
38.	Ila_ yaumil waqtil ma'lu_m(i).
39.	Qa_la rabbi bima_ agwaitani la uzayyinanna lahum fil ardi wa la'ugwiyannahum  ajma'in(a),
40.	Illa_ 'iba_daka minhumul mukhlasin(a).
41.	Qa_la ha_za_ sira_tun 'alayya mustaqim(un).
42.	Inna 'iba_di laisa laka 'alaihim sulta_nun illa_  man-ittaba'aka minal ga_win(a).
43.	Wa inna jahannama  lamau'iduhum ajma'in(a),
44.	Laha_ sab'atu abwa_b(in), likulli ba_bim minhum juz'um maqsu_m(un).
45.	Innal muttaqina fi  janna_tiw wa 'uyu_n(in).
46.	Udkhulu_ha_ bi sala_min a_minin(a).
47.	Wa naza'na_ ma_ fi sudu_rihim min gillin ikhwa_nan 'ala_ sururim mutaqa_bilin(a).
48.	La_ yamassuhum fiha_ nasabuw  wa ma_ hum minha_ bi mu'jizin(a).
49.	Nabbi' 'iba_di anni anal gafu_rur rahim(u).
50.	Wa anna 'aza_bi huwal 'aza_bul alim(u).
51.	Wa nabbi'hum 'an daifi ibra_him(a).
52.	Iz dakhalu_ 'alaihi faqa_la_ sala_ma_(n), qa_la inna minkum wajilu_n(a).
53.	Qa_lu_ la_ taujal inna_  nubasysyiruka bi gula_min 'alim(in).
54.	Qa_la abasysyartumu_ni 'ala_ am massaniyal kibaru fa bima_ tubasysyiru_n(a).
55.	Qa_lu_ basysyarna_ka bil haqqi fala_ takum minal qa_nitin(a).
56.	Qa_la wa may yaqnatu mir rahmati rabbihi illad da_llu_n(a).
57.	Qa_la fama_ khatbukum ayyuhal mursalu_n(a).
58.	Qa_lu_ inna_ ursilna_ ila_ qaaumim mujrimin(a),
59.	Illa_ a_la lu_t(in), inna_ lamunajju_hum ajma'in(a),
60.	Illa-mra'atahu_ qaddarna_ innaha_ laminal ga_birin(a).
61.	Falamma_ ja_'a a_la lu_tinil mursalin(a),
62.	Qa_la innakum qaumum  munkaru_n(a).
63.	Qa_la_ bal ji'na_ka bima_ ka_nu_ fihi yamtaru_n(a).
64.	Wa a_taina_ka bil haqqi wa inna_ lasa_diqu_n(a).
65.	Fa asri bi ahlika bi qit'im minal laili wa-ttabi' adba_rahum wa la_ yaltafit minkum ahaduw wa-mdu_ haisu tu'maru_n(a).
66.	Wa qadaina_ ilaihi za_likal amra anna da_bira ha_'ula_'i maqtu_'um musbihin(a).
67.	Wa ja_'a ahlul madinati yastabsyiru_n(a).
68.	Qa_la inna ha_'ula_'i daifi fala_ tafdahu_n(i),
69.	Wa-ttaqulla_ha wa la_  tukhzu_n(i).
70.	Qa_lu_ awalam nanhaka 'anil 'a_lamin(a).
71.	Qa_la ha_'ula_'i bana_ti in kuntum fa_'ilin(a).
72.	La'amruka innahum lafi sakratihim ya'mahu_n(a).
73.	Fa akhazathumus saihatu  musyriqin(a),
74.	Fa ja'alna_ 'a_liyaha_ sa_filaha_ wa amtarna_ 'alaihim hija_ratam min sijjil(in).
75.	Inna fi za_lika la a_ya_til lil mutawassimin(a),
76.	Wa innaha_ labisabilim muqim(in).
77.	Inna fi za_lika la a_yatal lil mu'minin(a).
78.	Wa in ka_na asha_bul aikati laza_limin(a),
79.	Fa-ntaqamna_ minhum, wa innahuma_ labi ima_mim mubin(in).
80.	Wa laqad kazzaba asha_bul hijril mursalin(a),
81.	Wa a_taina_hum a_ya_tina_ faka_nu_ 'anha_ mu'ridin(a),
82.	Wa ka_nu_ yanhitu_na minal  jiba_li buyu_tan a_minin(a).
83.	Fa akhazathumus saihatu musbihin(a),
84.	Fama_ agna_ 'anhum ma_ ka_nu_ yaksibu_n(a).
85.	Wa ma_ khalaqnas sama_wati wal  arda wa ma_ bainahuma_ illa_ bil haqq(i), wa innas sa_'ata  la a_tiyatun fa-sfahis safhal  jamil(a).
86.	Inna rabbaka huwal khalla_qul 'alim(u).
87.	Wa laqad a_taina_ka sab'am minal masa_ni wal qur'a_nal 'azim(a).
88.	La_ tamuddanna 'ainaika ila_  ma_ matta'na_ bihi azwa_jam minhum wa la_ tahzan 'alaihim wa-khfid jana_haka lil mu'minin(a).
89.	Wa qul inni anan nazirul  mubin(u).
90.	Kama_ anzalna_ 'alal muqtasimin(a),
91.	Allazina ja'alul qur'a_na 'idin(a).
92.	Fa warabbika lanas'alannahum ajma'in(a),
93.	'Amma_ ka_nu_ ya'malu_n(a).
94.	Fa-sda' bima_ tu'maru wa  a'rid nanil musyrikin(a).
95.	Inna_ kafaina_kal  mustahzi'in(a),
96.	Allazina yaj'alu_na ma'alla_hi  ila_han a_khar(a), fa saufa ya'lamu_n(a).
97.	Wa laqad na'lamu annaka yadiqu sadruka bima_  yaqu_lu_n(a),
98.	Fa sabbih bi hamdi rabbika wa kum minas sa_jidin(a),
99.	Wa-'bud rabbaka hatta_ ya'tiyakal yaqin(u).
.EndTopic
;_________________________
.Topic qsAn-Nahl " 16. An-Nahl"
1.	Ata_ amrulla_hi fala_  tasta'jilu_h(u), subha_nahu_ wa  ta'a_la_ 'amma_ yusyriku_n(a).
2.	Yunazzilul mala_'ikata bir ru_hi min amrihi 'ala_ may yasya_'u min 'iba_dihi an anziru_ annahu_ la_ ila_ha illa_ ana fa-ttaqu_n(i).
3.	Khalaqas sama_wa_ti wal arda bil haqq(i), ta'a_la_ 'amma_ yusyriku_n(a).
4.	Khalaqal insa_na min nutfatin  fa iza_ahuwa khasimum mubin(un).
5.	Wal an'a_ma khalaqaha_ lakum  fiha_ dif'uw wa mana_fi'u wa minha_ ta'kulu_n(a).
6.	Wa lakum fiha_ jama_lun hina turihu_na wa hina tasrahu_n(a),
7.	Wa tahmilu asqa_lakum ila_ baladil lam taku_nu_ ba_ligihi illaa_ bi syiqqil anfus(i), inna rabbakum la ra'u_fur rahim(uw),
8.	Wal khaila wal biga_la wal hamira litarkabu_ha_ wa zinah(tan), wa yakhluqu ma_ la_  ta'lamu_n(a).
9.	Wa 'alalla_hi qasdus sabili wa  minha_ ja_'ir(un), wa lau sya_'a  lahada_kum ajma'in(a).
10.	Huwal lazi anzala minas sama_'i ma_'al lakum minhu syara_buw wa minhu syajarun fihi tusimu_n(a).
11.	Yumbitu lakum bihiz zar'a waz zaitu_na wan nakhila wal a'na_ba wa min kullis samara_t(i), inna fi za_lika la a_yatal liqaumiy yatafakkaru_n(a).
12.	Wa sakhkhara lakummul laila wan naha_r(a), wasy syamsa wal qamar(a), wan nuju_mu musakhkhara_tum bi amrih(i), inna fi za_lika la a_ya_til liqaumiy ya'qilu_n(a),
13.	Wa ma_ zara'a lakum fil ardi mukhtalifan alwa_nuh(a_), inna fi za_lika la a_yatal liqaumiy yazzakkaru_n(a).
14.	Wa huwal lazi sakhkharal  bahra lita'kulu_ minhu lahman tariyyaw wa tastakhriju_ minhu hilyatan talbasu_naha_, wa taral fulka mawa_khira fihi wa litabtagu_ min fadlihi wa la'allakum tasykuru_n(a).
15.	Wa alqa_ fil ardi rawa_siya an tamida bikum wa anha_raw wa subulal la'allakum tahtadu_n(a),
16.	Wa 'ala_ma_t(in), wa bin najmi hum yahtadu_n(a).
17.	Afamay yakhluqu kamal la_ yakhluq(u), afala_  tazakkaru_n(a).
18.	Wa in ta'uddu_ ni'matalla_hi la_ tuhsu_ha_, innalla_ha lagafu_rur rahim(un).
19.	Walla_hu ya'lamu ma_ tusirru_na wa ma_ tu'linu_n(a).
20.	Wallazina yad'u_na min du_nilla_hi la_ yakhluqu_na  syai'aw wa hum yukhlaqu_n(a).
21.	Amwa_tun gairu ahya_'(in), wa ma_ yasy'uru_na ayya_na yub'asu_n(a).
22.	Ila_hukum ila_huw wa_hid(un), fallazina la_ yu'minu_na bil a_khirati qulu_buhum munkiratuw wa hum mustakbiru_n(a).
23.	La_ jarama annalla_ha ya'lamu ma_ yusirru_na wa ma_ yu'linu_n(a), innahu_ la_ yuhibbul mustakbirin(a).
24.	Wa iza_ qila lahum ma_ anzala rabbukum, qa_lu_ asa_tirul awwalin(a),
25.	Liyahmilu_ auza_rahum ka_milatay yaumal qiya_mah(ti), wa min auza_ril lazina yudillu_nahum bi gairi  'ilm(in), ala_ sa_'a ma_ yaziru_n(a).
26.	Qad makaral lazina min qablihim fa atalla_hu bunya_nahum minal qawa_'idi fa kharra 'alaihimus saqfu min fauqihim wa ata_humul 'aza_bu min haisu la_ yasy'uru_n(a).
27.	Summa yaumal qiya_mati yukhzihim wa yaqu_lu aina syuraka_'iyal lazina kuntum tusya_qqu_na fihim, qa_lal lazina u_tul 'ilma innal khizyal yauma was su_'a 'alal  ka_firin(a),
28.	Allazina tatawaffa_humul mala_'ikatu za_limi anfusihim, fa alqawus salama ma_ kunna_ na'malu min su_'(in), bala_ innalla_ha 'alimum bima_ kuntum ta'malu_n(a).
29.	Fa-dkhulu_ abwa_ba jahannama kha_lidina fiha_, fa labi'sa  maswal mutakabbirin(a).
30.	Wa qila lillazina-ttaqau ma_za_ anzala rabbukum, qa_lu_ khaira_(n), lillazina ahsanu_ fi ha_zihid dunya_ hasanah(tun), wa lada_rul  a_khirati khair(un), wa lani'ma da_rul muttaqin(a), 
31.	Janna_tu 'adniy yadkhulu_naha_ tajri min tahtihal anha_ru lahum fiha_ ma_ yasya_'u_n(a), kaza_lika yajzilla_hul muttaqin(a),
32.	Allazina tatawaffa_humul mala_'ikatu tayyibin(a), yaqu_lu_na sala_mun 'alaikum-udkhulul jannata bima_ kuntum ta'malu_n(a).
33.	Hal yanzuru_na illa_ an ta'tiyahumul mala_'ikatu au ya'tiya amru rabbik(a), kaza_lika fa'alal lazina min qablihim, wa ma_ zalamahumulla_hu wa la_kin ka_nu_ anfusahum yazlimu_n(a).
34.	Fa asa_bahum sayyi'a_tu ma_  'amilu_ wa ha_qa bihim ma_ ka_nu_  bihi yastahzi'u_n(a).
35.	Wa qa_lal lazina asyraku_ lau sya_'alla_hu ma_ 'abadna_ min  da_nihi min syai'in nahnu wa la_ a_ba_'una_ wa la_ harramna_ min du_nihi min syai'(in), kaza_lika fa'alal lazina min qablihim, fa hal 'alar rusuli illal bala_gul mubin(u).
36.	Wa laqad ba'asna_ fi kulli  ummatir rasu_lan an-i'budulla_ha wa-jtanibu_t ta_gu_t(a), fa minhum man hadalla_hu wa minhum man haqqat 'alaihid dala_lah(tu), fa siru_ fil ardi fa-nzuru_ kaifa ka_na 'a_qibatul mukazzibin(a).
37.	In tahris 'ala_ huda_hum fa innalla_ha la_ yahdi may yudillu wa ma_ lahum min na_sirin(a).
38.	Wa aqsamu_ billa_hi jahda aima_nihim, la_ yab'asulla_hu may yamu_t(u), bala_ wa'dan  'alaihi haqqaw wa la_kinna aksaran na_si la_ ya'lamu_n(a),
39.	Liyubayyina lahumul lazi yakhtalifu_na fihi wa  liya'lamal lazina kafaru_ annahum ka_nu_ ka_zibin(a).
40.	Innama_ qauluna_ lisyai'in iza_ aradna_hu an naqu_la lahu_ kun fayaku_n(u).
41.	Wallazina ha_jaru_ filla_hi mim ba'di ma_ zulimu_ lanubawwi'annahum fid dunya_ hasanah(tan), wa la'ajrul a_khirati akbar(u), lau ka_nu_  ya'lamu_n(a),
42.	Allazina sabaru_ wa 'ala_ rabbihim yatawakkalu_n(a).
43.	Wa ma_ arsalna_ min qablika illa_ riju_lan nu_hi ilaihim fas'alu_ ahlaz zikri in kuntum la_ ta'lamu_n(a),
44.	Bil bayyina_ti waz zubur(i), wa anzalna_ ilaikaz zikra  litubayyina lin na_si ma_  nuzzila ilaihim wa la'allahum yatafakkaru_n(a).
45.	Afa'aminal lazina makarus sayyi'a_ti ay yakhsifalla_hu bihimul arda au ya'tiyahumul 'aza_bu min haisu la_ yasy'uru_n(a),
46.	Au ya'khuzahum fi taqallubihim fama_ hum bi mu'jizin(a),
47.	Au ya'khuzahum 'ala_ takhawwuf(in), fa inna  rabbakum lara'u_fur  rahim(un).
48.	Awalam yarau ila_ ma_  khalaqalla_hu min syai'iy yatafayya'u zila_luhu_ 'anil yamini wasy syama_'ili sujjadal lilla_hi wa hum  da_khiru_n(a).
49.	Wa lilla_hi yasjudu ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ardi min da_bbatiw wal mala_'ikatu wa hum la_ yastakbiru_n(a).
50.	Yakha_fu_na rabbahum min fauqihim wa yaf'alu_na ma_ yu'maru_n(a).
51.	Wa qa_lalla_hu la_ tattakhizu_ ila_haini-snain(i), innama_ huwa ila_huw wa_hidun fa iyya_ya fa-rhabu_n(i).
52.	Wa lahu_ ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa lahud dinu  wa_siba_(n), afa gairalla_hi tattaqu_n(a).
53.	Wa ma_ bikum min ni'matin fa minalla_hi summa iza_ massakumud durru fa ilaihi taj'aru_n(a).
54.	Summa iza_ kasyafad durra 'ankum iza_ fariqum minkum bi rabbihim yusyriku_n(a),
55.	Liyakfuru_ bima_ a_tain_hum, fa tamatta'u_, fa saufa ta'lamu_n(a).
56.	Wa yaj'alu_na lima_ la_  ya'lamu_na nasibam mimma_ razaqna_hum, talla_hi latus'alunna 'amma_ kuntum taftaru_n(a).
57.	Wa yaj'alu_na lilla_hil bana_ti subha_nah(u_), wa lahum ma_ yasytahu_n(a).
58.	Wa iza_ busysyira ahaduhum bil unsa_ zalla wajhuhu_ muswaddaw wa huwa kazim(un).
59.	Yatawa_ra_ minal qaumi min su_'i ma_ busysyira bih(i), ayumsikuhu_ 'ala_ hu_nin am yadussuhu_ fit tura_b(i), ala_ sa_'a ma_ yahkumu_n(a).
60.	Lillazina la_ yu'minu_na bil  a_khirati masalus sau'(i), wa lilla_hil masalul a'la_, wa huwal 'azizul hakim(u).
61.	Wa lau yu'a_khizulla_hun na_sa bi zulmihim ma_ taraka 'alaiha_ min da_bbatiw wa la_kiy yu'akhkhiruhum ila_ ajalim musamma_(n), fa iza_  ja_'a ajaluhum la_ yasta'khiru_na sa_'ataw wa la_ yastaqdimu_n(a).
62.	Wa yaj'alu_na lilla_hi ma_  yakrahu_na wa tasifu alsinatuhumul kaziba anna lahumul husna_ la_ jarama anna  lahumun na_ra wa annahum  mufratu_n(a).
63.	Talla_hi laqad arsalna_ ila_ umamim min qablika fa zayyana lahumusy syaita_nu a'ma_lahum fa huwa waliyyuhumul yauma wa lahum 'aza_bun alim(un).
64.	Wa ma_ anzalna_ 'alaikal kita_ba illu_ litubayyina lahumul lazi-khtalafu_ fih(i), wa hudaw wa rahmatal liqaumiy yu'minu_n(a).
65.	Walla_hu anzala minas sama_'i ma_'an fa ahya_ bihil arda ba'da mautiha_, inna fi za_lika la a_yatal liqaumiy yasma'u_n(a).
66.	Wa inna lakum fil an'a_mi la'ibrah(tan), nusqikum  mimma_ fi butu_nihi mim baini  farsiw wa damil labanan  kha_lisan sa_'igal lisy  sya_ribin(a).
67.	Wa min samara_tin nakhili wal  a'na_bi tattakhizu_na minhu  sakaraw wa rizqan hasana_(n), inna fi za_lika la a_yatal liqaumiy ya'qilu_n(a).
68.	Wa auha_ rabbuka ilan nahli an-ittakhizi minal jiba_li buyu_taw wa minasy syajari wa mimma_ ya'risyu_n(a).
69.	Summa kuli min kullis samara_ti fa-sluki subula rabbiki zulula_(n), yakhruju mim butu_niha_ syara_bum mukhtalifun alwa_nuh(u_), fihi syifa_'ul lin na_s(i), inna fi za_lika la a_yatal liqaumiy yatafakkaru_n(a).
70.	Walla_hu khalaqakum summa yatawaffa_kum wa minkum may yuraddu ila_ arzalil 'umuri likaila_ ya'lama ba'da 'ilmin  syaia'a_(n), innalla_ha 'alimun  qadir(un).
71.	Walla_hu faddala ba'dakum 'ala_ ba'din fir rizq(i),  famal lazina fuddilu_ bi ra_ddi rizqihim 'ala_ ma_ malakat aima_nuhum fahum fihi sawa_'(un), fabini'matilla_hi yajhadu_n(a).
72.	Walla_hu ja'ala lakum min anfusikum azwa_jaw wa ja'ala lakum min azwa_jikum banina wa hafadataw wa razaqakum minat tayyiba_t(i), afabil ba_tili yu'minu_na wa bini'matilla_hi hum yakfuru_n(a).
73.	Wa ya'budu_na min du_nilla_hi ma_ la_ yamliku lahum rizqam minas sama_wa_ti wal ardi syai'aw wa la_ yastati'u_n(a).
74.	Fala_ tadribu_ lilla_hil amsa_l(a), innalla_ha ya'lamu wa antum la_ ta'lamu_n(a).
75.	Daraballa_hu masalan 'abdam mamlu_kal la_ yaqdiru 'ala_ syai'iw wa mar razaqna_hu minna_ rizqan hasanan fa huwa  yunfiqu minhu sirraw wa jahra_(n), hal yastawu_n(a), al hamdu lilla_h(i), bal aksaruhum la_ ya'lamu_n(a).
76.	Wa daraballa_hu masalar rajulaini ahaduhuma_ abkamu  la_ yaqdiru 'ala_ syai'iw wa huwa kullun 'ala_ maul_h(u), ainama_ yuwajjihhu la_ ya'ti bi khair(in), la_ yastawi huw(a), wa may ya'muru bil 'adli wa huwa 'ala_ sira_tim mustaqim(in).
77.	Wa lilla_hi gaibus sama_wa_ti wal ard(i), wa ma_ amrus sa_'ati illa_ ka lamhil basari au huwa aqrab(u), innalla_ha  'ala_ kulli syai'in qadir(un).
78.	Walla_hu akhrajakum mim  butu_ni ummaha_tikum la_ ta'lamu_na syai'a_(w), wa ja'ala lakumus sam'a wal absa_ra wal af'idah(ta), la'allakum tasykuru_n(a).
79.	Alam yarau ilat tairi  musakhkhara_tin fi jawwis sama_'(i),ma_ yumsikuhunna illalla_h(u), inna fi za_lika la a_ya_til liqaumiy  yu'minu_n(a).
80.	Walla_hu ja'ala lakum mim buyu_tikum sakanaw wa ja'ala lakum min julu_dil an'a_mi buyu_tan tastakhiffu_naha_  yauma za'nikum wa yauma iqa_matikum, wa min aswa_fiha_ wa adba_riha_ wa asy'a_riha_ asa_saw wa mata_'an ila_  hin(in).
81.	Walla_hu ja'ala lakum mimma_ khalaqa zila_law wa ja'ala  lakum minal jiba_li akna_naw wa ja'ala lakum sara_bila taqikumul harra wa sara_bila  taqikum ba'sakum, kaza_lika yutimmu ni'matahu_ 'alaikum la'allakum tuslimu_n(a).
82.	Fa in tawallau fa innama_  'alaikal bala_gul mubin(u).
83.	Ya'rifu_na ni'matalla_hi summa yunkiru_naha_ wa aksaruhumul ka_firu_n(a).
84.	Wa yauma nab'asu min kulli ummatin syahidan summa la_  yu'zana lillazina kafaru_ wa la_ hum yusta'tabu_n(a).
85.	Wa iza_ ra'al lazina zalamul  'aza_ba fala_ yukhaffafu 'anhum wa la_ hum  yunzaru_n(a).
86.	Wa iza_ ra'al lazina asyraku_  syuraka_'ahum qa_lu_ rabbana_ ha_'ula_'i syuraka_'unal lazina kunna_ nad'u_ min du_nik(a), fa alqau ilaihimul qaula innakum laka_zibu_n(a).
87.	Wa alqau ilalla_hi yauma'izinis salama wa dalla 'anhum ma_ ka_nu_ yaftaru_n(a).
88.	Allazina kafaru_ wa saddu_ 'an sabililla_hi zidna_hum 'aza_ban fauqal 'aza_bi bima_ ka_nu_  yufsidu_n(a).
89.	Wa yauma nab'asu fi kulli ummatin syahidan 'alaihim min anfusihim wa ji'na_ bika syahidan 'ala_ ha_'ula_'(i), wa nazzalna_ 'alaikal kita_ba tibya_nal likulli syai'iw wa hudaw wa rahmataw wa busyra_ lil muslimin(a).
90.	Innalla_ha ya'muru bil 'adli wal ihsa_ni wa ita_'i zil qurba_ wa yanha_ 'anil fahsya_'i wal munkari wal bagyi ya'izukum la'allakum tazakkaru_n(a).
91.	Wa aufu_ bi 'ahdilla_hi iza_  'a_hattum wa la_ tanqudul aima_na ba'da taukidiha_ wa qad ja'altumulla_ha 'alaikum kafila_(n), innalla_ha ya'lamu ma_ taf'alu_n(a).
92.	Wa la_ taku_nu_ kal lati  naqadat 'azlaha_ mim ba'di quwwatin anka_sa_(n), tattakhizu_na aima_nakum dakhalam bainakum an taku_na ummatun hiya arba_ min ummah(tin), innama_ yablu_kumulla_hu bih(i), wa layubayyinanna lakum yaumal qiya_mati ma_ kuntum fihi takhtalifu_n(a).
93.	Wa lau sya_'alla_hu laja'alakum ummataw wa_hidataw wa la_kiy yudillu may yasya_'u wa yahdi may yasya_'(u), wa latus'alunna  'amma_ kuntum ta'malu_n(a).
94.	Wa la_ tattakhizu_ aima_nakum dakhalam bainakum fa tazilla qadamum ba'da subu_tiha_ wa tazu_qus su_'a bima_ sadattum 'an sabililla_h(i), wa lakum 'aza_bun 'azim(un).
95.	Wa la_ tasytaru_ bi'ahdilla_hi samanan qalila_(n), innama_  'indalla_hi huwa khairul lakum in kuntum ta'lamu_n(a).
96.	Ma_ 'indakum yanfadu wa ma_ 'indalla_hi ba_q(in), wa lanajziyannal lazina sabaru_ ajrahum bi ahsani ma_ ka_nu_  ya'malu_n(a).
97.	Man 'amila sa_liham min zakarin au unsa_ wa huwa mu'minun fa lanuhyiyannahu_ haya_tan tayyibah(tan), wa lanajziyannahum ajrahum bi ahsani ma_ ka_nu_ ya'malu_n(a).
98.	Fa iza_ qara'tal qur'a_na fa-sta'iz billa_hi minasy syaita_nir rajim(i).
99.	Innahu_ laisa lahu_ sulta_nun 'alal lazina a_manu_ wa 'ala_ rabbihim yatawakkalu_n(a).
100.	Innama_ sulta_nuhu_ nalal lazi yatawallaunahu_ wal lazina  hum bihi musyriku_n(a).
101.	Wa iza_ baddalna_ a_yatam maka_na a_yah(tin), walla_hu a'lamu bima_ yunazzilu qa_lu_ innama_ anta muftar(in), bal aksaruhum la_ ya'lamu_n(a).
102.	Qul nazzalahu_ ru_hul qudusi mir rabbika bil haqqi liyusabbital lazina a_manu_ wa hudaw wa busyra_ lil muslimin(a).
103.	Wa laqad na'lamu annahum yaqu_lu_na innama_ yu'allimuhu_ basyar(un), lisa_nul lazi yulhidu_na ilaihi a'jamiyyuw wa ha_za_ lisa_nun 'arabiyyum mubin(un).
104.	Innal lazina la_ yu'minu_na bi a_ya_tilla_h(i), la_ yahdihimulla_hu wa lahum  'aza_bun alim(un).
105.	Innama_ yaftaril kazibal lazina la_ yu'minu_na bi  a_ya_tilla_h(i), wa ula_'ika humul ka_zibu_n(a).
106.	Man kafara billa_hi mim ba'di ima_nihi illa_ man ukriha wa qalbuhu_ mutma'innum bil ima_ni wala_kin man syaraha bil kufri sadran fa 'alaihim gadabum minalla_h(i), wa lahum 'aza_bun 'azim(un).
107.	Za_lika bi annahum-ustahabbul haya_tad dunya_ 'alal a_khirah(ti), wa  annalla_ha la_ yahdil qaumal ka_firin(a).
108.	Ula_'ikal lazina taba'alla_hu 'ala_ qulu_bihim wa sam'ihim wa absa_rihim, wa ula_'ika humul ga_filu_n(a).
109.	La_ jarama annahum fil a_khirati humul kha_siru_n(a).
110.	Summa inna rabbaka lillazina ha_jaru_ mim ba'di ma_ futinu_ summa ja_hadu_ wa sabaru_, inna rabbaka mim ba'diha_ lagafu_rur  rahim(un).
111.	Yauma ta'ti kullu nafsin tuja_dilu 'an nafsiha_ wa tuwaffa_ kullu nafsim ma_ 'amilat wa hum la_ yuzlamu_n(a).
112.	Wa daraballa_hu masalan qaryatan ka_nat a_minatam mutma'innatay ya'tiha_ rizquha_ ragadam min kulli maka_nin fa kafarat bi an'umilla_hi fa aza_qahalla_hu liba_sal ju_'i wal khaufi bima_ ka_nu_ yasna'u_n(a).
113.	Wa laqad ju_'ahum rasu_lum minhum fa kazzabu_hu fa akhazahumul 'azu_bu wa hum  za_limu_n(a).
114.	Fa kula_ mimma_ razaqakumulla_hu hala_lan tayyiba_(w), wa-sykuru_ ni'matalla_hi in kuntum iyya_hu ta'budu_n(a).
115.	Innama_ harrama 'alaikumul maitata wad dama wa lahmal khinziri wa ma_ uhilla ligairilla_hi bih(i), faman-idturra gaira ba_giw wa la_ 'a_din fa innalla_ha  gafu_rur rahim(un).
116.	Wa la_ taqu_lu_ lima_ tasifu alsinatukumul kaziba ha_za_ hal_luw wa ha_za_ hara_mul litaftaru_ 'alalla_hil kazib(a), innal lazina yaftaru_na 'alalla_hil kaziba la_ yuflihu_n(a).
117.	Mata_'un qaliluw wa lahum 'aza_bun alim(un).
118.	Wa 'alal lazina ha_du_ harramna_ ma_ qasasna_ 'alaika min qabl(u), wa ma_ zalamna_hum wa la_kin ka_nu_ anfusahum yazlimu_n(a).
119.	Summa inna rabbaka lillazina 'amilus su_'a bi jaha_latin summa ta_bu_ mim ba'di za_lika wa aslahu_ inna rabbaka mim ba'diha_ lagafu_rur rahim(un).
120.	Inna ibra_hima ka_na ummatan qa_nital lilla_hi hanifa_(n), wa lam yaku minal musyrikin(a),
121.	Sya_kiral li'an'umih(i), ijtaba_hu wa hada_hu ila_  sira_tim mustaqim(in).
122.	Wa a_taina_hu fid dunya_  hasanah(tan) wa innahu_ fil a_khirati  laminas sa_lihin(a).
123.	Summa auhaina_ ilaika an-ittabi' millata ibra_hima hanifa_(n), wa ma_ ka_na minal musyrikin(a).
124.	Innama_ ju'ilas sabtu 'alal lazina-khtalafu_ fih(i), wa inna rabbaka layahkumu bainahum yaumal qiya_mati fima_ ka_nu_ fihi yakhtalifu_n(a).
125.	Ud'a_ ila_ sabili rabbika bil hikmati wal mau'izatil hasanati wa ja_dilhum bil lati hiya ahsan(u), inna rabbaka huwa a'lamu biman dalla 'an sabilihi wa huwa a'lamu bil muhtadin(a).
126.	Wa in 'a_qabtum fa 'a_qibu_ bi misli ma_ 'u_qibtum bih(i), wa la'in sabartum lahuwa khairul lis sa_birin(a).
127.	Wa-sbir wa ma_ sabruka illa_ billa_hi wa la_ tahzan 'alaihim wa la_ taku fi daiqim mimma_ yamkuru_n(a).
128.	Innalla_ha ma'al lazina-ttaqau wal lazina  hum muhsinu_n(a).
.EndTopic
;_____________________________
.Topic qsBaniIsra_'il " 17. Bani Isra_'il"
1.	Subha_nal lazi asra_ bi nabdihi  lailam minal masjidil hara_mi ilal masjidil aqsal lazi ba_rakna_ haulahu_ linuriyahu_  min a_ya_tina_, innahu_ huwas sami'ul basir(u).  
2.	Wa a_taina_ mu_sal kita_ba wa ja'alna_hu hudal libani isra_'ila alla_ tattakhiztu_ min du_ni wakila_(n).
3.	Zurriyyata man hamalna_ ma'a nu_h(in), innahu_ ka_na 'abdan syaku_ra_(n).
4.	Wa qadaina_ ila_ bani isra_'ila fil kita_bi latufsidunna filardi marrataini wa lata'lunna 'uluwwan kabira_(n).
5.	Fa iza_ ja_'a wa'du u_la_huma_  ba'asna_ 'alaikum 'iba_dal lana_ uli ba'sin syadidin fa ja_su_ khila_lad diya_r(i), wa ka_na wa'dam maf'u_la_(n).
6.	Summa radadna_ lakumul karrata 'alaihim wa amdadna_kum bi amwa_liw wa banina wa ja'alna_kum aksara nafira_(n).
7.	In ahsantum ahsantum li anfusikum, wa in asa'tum falaha_, fa iza_ ja_'a wa'dul a_khirati liyasu_'u wuju_hakum wa liyadkhulul masjida kama_ dakhalu_hu awwala marratiw wa liyutabbiru_ ma_ 'alau tatbira_(n).
8.	'Asa_ rabbukum ay yarhamakum, wa in 'uttum 'udna_, wa ja'alna_ jahannama lil ka_firina hasira_(n).
9.	Inna ha_zal qur'a_na yahdi lil  lati hiya aqwamu wa  yubasysyirul mu'mininal lazina ya'malu_nas sa_liha_ti anna lahum ajran kabira_(w),
10.	Wa annal lazina la_ yu'minu_na bil a_khirati a'tadna_ lahum 'aza_ban alima_(n).
11.	Wa yad'ul insa_nu bisy syarri du'a_'ahu_ bil khair(i), wa ka_nal insa_nu 'aju_la_(n).
12.	Wa ja'alnal laila wan naha_ra a_yataini fa mahauna_ a_yatal laili wa ja'alna_a a_yatan naha_ri mubsiratal li tabtagu_ fadlam mir rabbikum wa lita'lamu_ 'adadas sinina wal  hisa_b(a), wa kulla syai'in fassalna_hu tafsila_(n).
13.	Wa kulla insa_nin alzamna_hu ta_'irahu_ fi 'unuqih(i), wa nukhriju lahu_ yaumal qiya_mati kita_bay yalqa_hu mansyu_ra_(n).
14.	Iqra' kita_bak(a), kafa_ bi nafsikal yauma 'alaika hasiba_(n).
15.	Man-ihtada_ fa innama_ yahtadi li nafsih(i), wa man dalla fa innama_ yadillu 'alaiha_, wa la_ taziru wa_ziratuw wizra ukhra_, wa ma_ kunna_ mu'azzibina hatta_ nab'asa rasu_la_(n).
16.	Wa iza_ aradna_ an nuhlika qaryatan amarna_ mutrafiha_ fa fasaqu_ fiha_ fa haqqa 'alaihal qaulu fa dammarna_ha_ tadmira_(n).
17.	Wa kam ahlakna_ minal quru_ni mim ba'di nu_h(in), wa kafa_ bi rabbika bi zunu_bi 'iba_dihi khabiram basira_(n).
18.	Man ka_na yuridul 'a_jilata'ajjalna_ lahu_ fiha_ ma_ nasya_'u liman nuridu summa ja'alna_ lahu_ jahannam(a), yasla_ha_ mazmu_mam madhu_ra_(n).
19.	Wa man ara_dal a_khirata wa sa'a_ laha_ sa'yaha_ wa huwa mu'minun fa ula_'ika ka_na sa'yuhum masyku ra_(n).
20.	Kullan numiddu ha_'ula_'i wa ha_'ula_'i min 'ata_'i rabbik(a), wa ma_ ka_na 'ata_'u rabbika mahzu_ra_(n).
21.	Unzur kaifa faddalna_ a'dahum 'ala_ ba'd(in), wa la la_khiratu akbaru daraja_tiw wa akbaru tafdila_(n).
22.	La_ taj'al ma'alla_hi ila_han  a_khara fa taq'uda mazmu_mam makhzu_la_(n).
23.	Wa qada_ rabbuka alla_ ta'budu_ illa_ iyya_hu wa bil wa_lidaini ihsa_na_(n), imma_ yabluganna'indakal kibara ahaduhuma_ au kila_huma_ fala_ taqul lahuma_ uffiw wa la_ tanharhuma_ wa  qul lahuma_ qaulan karima_(n).
24.	Wa-khfid lahuma_ jana_haz  zulli minar rahmati wa qur  rabbi-rhamhuma_ kama_ rabbaya_ni sagira_(n).
25.	Rabbukum a'lamu bima_ fi nufu_sikum, in taku_nu_ sa_lihina fa innahu_ ka_na lil  awwa_bina gafu_ra_(n).
26.	Wa a_ti zal qurba_ haqqahu_ wal miskina wa-bnas sabili wa la_  tubazzir tabzira_(n).
27.	Innal mubazzirina ka_nu_ ikhwa_nasy syaya_tin(i), wa ka_nasy syaita_nu li rabbihi kafu_ra_(n).
28.	Wa imma_ tu'ridanna 'anhumu-btiga_'a rahmatim mir rabbika tarju_ha_ fa qul lahum qaulam maisu_ra_(n).
29.	Wa la_ taj'al yadaka maglu_latan ila_ 'unuqika wa la_ tabsutha_ kullal basti fa taq'uda malu_mam mahsu_ra_(n).
30.	Inna rabbaka yabsutur rizqa limay yasya_'u wa yaqdir(u), innahu_ ka_na bi 'iba_dihi khabiram basira_(n).
31.	Wa la_ taqtulu_ aula_dakum khasy-yata imla_q(in), nahnu narzuquhum wa iyya_kum, inna qatlahum ka_na khit'an kabira_(n).
32.	Wa la_ taqrabuz zina_ innahu_ ka_na fa_hisyah(tan), wa sa_'a sabila_(n).
33.	Wa la_ taqtulun nafsal lati harramalla_hu illa_ bil haqq(i), wa man qutila mazlu_man faqad ja'alna_ li waliyyihi sulta_nan fala_  yusrif fil qatl(i), innahu_ ka_na mansu_ra_(n).
34.	Wa la_ ataqrabu_ ma_lal yatimi illa_ billati hiya ahasanu hatta_ yabluga asyuddah(u_),wa aufu_ bil 'ahd(i), innal 'ahda ka_na mas'u_lu_(n).
35.	Wa auful kaila iza_ kiltum wa  zinu_ bil qista_sil  mustaqim(i), za_lika khairuw wa ahsanu ta'wila_(n).
36.	Wa la_ taqfu ma_ laisa laka  bihi 'ilm(un), innas sam'a  wal basara wal fu'a_da kullu ula_'ika ka_na 'anhu mas'u_la_(n).
37.	Wa la_ tamsyi fil ardi  maraha_(n), innaka lan takhriqal arda wa lan tablugal jiba_la tu_la_(n).
38.	Kullu za_lika ka_na sayyi'uhu_ 'inda rabbika makru_ha_(n).
39.	Za_lika mimma_ auha_ ilaika  rabbuka minal hikmah(ti), wa la_ taj'al ma'alla_hi ila_han a_khara fa tulqa_ fi jahannama malu_mam madhu_ra_(n).
40.	Afa asfa_kum rabbukum bil banina wa-ttakhaza minal mala_'ikati ina_sa_(n), innakum lataqu_lu_na qaulan 'azima_(n).
41.	Wa laqad sarrafna_ fi ha_zal qura'a_ni liyazzakkaru_, wa ma_ yaziduhum illa_ nafu_ra_(n).
42.	Qul lau ka_na ma'ahu_ a_lihatun  kama_ yaqu_lu_na izal la-btagau ila_ zil 'arsyi sabila_(n).
43.	Subha_nahu_ wa ta'a_la_ 'amma_ yaqu_lu_na 'uluwwan kabira_(n).
44.	Tusabbihu lahus sama_wa_tus  sab'u wal ardu wa man fihinn(a), wa im min syai'in illa_ yusabbihu bi hamdihi wa  la_kil la_ tafqahu_na tasbihahum, innahu_ ka_na  haliman gafu_ra_(n).
45.	Wa iza_ qara'tal qur'a_na ja'alna_ bainaka wa bainal lazina la_ yu'minu_na bil a_khirati hija_bam mastu_ra_(w),
46.	Wa ja'alna_ 'ala_ qulu_bihim akinnatan ay yafqahu_hu wa fi a_za_nihim waqra_(n), wa iza_ zakarta rabbaka fil qur'a_ni wahdahu_ wallau 'ala_ adba_rihim nufu_ra_(n).
47.	Nahnu a'lamu bima_  yastami'u_na bihi iz  yastami'u_na ilaika wa iz hum najwa_ iz yaqu_luz za_limu_na in tattabi'u_na illa_ rajulam  mashu_ra_(n).
48.	Unzur kaifa daraba_ lakal ama_la fa dallu_ fala_  yastati'u_na sabila_(n).
49.	Wa qa_lu_ a'iza_ kunna_ 'iza_maw wa rufa_tan a'inna_  lamab'u_su_na khalqan  jadida_(n).
50.	Qul ku_nu_ hija_ratan au  hadida_(n),
51.	Au khalqam mimma_ yakburu fi sudu_rikum, fa sayaqu_lu_na may yu'iduna_, qulil lazi fatarakum awwala marrah(tin), fa sayungidu_na  ilaika ru'u_sahum wa yaqu_lu_na mata_ huw(a), qul 'asa_ ayyaku_na qariba_(n).
52.	Yauma yad'u_kum fa  tastajibu_na bi hamdihi wa  tazunnu_na il labistum illa_ qalila_(n).
53.	Wa qul li'iba_di yaqu_lul lati hiya ahsan(u), innasy  syaita_na yanzagu bainahum , innasy syaita_na ka_na lil  insa_ni 'aduwwam mubina_(n).
54.	Rabbukum a'lamu bikum, iy yasya' yarhamkum au iy yasya' yu'azzibkum, wa ma_ arsalna_ka 'alaihim wakila_(n).
55.	Wa rabbuka a'lamu biman fis sama_wa_ti wal ard(i), wa ladaq faddalna_ ba'dan nabiyyina 'ala_ ba'diw wa a_taina_ da_wu_da zabu_ra_(n).
56.	Qul-id'ul lazina za'amtum min du_nihi fala_ yamliku_na kasyfad durri 'ankum wa la_ tahwila_(n). 57.Ula_'ikal lazina yad'u_na yabtagu_na ilu_ rabbihimul wasilata ayyuhum aqrabu wa yarj_na rahmatahu_ wa yakha_fu_na 'aza_bah(u_), inna  'aza_ba rabbika ka_na  mahzu_ra_(n).
58.	Wa im min qaryatin illa_  nahnu muhliku_ha_ qabla yaumil  qiya_mati au mu'azzibu_ha_ 'aza_ban syadida_(n), ka_na  za_lika fil kita_bi mastu_ra_(n).
59.	Wa ma_ mana'ana_ an nursila bil a_ya_ti illa_ an kazzaba bihal awwalu_n(a), wa a_taina_ samu_dan na_qata mubsiratan fazalamu_ biha_, wa ma_ nursilu bil a_ya_ti illa_ takhwifa_(n).
60.	Wa iz qulna_ laka inna  rabbaka aha_ta bin na_s(i), wa ma_ ja'alnar ru'yal lati araina_ka illa_ fitnatal lin na_si wasy syajaratal  mal'u_nata fil qur'a_n(i), wa nukhawwifuhum, fama_ yaziduhum illa_ tugya_nan kabira_(n).
61.	Wa iz qulna_ lil  mala_'ikati-sjudu_ li a_dama fasajadu_ illa_ iblis(a), qa_la a'asjudu liman khalaqta tina_(n).
62.	Qa_la ara'aitaka ha_zal lazi karramta 'alayya la'in akhkhartani ila_ yaumil qiya_mati la'ahtanikanna zurriyyatahu_ illa_ qalila_(n).
63.	Qa_la-zhab faman tabi'aka minhum fa inna jahannama jaza_'ukum jaza_'am maufu_ra_(n).
64.	Wa-stafziz man-istata'ta minhum bi sautika wa ajlib 'alaihim bi khailika wa rajilika wa sya_rik-hum fil amwa_li wal aula_di wa 'idhum, wa ma_ ya'iduhumusy syaita_nu illa_ guru_ra_(n).
65.	Inna 'iba_di laisa laka 'alaihim sulta_n(un), wa kafa_  bi rabbika wakila_(n).
66.	Rabbukumul lazi yuzji lakumul fulka fil bahri litabtagu_ min fadlih(i), innahu_ ka_na bikum rahimu_(n).
67.	Wa iza_ massakumud durru fil bahri dalla man tad'u_na illa_ iyya_h(u), falamma_ najja_kum ilal barri a'radtum, wa  ka_nal insa_nu kafu_ra_(n).
