68.	Afa amintum ay yakhsifa bikum ja_nibal barri au yursila 'alaikum ha_siban summa la_ tajidu lakum wakila_(n),
69.	Am amintum ay yu'idakum fihi ta_ratan ukhra_ fayursila 'alaikum qa_sifam minar rihi fayugriqakum bima_ kafartum, summa la_ tajidu lakum'alaina_ bihi tabi'a_(n).
70.	Wa laqad karramna_ bani a_dama wa hamalna_hum fil barri wal bahri wa razaqna_hum minat tayyiba_ti wa faddalna_hum 'ala_ kasirim mimman khalaqna_ tafdila_(n).
71.	Yauma nad'u_ kulla una_sim bi ima_mihim, faman u_tiya kita_bahu_ bi yaminihi fa ula_'ika yaqra'u_na kita_bahum wa la_ yuzlamu_na fatila_(n).
72.	Wa man ka_na fi ha_zihi a'ma_ fa huwa fil a_khirati a'ma_ wa adallu sabila_(n).
73.	Wa in ka_du_ layaftinu_naka 'anil lazi auhaina_ ilaika litaftariya 'alaina_ gairah(u_), wa izal la-ttakhazu_ka khalila_(n).
74.	Wa lau la_ an sabbatna_ka  laqad kitta tarkanu ilaihim  syai'an qalila_(n), 
75.	Izal la'azaqna_ka di'fal haya_ti wa di'fal mama_ti summa la_ tajidu laka 'alaina_ nasira_(n).
76.	Wa in ka_du_ layastafizzu_naka minal ardi liyukhriju_ka minha_ wa izal la_ yalbasu_na khila_faka illa_ qalila_(n).
77.	Sunnata man qad arsalna_  qablaka mir rusulina_ wa la_ tajidu lisunnatina_  tahwila_(n).
78.	Aqimis sala_ta lidulu_kisy syamsi ila_ gasaqil laili wa qur'a_nal fajr(i), inna qur'a_nal fajri ka_na masyhu_da_(n).
79.	Wa minal laili fa tahajjad bihi na_filatal lak(a), 'asa_ ay yab'asaka rabbuka maqa_mam mahmu_da_(n).
80.	Wa qur rabbi adkhilni mudkhala sidqiw wa akhrijni mukhraja sidqiw wa-j'al li mil ladunka sulta_nan nasira_(n).
81.	Wa qul ja_'al haqqu wa zahaqal ba_til(u), innal ba_tila ka_na zahu_qa_(n).
82.	Wa nunazzilu minal qur'a_ni ma_ huwa syifa_'uw wa rahmatul lil mu'minin(a), wa la_  yaziduz za_limina illa_ khasa_ra_(n).
83.	Wa iza_ an'amna_ 'alal insa_ni a'rada wa na'a_ bi ja_nibih(i), wa iza_ massahusy syarru ka_na ya'u_sa_(a).
84.	Qul kulluy ya'malu 'ala_ sya_kilatih(i), fa rabbukum a'lamu biman huwa ahda_ sabila_(n).
85.	Wa yas'alu_naka 'anir ru_h(i), qulir ru_hu min amri rabbi wa  ma_ u_titum minal 'ilmi illa_ qalila_(n).
86.	Wa la'in syi'na_ lanazhabanna billazi auhaina_ ilaika summa la_ tajidu laka bihi 'alaina_ wakila_(n),
87.	Illa_ rahmatam mir rabbik(a), inna fadlahu_ ka_na 'alaika kabira_(n).
88.	Qul la'inijtama'atil insu wal jinnu 'ala_ ay ya'tu_ bi misli ha_zal qur'a_ni la_ ya'tu_na bi mislihi wa lauka_na ba'dahum liba'din zahira_(n).
89.	Wa laqad sarrafna_ lin na_si fi ha_zal qur'a_ni min kulli masal(in), fa aba_ aksarun na_si illa_ kufu_ra_(n).
90.	Wa qa_lu_ lan nu'mina laka hatta_ tafjura lana_ minal ardi yambu_'a_(n),
91.	Au taku_na laka jannatum min nakhiliw wa 'inabin fa  tufajjiral anha_ra khila_laha_ tafjira_(n),
92.	Au tusqitas sama_'a kama_  za'amta 'alaina_ kisafan au ta'tiya billa_hi wal mala_'ikati qabila_(n),
93.	Au yaku_na laka baitum min zukhrufin au tarqa_ fis sama_'(i), wa lan nu'mina liruqiyyika hatta_ tunazzila 'alaina_ kita_ban naqra'uh(u_), qul subha_na rabbi hal kuntu illa_ basyarar rasu_la_(n).
94.	Wa ma_ mana'an na_sa ay  yu'minu_ iz ja_'ahumul huda_ illa_ an qa_lu_ aba'asalla_hu  basyarar rasu_la_(n).
95.	Qul lau ka_na fil ardi mala_'ikatuy yamsyu_na mutma'innina lanazzalna_ 'alaihim minas sama_'i malakar rasu_la_(n).
96.	Qul kafa_ billa_hi syahidam baini wa bainakum, innahu_ ka_na bi'iba_dihi khabiram basira_(n).
97.	Wa may yahdilla_hu fahuwal muhtad(i), wa may yudlil falan tajida lahum auliya_'a min du_nih(i), wa nahsyuruhum yaumal qiya_mati 'ala_ wuju_hihim 'umyaw wa bukmaw wa summa_(n), ma'wa_hum jahannam(u), kullama_ khabat zidna_hum sa'ira_(n).
98.	Za_lika jaza_'uhum bi annahum kafaru_ bi a_ya_tina_ wa qa_lu_ a'iza_ kunna_ 'iza_maw wa rufa_tan a'inna_ lamab'u_su_na khalqan jadida_(n).
99.	Awalam yarau analla_hal lazi khalaqas sama_wa_ti wal arda qa_dirun 'ala_ ay yakhluqa mislahum wa ja'ala lahum ajalal la_ raiba fih(i), fa abaz za_limu_na illa_  kufu_ru_(n).
100.	Qul lau antum tamliku_na khaza_'ina rahmati rabbi izal la'amsaktum khasy-yatal infa_q(i), wa ka_nal insa_nu qatu_ra_(n).
101.	Wa laqad a_taina_ mu_sa_ tis'a a_ya_tim bayyina_tin fas'al bani isra_'ila iz ja_'ahum faqa_la lahu_ fir'aunu inni la'azunnuka ya_ mu_sa_  mashu_ra_(n).
102.	Qa_la laqad 'alimta ma_  anzala ha_'ula_'i illa_ rabbus sama_wa_ti wal ardi basa_'ir(a), wa inni la'azunnuka ya_ fir'aunu masbu_ra_(n).
103.	Fa ara_da ay yastafizzahum minal ardi fa agraqna_hu wa mam ma'ahu_ jami'a_(w),
104.	Wa qulna_ mim ba'dihi li bani isra_'ila-skunul arda fa iza_ ja_'a wa'dul a_khirati ji'na_ bikum lafifa_(n).
105.	Wa bil haqqi anzalna_hu wa bil haqqi nazal(a), wa ma_ arsalna_ka illa_ mubasysyiraw wa nazira_(n).
106.	Wa qur'a_nan faraqna_hu litaqra'ahu_ 'alan na_si 'ala_ muksiw wa nazzalna_hu tanzila_(n).
107.	Qul a_minu_ bihi au la_ tu'minu_, innal lazina u_tul 'ilma min qablihi iza_ yutla_ 'alaihim yakhirru_na lil azqa_ni sujjada_(w),
108.	Wa yaqu_lu_na subha_na rabbina_  in ka_na wa'du rabbina_  lamaf'u_la_(n).
109.	Wa yakhirru_na lil azqa_ni yabku_na wa yaziduhum khusyu_'a_(n).
110.	Qul-id'ulla_ha aw-id'ur rahma_n(a), ayyam ma_ tad'u_ falahul asma_'ul husna_, wa la_ tajhar bi sala_tika wa la_ tukha_fit biha_ wa-btagi baina za_lika sabila_(n).
111.	Wa qulil hamdu lilla_hil lazi lam yattakhiz waladaw  wa lam yakul lahu_ syarikun fil mulki wa lam yakul lahu_ waliyyum minaz zulli wa kabbirhu takbira_(n).
.EndTopic
;_________________________
.Topic qsAl-Kahfi " 18. Al-Kahfi"
1.	Al hamdu lilla_hil lazi anzala 'ala_ 'abdihil kita_ba wa lam yaj'al lahu_ 'iwaja_(n).
2.	Qayyimal liyunzira ba'san syadidam mil ladunhu wa yubasysyiral mu'mininal lazina ya'malu_nas sa_liha_ti anna lahum ajran hasana_(m),
3.	Ma_kisina fihi abada_(w),
4.	Wa yunziral lazina qa_lu-ttakhazalla_hu walada_(m),
5.	Ma_ lahum bihi min 'ilmiw wa la_ li'a_ba_'ihim, kaburat kalimatan takhruju min afwa_hihim, iy yaqu_lu_na illa_ kaziba_(n).
6.	Fa la'allaka ba_khi'un nafsaka 'ala_ a_sa_rihim il lam yu'minu_  bi ha_zal hadisi asafa_(n).
7.	Inna_ ja'alna_ ma_ 'alal ardi zinatal laha_ linabluwahum ayyuhum ahsanu 'amala_(n).
8.	Wa inna_ laja_'ilu_na ma_ 'alaiha_  sa'idan juruza_(n).
9.	Am hasibta anna asha_bal kahfi  war raqimi ka_nu_ min a_ya_tina_ 'ajaba_(n).
10.	Iz awal fityatu ilal kahfi  faqa_lu_ rabbana_ a_tina_ mil ladunka rahmataw wa hayyi' lana_ min amrina_ rasyada_(n).
11.	Fa darabna_ 'ala_ a_za_nihim fil kahfi sinina 'adada_(n).
12.	Summa ba'asna_hum lina'lama ayyul hizbaini ahsa_ lima_ labisu_ amada_(n).
13.	Nahnu naqussu 'alaika naba'ahum bil haqq(i), innahum fityatun a_manu_ bi rabbihim wa zidna_hum huda_(w), 
14.	Wa rabatna_ 'ala_ qulu_bihim iz qa_mu_ faqa_lu_ rabbuna_ rabbus sama_wa_ti wal ardi lan nad'uwa min du_nihi ila_hal laqad qulna_ izan syatata_(n).
15.	Ha_'ula_'i qaumuna-ttakhazu_ min du_nihi a_lihah(tan), lau la_ ya'tu_na 'alaihim bi sulta_nim bayyin(in), faman azlamu mim man-iftara_ nalalla_hi kaziba_(n).
16.	Wa iz-i'tazaltumu_hum wa ma_ ya'budu_na illalla_ha fa'wu_ ilal kahfi yansyur lakum rabbukum mir rahmatihi wa yuhayyi' lakum min amrikum mirfaqa_(n).
17.	Wa tarasy syamsa iza_ tala'at taza_waru 'an kahfihim za_tal yamini wa iza_ garabat taqriduhum za_tasy syima_li wa hum fi fajwatim minh(u), za_lika min a_ya_tilla_h(i), may yahdilla_hu fa huwal muhtadi wa may yudlil falan tajida lahu_ waliyyam mursyida_(n).
18.	Wa tahsabuhum aiqa_zaw wa hum ruqu_d(uw), wa nuqallibuhum za_tal yamini wa za_tasy syima_l(i), wa kalbuhum ba_situn zira_'aihi bil wasid(i), law-ittala'ta 'alaihim lawallaita minhum fira_raw wa lamuli'ta minhum ru'ba_(n).
19.	Wa kaza_lika ba'asna_hum  liyatasa_'alu_ bainahum, qa_la qa_'ilum minhum kam labistum, qa_lu_ labisna_ yauman au ba'da yaum(in), qa_lu_ rabbukum a'lamu bima_ labistum, fa-b'asu_ ahadakum bi wariqikum ha_zihi ilal madinati falyanzur ayyuha_ azka_ ta'a_man falya'tikum bi rizqim minhu walyatalattaf  wa la_ yusy'iranna bikum ahada_(n).
20.	Innahum iy yazharu_ 'alaikum yarjumu_kum au yu'idu_kum fi millatihim wa lan tuflihu_ izan abada_(n).
21.	Wa kaza_lika a'sarna_ 'alaihim liya'lamu_ anna wa'dalla_hi  haqquw wa annas sa_'ata la_ raiba fiha_, iz yatana_za'u_na bainahum amrahum faqa_lu-bnu_ 'alaihim bunya_na_(n), rabbuhum a'lamu bihim, qa_lal lazina galabu_ 'ala_ amrihim lanattakhizanna 'alaihim masjida_(n).
22.	Sayaqu_lu_na sala_satur ra_bi'uhum kalbuhum, wa yaqu_lu_na khamsatun sa_disuhum kalbuhum rajmam bil gaib(i), wa yaqu_lu_na sab'atuw wa sa_minuhum kalbuhum, qur rabbi a'lamu bi 'iddatihim ma_ ya'lamuhum illa_ qalil(un), fala_ tuma_ri fihim illa_ mira_'an za_hira_(w), wa la_ tastafti fihim minhum ahada_(n).
23.	Wa la_ taqa_lanna lisyai'in inni fa_'ilun za_lika gada_(n),
24.	Illa_ ay yasya_'alla_h(u), wa-zkur rabbaka iza_ nasita wa qul 'asa_ ay yahdiyani rabbi li'aqraba min ha_za_ rasyada_(n).
25.	Wa labisu_ fi kahfihim sala_sa mi'atin sinina wa-zda_du_ tis'a_(n).
26.	Qulilla_hu a'lamu bima_ labisa_, lahu_ gaibus sama_wa_ti wal ard(i), absir bihi wa asmi', ma_ lahum min du_nihi miw waliyy(in), wa la_ yusyriku fi hukmihi  ahada_(n).
27.	Wa-tlu ma_ u_hiya ilaika min kita_bi rabbik(a), la_ mubaddila likalima_tih(i), wa lan tajida min du_nihimultahada_(n).
28.	Wa-sbir nafsaka ma'al lazina yad'u_na rabbahum bil gada_ti wal 'asyiyyi yurida_na wajhahu_ wa la_ ta'du 'aina_ka 'anhum, turidu zinatal haya_tid dunya_, wa la_ tuti' man agfalna_ qalbahu_ 'an zikrina_ wa-ttaba'a hawa_hu wa ka_na amruhu_ furuta_(n).
29.	Wa qulil haqqu mir rabbikum, faman sya_'a falyu'miw wa man sya_'a falyakfur, inna_ a'tadna_ liz za_limina na_ra_(n), aha_ta bihim sura_diquha_, wa iy yastagisu_ yuga_su bi ma_'in kal muhli yasywil wuju_h(a), bi'sasy syara_b(u), wa sa_'at murtafaqa_(n).
30.	Innal lazina a_manu_ wa 'amilus sa_liha_ti inna_ la_ nudi'u ajra man ahsana  'amala_(n).
31.	Ula_'ika lahum janna_tu 'adnin tajri min tahtihimul anha_ru yuhallauna fiha_ min asa_wira min zahabiw wa yalbasu_na siya_ban khudram min sundusiw wa istabraqim muttaki'ina fiha_ 'alal ara_'ik(i), ni'massawa_b(u), wa hasunat murtafaqa_(n).
32.	Wa-drib lahum masalar  rajulaini ja'alna_ li'ahadihima_ jannataini min a'na_biw wa hafafna_huma_ bi nakhliw wa ja'alna_ bainahuma_ zar'a_(n).
33.	Kiltal jannataini a_tat ukulaha_ wa lam tazlim minhu syai'a_(w), wa fajjarna_ khila_lahuma_ nahara_(w),
34.	Wa ka_na lahu_ samar(un), faqa_la lisa_hibihi wa huwa yuha_wiruhu_ ana aksaru minka ma_law wa a'azzu nafara_(n).
35.	Wa dakhala jannatahu_ wa huwa za_limul li nafsih(i), qa_la ma_ azunnu an tabida ha_zihi  abada_(w),
36.	Wa ma_ azunnus sa_'ata qa_'imataw wa la'ir rudittu ila_ rabbi la'ajidanna khairam minha_ munqalaba_(n).
37.	Qa_la lahu_ sa_hibuhu_ wa huwa yuha_wiruhu_ akafarta billazi khalaqaka min tura_bin summa min nutfatin summa sawwa_ka rajula_(n).
38.	La_kinna huwalla_hu rabbi wa la_ usyriku bi rabbi ahada_(n).
39.	Wa lau la_ iz dakhalta jannataka qulta ma_ sya_'alla_h(u), la_ quwwata illa_ billa_h(i), in tarani ana aqalla minka ma_law wa walada_(n).
40.	Fa 'asa_ rabbi ay yu'tiyani khairam min jannatika wa yursila 'alaiha_ husba_nam minas sama_'i fatusbiha sa'idan zalaqa_(n).
41.	Au yusbiha ma_'uha_ gauran falan tastati'a lahu_ talaba_(n).
42.	Wa uhita bi samarihi fa asbaha yuqallibu kaffaihi 'ala_ ma_ anfaqa fiha_ wa hiya kha_wiyatun 'ala_ 'uru_syiha_ wa yaqu_lu ya_ laitani lam usyrik bi rabbi ahada_(n).
43.	Wa lam takul lahu_ fi'atuy yansuru_nahu_ min du_nilla_hi wa ma_ ka_na muntasira_(n).
44.	Huna_likal wala_yatu lilla_hil haqq(i), huwa khairun sawa_baw wa khairun 'uqba_(n).
45.	Wa-drib lahum masalal haya_tid dunya_ kama_'in anzalna_hu minas sama_'i fa-khtalata bihi naba_tul ardi fa asbaha hasyiman tazru_hur riya_h(u), wa ka_nalla_hu 'ala_ kulli syai'im  muqtadira_(n).
46.	Al ma_lu wal banu_na zinatul haya_tid dunya_, wal ba_qiya_tus sa_liha_tu khairun 'inda rabbika sawa_baw wa khairun amala_(n).
47.	Wa yauma nusayyirul jiba_la wa taral arda ba_rizataw wa hasyarna_hum falam nuga_dir minhum ahada_(n).
48.	Wa 'uridu_ 'ala_ rabbika saffa_(n), laqad ji'tumu_na_ kama_ khalaqna_kum awwala marrah(tim), bal za'amtum allan naj'ala lakum mau'ida_(n).
49.	Wa wudi'al kita_bu fataral mujrimina musyfiqina mimma_ fihi wa yaqu_lu_na ya_  wailatana_ ma_li ha_zal kita_bi la_ yuga_diru sagirataw wa la_ kabiratan illa_ ahsa_ha_, wa wajadu_ ma_ 'amilu_ ha_dira_(n), wa la_ yazlimu rabbuka ahada_(n).
50.	Wa iz qulna_ lil mala_'ikati-sjudu_ li'a_dama fasajadu_ illa_ iblis(a), ka_na minal jinni fafasaqa 'an amri rabbih(i), afatattakhizu_nahu_ wa zurriyyatahu_ auliya_'a min du_ni wa hum lakum 'aduww(un), bi'sa liz za_limina badala_(n).
51.	Ma_ asyhattuhum khalqas sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa la_ khalqa anfusihim, wa ma_  kuntu muttakhizal mudillina 'aduda_(n).
52.	Wa yauma yaqu_lu na_du_ syuraka_'iyal lazina za'amtum fa da'auhum falam yastajibu_ lahum wa ja'alna_ bainahum maubiqa_(n).
53.	Wa ra'al mujrimu_nan na_ra fa zannu_ annahum muwa_qi'uha_ wa  lam yajidu_ 'anha_ masrifa_(n).
54.	Wa laqad sarrafna_ fi ha_zal qur'a_ni lin na_si min kulli masal(in), wa ka_nal insa_nu aksara syai'in jadala_(n).
55.	Wa ma_ mana'an na_sa ay yu'minu_ iz ja_'ahumul huda_ wa yastagfiru_ rabbahum illa_ ay ta'tiyahum sunnatul awwalina  au ya'tiyahumul 'azu_bu qubula_(n).
56.	Wa ma_ nursilul mursalina illa_ mubasysyirina wa munzirin(a), wa yuja_dilul  lazina kafaru_ bil ba_tili liyudhidu_ bihil haqqa wa-ttakhazu_ a_ya_ti wa ma_ unziru_ huzuwa_(n).
57.	Wa man azlamu mim man zukkira bi a_ya_ti rabbihi fa a'rada 'anha_ wa nasiya ma_ qaddamat yada_h(u), inna_ ja'alna_ 'ala_ qulu_bihim akinnatan ay yafqahu_hu wa fi a_za_nihim waqra_(n), wa in tad'uhum ilal huda_ falay yahtada_ izan abada_(n).
58.	Wa rabbukal gafu_ru zur rahmah(ti), lau yu'a_khizuhum bima_ kasabu_ la'ajjala lahumul 'aza_b(a), bal lahum mau'idul lay yajidu_ min du_nihi mau'ila_(n).
59.	Wa tilkal qura_ ahlakna_hum  lamma_ zalamu_ wa ja'alna_ limahlikihim mau'ida_(n).
60.	Wa iz qa_la mu_sa_ lifata_hu la_ abrahu hatta_ abluga majma'al bahraini au amdiya  huquba_(n).
61.	Falamma_ balaga majma'a bainihima_ nasiya_ hu_tahuma_ fa-ttakhaza sabilahu_ fil bahri saraba_(n).
62.	Falamma_ ja_waza_ qa_la lifata_hu a_tina_ gada_'ana_, laqad laqina_ min safarina_ ha_za_ nasaba_(n).
63.	Qa_ ara'aita iz awaina_ ilas sakhrati fa inni nasitul hu_t(a), wa ma_ ansa_nihu illasy syaita_nu anazkurah(u_), wa-ttakhaza  sabilahu_ fil bahri 'ajaba_(n).
64.	Qa_la za_lika ma_ kunna_  nabg(i), fa-rtadda 'ala_ a_sa_rihima_ qasasa_(n),
65.	Fa wajada_ 'abdam min'iba_dina_ a_taina_hu rahmatam min 'indina_ wa 'allamna_hu mil ladunna_ 'ilma_(n).
66.	Qa_la lahu_ mu_sa_ hal  attabi'uka 'ala_ an tu'allimani mimma_ 'ullimta rusyda_(n).
67.	Qa_la innaka lan tastati'a ma'iya sabra_(n).
68.	Wa kaifa tasbiru 'ala_ ma_ lam tuhit bihi khubra_(n).
69.	Qa_la satajiduni in sya_'alla_hu sa_biraw wa la_ a'si laka amra_(n).
70.	Qa_la fa in-ittaba'tani fala_ tas'alni 'an syai'in hatta_ uhdisa laka minhu zikra_(n).
71.	Fa-ntalaqa_, hatta_ iza_ rakiba_ fis safinati kharaqaha_, qa_la akharaqtaha_ litugriqa ahlaha_, laqad ji'ta syai'an  imra_(n).
72.	Qa_la alam aqul innaka lan tastati'a ma'iya sabra_(n).
73.	Qa_la la_ tu'a_khizni bima_  nasitu wa la_ turhiqni min amri 'usra_(n).
74.	Fa-ntalaqa_, hatta_ iza_ laqiya_ gula_man faqatalah(u_), qa_la aqatalta nafsan zakiyyatam bi gairi nafs(in), laqad ji'ta syai'an nukra_(n). 
75.	Qa_la alam aqul laka in naka lan tastati'a ma'iya sabra_
76.	Qa_la in sa altuka 'an sai im ba'daha_ fala_ tusha_hibni qad balaghta mil ladun ni 'udzra_
77.	Fanthalaqa_ hat ta_ iza_ ataya_ ahla qaryatinis tat'ama_ ahlaha_ fa abau ay yudhay yifu_huma_ fawajada_ fiha_ jida_ray yuridu ay yanqad dafa aqa_mah qa_la lau syi'ta lat takhazta 'alaihi ajra_
78.	Qa_la ha_za_ fira_qu baini wa bainik sa unab bi uka bita wili ma_ lam tasti 'alaihi shabra_
79.	Am mas safinatu faka_nat limasa_kina ya'malu_na fil bahri fa aratu an a'ibaha_ wa ka_na wara_ ahum ma likuy ya'khudzu kul la safinatin gasba_
80.	Wa am mal gula_mu faka_na abawa_hu mu'minaini fakhasyina_ ay yurhi qahuma_ thughya_naw wa kufra_
81.	Fa aradna_ ay yubdilahuma_ rab buhuma_ khairam minhu zaka_taw wa aqraba ruhma_
82.	Wa am mal jida_ru faka_na lighula_maini yatimaini fil madinati wa ka_na tahtahu_ kanzul lahuma_ wa ka_na abu_huma_ sa_liha_ fa ara_da rabbuka ay yablugha_ asyud dahuma_ wa yastakhrija_ kanzahuma_ rahmatam mir rab bik wa ma_ fa'altuhu_ an amri za_lika ta'wilu ma_ lam tasti 'alaihi sabra_
83.	Wa yas alu_naka 'an dzil qarnain qul sa atlu_ alaikum minhu zikra_
84.	In na_ mak kan na_ lahu_ fil ardi wa a_taina_hu min kul li sai in sababa_
85.	Fa atba'a sababa_
86.	Hat ta_ iza_ balagha magribas samsi wajadaha_ taghrubu fi ainin hami atiw wa wajada 'indaha_ qauma_ qulna_ ya_ zal qarnaini im ma_ an tu'az ziba wa im ma_ an tat takhiza fihim husna_
87.	Qa_la am ma_ man zalama fasaufa nu'az zibuhu_ sum ma yurad du ila_ rab bihi fayu'az zibuhu_ aza_ban nukra_
88.	Wa am ma_ man a_mana wa amila sha_lihan falahu_ jaza_ anil husna_ wa sanaqu_lu lahu_ min amrina_ yusra_
89.	Sum ma atba'a sababa_
90.	Hat ta_ iza_ balagha mathli'as samsi wajadaha_ tathlu'u ala_ qaumil lamnaj'al lahum min du_niha_ sitra_
91.	Kaza_lik wa qad ahathna_ bima_ ladaihi khubra_
92.	Sum ma atba'a sababa_
93.	Hat ta_ iza_ balagha bainas sad daini wajada min du_nihima_ qaumal la_ yaka_du_na yafqahu_na qaula_
94.	Qa_lu_ ya_ zal qarnaini in na yaju_ja wa ma'ju_ja mufsidu_na fil ardi fahal naj'alu laka kharjan 'ala_ an taj'ala bainana_ wa bainahum sad da_
95.	Qa_la ma_ mak kan ni fihi rab bi khairun fa a'inu_ni biquw watin aj'al bainakum wa bainahum radma_
96.	A_tu_ni zubaral hadid hat ta_ iza_ sa_wa_ bainas sadafain qa_lan fukhu_ hat ta_ idza_ ja'alahu_ na_ran qa_la a_tu_ni ufrig 'alaihi qithra_
97.	Famas tha_'u_ ay yazharu_hu wa mas tata_'u_ lahu_ naqba_
98.	Qa_la ha_dza_ rahmatum mir rab bi fa idza_ ja_ a wa'du rab bi ja'alahu_ dak ka_ wa ka_na wa'du rab bi haq qa_
99.	Wa tarakna_ ba'dhahum yauma idziy yamu_ju fi ba'diw wa nufikha fis su_ri fajama'na_hum jam'a_
100.	Wa 'aradhna_ jahan nama yauma idzil lil ka_firina 'ardha_
101.	Nil lazina ka_nat a'yunuhum fi gita_in 'an zikri wa ka_nu_ la_ yastati'una sam'a_
102.	Afahasibal lazina kafaru_ ay yat takhizu_ iba_di min du_ni auliya_ in na_ a'tadna_ jahan nama lilka_firina nuzula_
103.	Qul hal nunab bi ukum bil akhsarina a'ma_la_
104.	Al lazina dhal la sa'yuhum fil haya_tid dun ya_ wa hum yahsabu_na an nahum yuhsinu_na shun'a_
105.	Ula_ ikal lazina kafaru_ bi a_ya_ti rab bihim wa liqa_ ihi fahabitat a'ma_luhum fala_ nuqimu lahum yaumal qiya_mati wazna_
106.	Za_lika jaza_uhum jahan namu bima_ kafaru_ wat takhadzu_ a_ya_ti wa rusuli huzuwa_
107.	In nal lazina a_manu_ wa 'amilus sa_liha_ti ka_nat lahum jan na_tul firdausi nuzula_
108.	Kha_lidina fiha_ la_ yabghu_na 'anha_ hiwala_
109.	Qul lau ka_nal bahru mida_dal likalima_ti rab bi lanafidal bahru qabla antanfada kalima_tu rab bi wa lau ji na_ bimitslihi madada_
110.	Qul in nama_ ana basyarum mitslukum yu_ha_ ilay ya an nama_ ila_hukum ila_huw wa_hid faman ka_na yarju_ liqa_ a rab bihi falya'mal amalan sa_lihaw wa la_ yusrik bi'iba_dati rab bihi ahada_
.EndTopic
;____________________________
.Topic qsMaryam  " 19. Maryam"
1.	Ka_f ha_ ya_ 'ai in sha_d
2.	Zikru rahmati rab bika 'abdahu_ zakariy ya_
3.	Iz na_da_ rab bahu_ nida_ an khafiy ya_
4.	Qa_la rab bi in ni wahanal 'azhmu min ni was ta'alar ra'su saibaw wa lam akum bidu'a_ ika rab bi saqiy ya_
5.	Wa in ni khiftul mawa_liya miw wara_i wa ka_natim ra ati 'a_qiran fahab li mil ladunka waliy ya_
6.	Yaritsuni wayaritsu min a_li ya'ku_b waj'alhu rab bi radhiy ya_
7.	Ya_ zakariy ya_ in na_ nubas siruka bighula_minis muhu_ yahya_ lam naj'al lahu_ min qablu samiy ya_
8.	Qa_la rab bi an na_ yaku_nu li ghula_muw wa ka_natim ra ati 'a_qiraw wa qad balaghtu minal kibari 'itiy ya_
9.	Qa_la kadza_lik qa_la rab buka huwa 'alay ya hay yinuw wa qad khalaqtuka min qablu wa lam taku sai a_
10.	Qa_la rab bij'al li a_yah qa_la a_yatuka al la_ tukal liman na_sa tsala_tsa laya_lin sawiy ya_
11.	Fakhraja 'ala_ qaumihi minal mihra_bi fa auha_ ilaihim an sab bihu_ bukrataw wa asyiy ya_
12.	Ya_ yahya_ khudzil kita_ba biquw wah wa a_taina_hul hukma sabiy ya_
13.	Wa hana_nam mil ladun na_ wa zaka_h wa ka_na taqiy ya_
14.	Wa bar ran biwa_lidaihi wa lam yakun jab bara_n ashiy ya_
15.	Wa sala_mun 'alaihi yauma wulida wa yauma yamu_tu wa yauma yub'atsu hay ya_
16.	Wadz kur fil kita_bi maryam idzin tabadzat min ahliha_ maka_nan syarqiy ya_
17.	Fat takhadzat min du_nihim hija_ba_ fa arsalna_ ilaiha_ ru_hana_fatamats sala laha_ basyaran sawiy ya_
18.	Qa_lat in ni a'u_dzu bir rahma_ni minka in kunta taqiy ya_
19.	Qa_la in nama_ ana rasu_lu rab bik li ahaba laki ghula_man zakiy ya_
20.	Qa_lat an na_ yaku_nu li ghula_muw wa lam yamsasni basyaruw wa lam aku baghiy ya_
21.	Qa_la kadza_lik qa_la rab buki huwa alay ya hay yin wa linaj'alahu_ a_ya_tal lin na_si wa rahmatam min na_ wa ka_na amram maqdhiy ya_
22.	Fahamalat hu fan tabadzat bihi maka_nan qashiy ya_
23.	Fa aja_ ahal makha_dhu ila_ jidz'in nakhlah qa_lat ya_ laitani mit ti qabla ha_dza_ wa kuntu nas yam mansiy ya_
24.	Fana_da_ha_ min tahtiha_ al la_ tahzani qad ja'ala rab buki tahtaki sariy ya_
25.	Wa huz zi ilaiki bijidz'in nakhlati tusa_qith alaiki ruthaban janiy ya_
26.	Fakuli was rabi wa qar ri aina_ fa im ma_ tarayin na minal basyari ahadan faqu_li in ni nadzartu lir rahma_ni shauman falan ukal limal yauma insiy ya_
27.	Fa atat bihi qaumaha_ tahmiluh qa_lu_ ya_ maryamu laqad ji'ti sai an fariy ya_
28.	Ya_ ukhta ha_ru_na ma_ ka_na abu_kim ra a sau iw wa ma_ ka_nat um muki baghiy ya_
29.	Fa asa_rat ilaihi qa_lu_ kaifa nukal limu man ka_na fil mahdi shabiy ya_
30.	Qa_la in ni abdul la_h a_ta_niyal kita_ba wa ja'a ani nabiy ya_
31.	Wa ja'alani muba_rakan aina ma_ kuntu wa ausha_ni bis sala_ti waz zaka_ti ma_ dumtu hay ya_
32.	Wa bar ram biwa_lidati wa lam yaj'alni jab ba_ran syaqiy ya_
33.	Was sala_mu 'alay ya yauma wulidtu wa yauma amu_tu wa yauma ub'atsu hay ya_
34.	Za_lika 'isab nu maryam qaulal haq qil lazi fihi yamtaru_n
35.	Ma_ ka_na lil la_hi ay yat takhidza miw waladin subha_nah idza_ qadha_ amran fa in nama_ yaqu_lu lahu_ kun fayaku_n
36.	Wa in nal la_ha rab bi wa rab bukum fa'budu_h ha_dza_ shira_thum mustaqim
37.	Fakh talafal ahza_bu mim bainihim fawailul lil lazina kafaru_ mim mashadi yaumin 'azhim
38.	Asmi'bihim wa abshir yauma ya'tu_nana_ la_kiniz zha_limu_nal yauma fi dhala_lim mubin
39.	Wa andzirhum yaumal hasrati idz qudhiyal amr wa hum fi ghaflatiw wahum la_ yu'minu_n
40.	In na_ nahnu naritsul ardha wa man alaiha_ wa ilaina_ yurja'u_n
41.	Wadz kur fil kita_bi ibra_him in nahu_ ka_na shid diqan nabiy ya_
42.	Idz qa_la li abihi ya_ abati lima ta'budu ma_ la_ yasma'u wa la_ yubshiru wa la_ yughni 'anka sai a_
43.	Ya_ abati in ni qad ja_ ani minal 'ilmi ma_ lam ya'tika fat tabi'ni ahdika shira_than sawiy ya_
44.	Ya_ abati la_ ta'budis saitha_n inas saitha_na ka_na lir rahma_ni ashiy ya_
45.	Ya_ abati in ni akha_fu ay yamas saka adza_bum minar rahma_ni fataku_na lis saitha_ni waliy ya_
46.	Qa_la ara_ghibun anta an a_lihati ya_ ibra_him la il lam tantahi la arjuman naka wah jurni maliy ya_
47.	Qa_la sala_mun 'alaika sa astaghfiru laka rab bi in nahu_ ka_na hafiy ya_
48.	Wa a'tazilukum wa ma_ tad'u_na min du_nil la_hi wa ad'u_ rab bi asa_ al la_ aku_na bidu'a_i rab bi syaqiy ya_
49.	Falam ma tazalahum wa ma_ ya'budu_na min du_nil la_hi wahabna_ lahu_ is ha_qa wa ya'qu_b wa kul lan ja'alna_ nabiy ya_
50.	Wa wahabna_ lahum mir rahmatina_ wa ja'alna_ lahum lisa_na shidqin 'aliy ya_
51.	Wadz kur fil kita_bi musa_ in nahu_ ka_na mukhlashaw wa ka_na rasu_lan nabiy ya_
52.	Wa na_daina_hu min ja_nibit thu_ril aimani wa qar rabna_hu najiy ya_
53.	Wa wahabna_ lahu_ mir rahmatina_ akha_hu ha_ru_na nabiy ya_
54.	Wadz kur fil kita_bi isma_'ila in nahu_ ka_na sha_diqal wa'di wa ka_na rasu_lan nabiy ya_
55.	Wa ka_na ya'muru ahlahu_ bis shala_ti waz zaka_h wa ka_na inda rab bihi mardhiy ya_
56.	Wadz kur fil kita_bi idris in nahu_ ka_na shid diqan nabiy ya_
57.	Wa rafa'na_hu maka_nan 'aliy ya_
58.	Ula_ ikal lazina an'amal la_hu 'alaihim minan nabiy yina min dzur riy yati a_dam wa mim man hamalna_ ma'a nu_hiw wa min dzur riy yati ibra_hima wa isra_ ila wa mim man hadaina_ waj tabaina_ idza_ tutla_ 'alaihim a_ya_tur rahma_ni khar ru_ suj jadaw wa bukiy ya_
59.	Fakhalafa mim ba'dihim khulfun adha_'us sala_ta wat taba'us sahawa_ti fasaufa yalqauna ghay ya_
60.	Il la_ man ta_ba wa a_mana wa 'amila sha_lihan fa ula_ ika yadkhulu_nal jannata wa la_ yuzhlamu_na sai a_
61.	Jan na_ti adninil lati wa'adar rahma_nu iba_dahu_ bil ghaib in nahu_ ka_na wa'duhu_ ma'tiy ya_
62.	La_ yasma'u_na fiha_ laghwan il la_ sala_ma_ wa lahum rizquhum fiha_ bukrataw wa asyiy ya_
63.	Tilkal jan natul lati nu_ritsu min 'iba_dina_ man ka_na taqiy ya_
64.	Wa ma_ natanaz zalu il la_ bi amri rab bika lahu_ ma_ baina aidina_ wama_ khalfana_ wa ma_ baina dza_lik wa ma_ ka_na rab buka nasiy ya_
65.	Rab bus sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa ma_ bainahuma_ fa'bud hu wash thabir li'iba_datih hal ta'lamu lahu_ samiy ya_
66.	Wa yaqu_lul insa_nu a idza_ ma_ mittu lasaufa ukhraju hay ya_
67.	Awa la_ yadzkurul insa_nu an na khalaqna_hu min qablu wa lam yaku sai a_
68.	Fawarab bika lanahsyuran nahum wasysyaya_thina sum ma lanuhdhiran nahum haula jahan nama jitsiy ya_
69.	Sum ma lananzi'an na min kul li si'atin ay yuhum asyad du alar rahma_ni itiy ya_
70.	Sum ma lanahnu a'lamu bil lazina hum aula_ biha_ shiliy ya_
71.	Wa im minkum il la_ wa_riduha_ ka_na 'ala_ rab bika hatmam maqdhiy ya_
72.	Sum ma nunaj jil lazinat taqauw wa nadzaruzh zha_limina fiha_ jitsiy ya_
73.	Wa iza_ tutla_ 'alaihim a_ya_tuna_ bay yina_tin qa_lal lazina kafaru_ lil lazina a_manu_ ay yul fariqaini khairum maqa_maw wa ahsanu nadiy ya_
74.	Wa kam ahlakna_ qablahum min qarnin hum ahsanu atsa_tsaw wari'ya_
75.	Qul man ka_na fidh dhala_lati falyamdud lahur rahma_nu mad da_ hat ta_ idza_ ra au ma_ yu_'adu_na im mal adza_ba wa im mas sa_'ah fasaya'lamu_na man huwa syar rum maka_naw wa adh'afu junda_
76.	Wa yazidul la_hul ladzinah tadau huda_ wal ba_qiya_tush sha_liha_tu khairun 'inda rab bika tsawa_baw wa khairum marad da_
77.	Afara aital lazi kafara bi a_ya_tina_ wa qa_la la u_tayan na ma_law wawalada_
78.	Ath thala'al ghaiba amit takhadza indar rahma_ni ahda_
79.	Kal la_ sanaktubu ma_ yaqu_lu wa namud du lahu_ minal adza_bi mad da_
80.	Wa naritsuhu_ ma_ yaqu_lu wa ya'tina farda_
81.	Wat takhadzu_ min du_nil la_hi a_lihatal liyaku_nu_ lahum iz za_
82.	Kal la_ sayakfuru_na bi'iba_datihim wa yaku_nu_na 'alaihim dhid da_
83.	Alam tara an na_ arsalna_sy syaya_thina 'alal ka_firina ta'uz zuhum azza_
84.	Fala_ ta'jal alaihim in nama_ na'uddu lahum ad da_
85.	Yauma nahsyurul mut taqina ilar rahma_ni wafda_
86.	Wa nasu_qul mujrimina ila_ jahan nama wirda_
87.	La_ yamliku_nas syafa_'ata il la manit takhadza indar rahma_ni ahda_
88.	Wa qa_lut takhadzar rahma_nu walada_
89.	Laqad ji'tum sai an id da_
90.	Taka_dus sama_wa_tu yatafath tharna minhu wa tansyaq qul ardhu wa takhir rul jiba_lu had da_
91.	An da'au lir rahma_ni walada_
92.	Wa ma_ yan baghi lir rahma_ni ay yat takhidza walada_
93.	In kul lu man fis sama_wa_ti wal ardhi il la_ a_tir rahma_ni 'abda_
94.	Laqad ahsha_hum wa ad dahum ad da_
95.	Wa kul luhum a_tihi yaumal qiya_mati farda_
96.	In nal lazina a_manu_ wa 'amilus sha_liha_ti sayaj'alu lahumur rahma_nu wud da_
97.	Fa in nama_ yas sarna_hu bilisa_nika litubasy syira bihil mut taqina wa tundzira bihi qaumal lud da_
98.	Wa kam ahlakna_ qablahum min qarn hal tuhis su minhum min ahadin autasma'u lahum rikza_
.EndTopic

.Topic qsThaha " 20. Thaha"
1.	Tha_ ha_
2.	Ma_ anzalna_ alaikal qur a_na litasyqa_
3.	Illa tadz kiratal limay yakhsya_
4.	Tanzilam mim man khalaqal ardha was sama_wa_ti 'ula_
5.	Ar rahma_nu 'alal arsyis tawa_
6.	Lahu_ ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ardi wa ma_ bainahuma_ wa ma_ tahtats tsara_
7.	Wa in tajhar bil qauli fa in nahu_ ya'lamus sir ra wa akhfa_
8.	Al la_hu la_ ila_ha il la_ huwa lahul asma_ ul husna_
9.	Wa hal ata_ka haditsu mu_sa_
10.	Idz ra a_ na_ran faqa_la li ahlihim kutsu_ in ni a_nastu na_ral la'al li a_tikum minha_ biqabasin au ajidu 'alan na_ri huda_
11.	Falam ma_ ata_ha_ nu_diya ya_ mu_sa_
12.	In ni ana rab buka fakh la na'laik in naka bil wa_dil muqad dasi thuwa_
13.	Wa anakh tartuka fastami lima_ yu_ha_
14.	In nani anal la_hu la_ ila_ha il la_ ana fa'budni wa aqimish shala_ta lidzikri
15.	In nas sa_'ata a_tiyatun aka_dun ukhfiha_ litujza_ nafsim bima_ tas'a_
16.	Fala_ yashud dan naka 'anha mal la_ yu.minu biha_ wat taba'a hawa_hu fatarda_
17.	Wa ma_ tilka biyaminika ya_ mu_sa_
18.	Qa_la hiya asha_y atawak ka u 'alaiha_ wa ahus syu biha_ 'ala_ ghanami waliya fiha_ ma a_ribu ukhra_
19.	Qa_la alqiha_ ya_ mu_sa_
20.	Fa alqa_ha_ fa idza_ hiya hay yatun tas'a_
21.	Qa_la khudz ha_ wa la_ takhal sanu'iduha_ siratahal u_la_
22.	Wadh mum yadaka ila_ jana_hika takhruj baidha_'a min ghairi su_ in a_yatan ukhra_
23.	Linuriyakamin a_ya_tinal kubra_
24.	Idzhab ila_ fir'auna in nahu_ thagha_
25.	Qa_la rab bis rah li shadri
26.	Wa yas sir li amri
27.	Wah lul uqdatam mil lisa_ni
28.	Yafqahu_ qauli
29.	Waj'al li waziram min ahli
30.	Ha_ru_na akhi
31.	Usydud bihi azri
32.	Wa asyrik hu fi amri
33.	Kai nusab bihaka katsira_
34.	Wa nadzkuraka katsira_
35.	In naka kunta bina_ bashira_
36.	Qa_la qad u_tita su'laka ya_ mu_sa_
37.	Wa laqad manan na_ 'alaika mar ratan ukhra_
38.	Idz auhaina_ ila_ um mika ma_ yu_ha_
39.	Aniq dzifihi fit ta_bu_ti faqdzi fihi fil yam mi falyulqihil yam mu bis sa_hili ya'khudzhu aduw wul li wa aduwwul lah wa alqaitu alaika mahab batam min ni walitushna'a ala_ aini
40.	Idz tamsyi ukhtuka fataqu_lu hal adul lukum 'ala_ may yakfuluh faraja'na_ka ila_ um mika kaitaqar ra ainuha_ wa la_ tahzan wa qatalta nafsan fanaj jaina_ka minal gham mi wafatan na_ka futu_na_ falabitsta sinina fi ahli mad yana sum ma ji'ta 'ala_ qadariy ya_ mu_sa_
41.	Wash thana'tuka linafsi
42.	Idzhab anta wa akhu_ka bi a_ya_ti wa la_ taniya_ fi dzikri
43.	idzhaba_ ila_ fir'auna in nahu_ thagha_
44.	Faqu_la_ lahu_ qaulal lay yinal la'al lahu_ yatadzak karu au yakhsya_
45.	Qa_la rab bana_ in nana_ nakha_fu ay yafrutha alaina_ au ay yathgha_
46.	Qa_la la_ takha_fa_ in nani ma'akuma_ asma'u wa ara_
47.	Fa'tiya_hu faqu_la_ in na_ rasu_la_ rab bika fa arsil ma'ana_ bani isra_ ila wa la_ tu'adz dzibhum qad ji'na_ka bi a_yatim mir rab bik was sala_mu 'ala_ manit taba'al huda_
48.	In na_ qad u_hiya ilaina_ an nal adza_ba 'ala_ man kadz dzaba wa tawal la_
49.	Qa_la famar rab bukuma_ ya_ mu_sa_
50.	Qa_la rab bunal ladzi a'tha_ kul la sai in khalqahu_ sum ma bada_
51.	Qa_la fama_ ba_lul quru_nil u_la_
52.	Qa_la ilmuha_ 'inda rab bi fi kita_b la_ yadhil lu rab bi wa la_ yansa_
53.	Al ladzi ja'ala lakumul ardha mahdaw wa salaka lakum fiha_ subulaw wa anzala minas sama_i ma_ fa akhrajna_ bihi azwa_jam min naba_tin syat ta_
54.	Kulu_ war'au an'a_makum in na fi dza_lika la a_ya_til li ulin nuha_
55.	Minha_ khalaqna_kum wa fiha_ nu'idukum wa minha_ nukhrijukum ta_ratan ukhra_
56.	Wa laqad araina_hu a_ya_tina_ kullaha_ fakadz dzaba wa aba_
57.	Qa_la aji'tana_ litukhrijana_ min ardhina_ bisihrika ya_ mu_sa_
58.	Falana'tiyan naka bisihrim mitslihi faj'al bainana_ wa bainaka mau'idal la_ nukhlifuhu_ nahnu wa la_ anta maka_nan suwa_
59.	Qa_la mau'idukum yaumuz zinati wa ay yuhsyaran na_su dhuha_
60.	Fatawal la_ fir'aunu fajama'a kaidahu_ sum ma ata_
61.	Qa_la lahum mu_sa_ wailakum la_ taftaru_ 'alal la_hi kadziban fayus hitakum bi'adza_b wa qad kha_ba manif tara_
62.	Fatana_za'u_ amrahum bainahum wa asar run najwa_
63.	Qa_lu_ in ha_dza_ni lasa_hira_ni yurida_ni ay yukhrija_kum min ardhikum bisihrihima_ wa yadz haba_ bi thariqatikumul mutsla_
64.	Fa ajmi'u_ kaidakum sum ma tu_shaf fa_ wa qad aflahal yauma manis ta'la_
65.	Qa_lu_ ya_ mu_sa_  im ma_ an tulqiya wa im ma_ an naku_na aw wala man alqa_
66.	Qa_la bal alqu_ fa idza_ hiba_luhum wa ishiy yuhum yukhay yalu ilaihi min sihrihim an naha_ tas'a_
67.	Fa aujasa fi nafsihi khifatam mu_sa_
68.	Qulna_ la_ takhaf in naka antal a'la_
69.	Wa alqi ma_ fi yaminika talqaf ma_ shana'u_ in nama_ shana'u_ kaidu_sa_hir wa la_ yuflihus sa_hiru haitsu ata_
70.	Fa ulqiyas saharatu suj jadan qa_lu_ a_man na_ birab bi ha_ru_na wa mu_sa_
71.	Qa_la a_mantum lahu_ qabla an a_dzana lakum in nahu_ lakabirukumul ladzi 'al lamakumus sihr fala uqath thi'an na aidiyakum wa arjulakum min khila_fiw wa la ushal liban nakum fi judzu_ in nakhli wa lata'lamun na ay yuna_ asyad du 'adza_baw wa abqa_
72.	Qa_lu_ lan nutsiraka 'ala_ ma_ ja_'ana_ minal bay yina_ti wal ladzi fatharana_ faqdhi ma_ anta qa_dh innama_ taqdhi ha_dzihil haya_tad dunya_
73.	In na_ a_man na_ birab bina_ liyaghfira lana_ khatha_ya_na_ wa ma_ akrahtana_ 'alaihi minas sihr wal la_hu khairuw wa abqa_
74.	In nahu_ may ya'ti rab bahu_ mujriman fa in na lahu_ jahan nam la_ yamu_tu fiha_ wa la_ yahya_
75.	Wa may ya'tihi mu'minan qad 'amilash sha_liha_ti fa ula_ ika lahumud daraja_tul 'ula_
76.	Jan na_tu 'adnin tajri min tahtihal anha_ru kha_lidina fiha_ wa dza_lika jaza_ u man tazak ka_
77.	Wa laqad aihaina_ ila_ mu_sa_ an asri bi'iba_di fadhrib lahum thariqan filbahri yabasal la_ takha_fu darakaw wa la_ takhsya_
78.	Fa atba'ahum fir'aunu bijunu_dihi faghasyiyahum minal yam mi ma_ ghasyiyahum
79.	Wa adhal la fir'aunu qaumahu_ wa ma_ hada_
80.	Ya_ bani isra_ illa qad anjaina_kum min aduw wikum wa wa_'adna_kum ja_nibath thu_ril aimana wa naz zalna_ 'alaikumul man na was salwa_
81.	Kulu_ min thay yiba_ti ma_ razaqna_kum wa la_ tathghau fihi fayahil la 'alaikum ghadhabi wa may yahlil 'alaihi ghadhabi faqad hawa_
82.	Wa in ni laghaf fa_rul liman ta_ba wa a_mana wa 'amila sha_lihan sum mahtada_
83.	Wa ma_ a'jalaka an qaumika ya_ mu_sa_
84.	Qa_la hum ula_i 'ala_ atsari wa 'ajiltu ilaika rab bi litardha_
85.	Qa_la fa in na_ qad fatan na_ qaumaka min ba'dika wa adhal lahumus sa_miriy
86.	Faraja'a mu_sa_ ila_ qaumihi ghadhba_na asifa_ qa_la ya_ qaumi alam ya'idkum rab bukum wa'dan hasana_ afatha_la 'alaikumul ahdu am aradtum ay yahil la 'alaikum ghadhabum mir rab bikum fa akhlaftum mau'idi
87.	Qa_lu_ ma_ akhlafna_ mau'idaka bimalkina_ wa la_kin na_ hum milna_ auza_ram min zinatil qaumi faqadzaf na_ha_ fakadza_lika alqas sa_miriy
88.	Fa akhraja lahum ijlan jasadal lahu_ khuwa_run faqa_lu_ ha_dza_ ila_hukum wa ila_hu mu_sa_ fanasiya
89.	Afala_ yarauna al la_ yarji'u ilaihim qaulaw wa la_ yamliku lahum dharraw wa la_ naf'a_
90.	Wa laqad qa_la lahum ha_ru_nu min qablu ya_ qaumi in nama_ futintum bih wa in na rab bakumur rahma_nu fat tabi'u_ni wa athi'u_ amri
91.	Qa_lu_ lan nabraha 'alaihi 'a_kifina hat ta_ yarji'a ilaina_ mu_sa_
92.	Qa_la ya_ ha_ru_nu ma_ mana'aka idz ra aitahum dhal lu_
93.	Al la_ tat tabi'an afa'ashaita amri
94.	Qa_la yabna um ma la_ ta'khudz bilihyati wa la_ bira'si in ni khasyitu an taqu_la far raqta baina bani isra_ ila wa lam tarqub qauli
95.	Qa_la fama_ khatbuka ya_sa_miriy
96.	Qa_la bashurtu bima_ lam yabshuru_ bihi faqabadhtu qabdhatam min atsarir rasu_li fanabadz tuha_ wa kadza_lika saw walat li nafsi
97.	Qa_la fadz hab fa in na laka fil haya_ti an taqu_la la_ misa_sa wa in na laka mau'idal lan tukhlafah wanzhur ila_ ila_hikal ladzi zhalta 'alaihi a_kifa_ lanuhar riqan nahu_ sum ma lanansifan nahu_ fil yam mi nasfa_
98.	In nama_ ila_hukumul la_hul ladzi la_ ila_ha il la_ hu_ wasi'a kul la sai in 'ilma_
99.	Kadza_lika naqush shu 'alaika min amba_i ma_ qad sabaq wa qad a_taina_ka mil ladun na_ zikra_
100.	Man a'radha 'anhu fa in nahu_ yahmilu yaumal qiya_mati wizra_
101.	Kha_lidina fih wa sa_ a lahum yaumal qiya_mati himla_
102.	Yauma yunfakhu fis su_ri wa nahsyurul mujrimina yauma idzin zurqa_
103.	Yatakha_fatu_na bainahum il labitstum il la_ asyra_
104.	Nahnu a'lamu bima_ yaqu_lu_na idz yaqu_lu amtsaluhum thariqatan il labitstum il la_ yauma_
105.	Wa yas alu_naka 'anil jiba_li faqul yansifuha_ rab bi nasfa_
106.	Fayadzaruha_ qa_'an shafshafa_
107.	La_ tara_ fiha_ iwajaw wa la_ amta_
108.	Yauma idziy yat tabi'u_nad da_'iya la_ iwaja lah wa khasya'atil ashwa_tu lir rahma_ni fala_ tasma'u il la_ hamsa_
109.	Yauma idzil la_ tanfa'usy syafa_'atu il la_ man adzina lahur rahma_nu wa radhiya lahu_ qaula_
110.	Ya'lamu ma_ baina aidihim wa ma_ khalfahum wa la_ yuhithu_na bihi 'ilma_
111.	Wa'anatil wuju_hu lilhay yil qay yu_m wa qad kha_ba hamala zhulma_
112.	Wa may ya'mal minas sha_liha_ti wa huwa mu'minun fala_ yakha_fu zhulmaw wa la_ hadhma_
113.	Wa kadza_lika anzalna_hu qur a_nan arabiy yaw wa shar rafna_ fihi minal wa'idi la'al lahum yat taqu_na au yuhditsu lahum zikra_
114.	Fata'a_lal la_hul malikul haq wa la_ taj'al bil qur a_ni min qabli ay yuqdha_ ilaika wahyuhu_ wa qur rab bi zidni 'ilma_
115.	Wa laqad 'ahidna_ ila_ a_dama min qablu fanasiya wa lam najid lahu_ azma_
116.	Wa idz qulna_ lilmala_ ikatis judu_ li a_dama fasajadu_ il la_ iblis aba_
117.	Faqulna_ ya_ a_damu in na_ ha_dza_ aduw wul laka wa lizaujika fala_ yukhrijan nakuma_ minal jan nati fatasqa_
118.	In na laka al la_ taju_'a fiha_ wa la_ ta'ra_
119.	Wa an naka la_ tazhma u fiha_ wa la_ tadha_
120.	Fawaswasa ilaihis syaitha_nu qa_la ya_ a_damu hal adul luka 'ala_ syajaratil khuldi wa mulkil la_ yabla_
121.	Fa akala_ minha_ fabadat lahuma_ sau a_tuhuma_ wa thafiqa_ yakhshifa_ni 'alaihima_ miw waraqil jan nati wa 'asha_ a_damu rab bahu_ faghawa_
122.	Sum maj taba_hu rab buhu_ fata_ba 'alaihi wa hada_
123.	Qa_lah bitha_ minha_ jami'an ba'dhukum liba'dhin 'aduw fa im ma_ ya'tiyan nakum min ni hudan famanit taba'a huda_ya fala_ yadhil lu wa la_ yasqa_
124.	Wa man a'rada 'an dzikri fa in na lahu_ ma'isyatan dhankaw wa nahsyuruhu_ yaumal qiya_mati a'ma_
125.	Qa_la rab bi lima hasyartani a'ma_ wa qad kuntu bashira_
126.	Qa_la kadza_lika atatka a_ya_tuna_ fanasitaha_ wa kadza_likal yauma tunsa_
127.	Wa kadza_lika najzi man asrafa wa lam yu'mim bi a_ya_ti rab bih wa la'adza_bul a_khirati asyad du wa abqa_
128.	Afalam yahdi lahum kam ahlakna_ qablahum minal quru_ni yamsyu_na fi masa_kinihim in na fi dza_lika la a_ya_til li ulin nuha_
129.	Wa laula_ kalimatun sabaqat mir rab bika laka-na li za_maw wa ajalum musam ma_
130.	Fashbir 'ala_ ma_ yaqu_lu_na wa sab bih bihamdi rab bika qabla thulu_'is samsi wa qabla ghuru_biha_ wa min a_na_ il laili fasab bih wa athra_fannaha_ri la'al laka tardha_
131.	Wa la_ tamud dan na 'ainaika ila_ ma_ mat ta'na_ bihi azwa_jam minhum zahratal haya_tid dun ya_ linaftinahum fih wa rizqu rab bika khairuw wa abqa_
132.	Wa'mur ahlaka bis sa la_ti was thabir 'alaiha_ la_ nas aluka rizqa_ nahnu narzuquk wal 'a_qibatu lit taqwa_
133.	Wa qa_lu_ laula_ ya'tina_ bi a_yatin mir rab bih awalam ta'ti him bay yinatu ma_ fis shuhufil u_la_
134.	 Wa lau an na- ahlakna_hum bi'adza_ bim min qablihi laqa_lu_ rab bana_ laula_ arsalta ilaina_ rasu_lan fanattabi'a a_ya_tika min qabli an nadzil la wa nakhza_
135.	Qul kul lum mutarab bishun fatarab bashu_ fasata'lamu_na man ashsha_bush shira_this sawiy yi wa manih tada_
.EndTopic
;_________________________________	
.Topic qsAl-Anbia_   " 21. Al Anbia_"
1.	Iqtaraba lin na_si hisa_buhum wa hum fi gaflatim muridu_n
2.	Ma_ yatihim min zikrim mir rab bihim muhdasin il las tamau_hu wa hum yalabu_n
3.	La_hiyatan qulu_buhum wa asar run najwal lazina zalamu_ hal ha_za_ il la_ basarum afatatu_nas sihra wa antum tubsiru_n
4.	Qa_la rab bi yalamul qaula fis sama_i wal ard wa huwas samiul alim
5.	Bal qa_lu_ adga_su ahla_ mim balit tara_hu bal huwa sa_iru falya tina_ bi a_ya_tin kama_ ursilal aw walu_n
6.	Ma_ a_mant qablahum min qaryatin ahlakna_ha_ afahum yuminu_n
7.	Wa ma_ arsalna_ qablaka il la_ rija_lan nu_hi ilaihim fas alu_ ahlaz zikri in kuntum la_ talamu_n
8.	Wa ma_ ja'alna_hum jasadal la_ yakulu_nat taa_ma wa ma_ ka_nu_ ha_lidin
9.	Sum ma sadaqna_humul wada faanjaina_hum wa man nasa_u wa ahlaknal musrifin
10.	Laqad anzalna_ ilaikum kita_ban fihi zikrukum afala_ taqilu_n
11.	Wa kam qasamna_ min qaryatin ka_nat za_limataw wa ansana_ badaha_ qauman a_harin
12.	Falam ma_ ahas su_ basana_ iza_ hum minha_ yarkudu_n 
13.	La_ tarkudu_ war ji u_ ila_ ma_ utriftum fihi wa masa_kinikum la'al lakum tus alu_n
14.	Qa_lu_ ya_ wailana_ in na_ kun na_ za_limin
15.	Fama_ za_lat tilka dawa_hum hat ta_ ja'alna_hum hasidan ha_midin
16.	Wa ma_ halaqnas sama_a wal arda wa ma_ bainahuma_ la_ibin
17.	Lau aradna_ an nat tahiza lahwal lat tahazna_hu mil ladun na_ in kun na_ fa_ilin
18.	Bal naqzifu bil haq qi alal ba_tili fayadmauhu_ fa iza_ huwa za_hiq wa lakumul wailu mim ma_ tasifu_n
19.	Wa la_hu_ manfis sama_wa_ti wal ard waman indahu_ la_ yastakbiru_na an iba_datihi wala_ yastahsiru_n
20.	Yusab bihu_nal laila wan naha_ra la_ yafturu_n
21.	Amit tahazu_ a_lihatam minal ardi hum yunsiru_n
22.	Lau ka_na fihima_a_lihatun il lal la_hu lafasadata_ fasubha_nal la_hi rab bil arsi am ma_ yasifu_n
23.	La_ yus alu am ma_ yafalu wa hum yus alu_n
24.	Amit tahazu_ min du_nihi a_lihah qul ha_tu_ burha_nakum ha_za_ zikru mam maiya wa zikru man qahli bal aksaruhum la_ yalamu_nal haqa fahum muridu_n
25.	Wa ma_ arsalna_ min qablika mir rasu_lin il la_ nu_hi ilaihi an nahu_ la_ ila_ha il la_ ana fabudu_n
26.	Wa qa_lu tahazar rahma_nu waladan subha_nah bal iba_dum mukramu_n
27.	La_ yasbiqu_nahu_ bil qauli wa hum bi amrihi yamalu_n
28.	Yalamu ma_ baina aidihim wa ma_ halfahum wa la_ yasfau_na il la_ limanir tada_ wa hum min hasyatihi musfiqu_n
29.	Wa may yaqul minhum in ni ila_hum min du_nihi faza_lika najzihi jahan nam kaza_lika najziz za_limin
30.	Awalam yaral lazina kafaru_ an nas sama_wa_ti wal arda ka_nata_ ratqan fafataqna_huma_ wa ja'alna_ minal ma_i kul la sai in hay afala_ yuminu_n
31.	Wa ja'alna_ fil ardi rawa_siya an tamida bihim wa ja'alna_ fiha_ fija_jan subulal la'al lahum yahtadu_n
32.	Wa ja'alnas sama_a saqfam mahfu_zaw wa hum an a_ya_tiha_ muridu_n
33.	Wa huwal lazi halaqal laila wan naha_ra was samsa wal qamar kul lun fi falakiy yasbahu_n
34.	Wa ma_ ja'alna_ libasarim min qablikal huld afa im mit ta fahumul ha_lidu_n
35.	Kul lu nafsin za_ iqatul maut wa nablu_kum bis sar ri wal hairi fitnah wa ilaina_ turjau_n
36.	Wa iza_ ra a_kal lazina kafaru_ iy yat tahizu_naka il la_ huzu wa_ aha_zal lazi yazkuru a_lihatakum wa hum bizikrir rahma_ni hum ka_firu_n
37.	Huliqal insa_nu min ajal sa urikum a_ya_ti fala_ tastajilu_n
38.	Wa yaqu_lu_na mata_ ha_zal wadu in kuntum sa_diqin
39.	Lau yalamul lazina kafaru_ hina la_ yakuf fu_na aw wuju_hihimun na_ra wa la_ an zuhu_rihim wa la_ hum yunsaru_n
40.	Bal tatihim bagtatan fatabhatuhum fala_ yastatiu_na rad daha_ wa la_hum yunzaru_n
41.	Wa laqadis tuhzi a birusulim min qablika faba_qa bil lazina sahiru_ minhum ma_ ka_nu_ bihi yastahzi u_n
42.	Qul may yakla ukum bil laili wan naha_ri minar rahma_n bal hum an zikri rab bihim muridu_n
43.	Am lahum a_lihatun tamnauhum min du_nina_ la_ yastatiu_na nasra anfusihim wa la_ hum min na_ yushabu_n
44.	Bal mat tana_ ha_ ula_i wa a_ba_ ahum hat ta_ ta_la alaihimul umur afala_ yarauna an na_ natil arda nanqusuha_ min atra_fiha_ afahumul ga_libu_n
45.	Qul in nama_ unzirukum bil wahyi wa la_ yasmaus sum mud dua_ a iza_ ma_ yunzaru_n
46.	Wa la im mas sat hum nafhatum min aza_bi rab bika layaqu_lun na ya_ wailana_ in na_ kun na_ za_limin
47.	Wa nadaul mawa_zinal qista liyaumil qiya_mati fala_ tuzlamu nafsun sai an wa in ka_na misqa_la hab batim min hardalin ataina_ biha_ wa kafa_ bina_ ha_sibin
48.	Wa laqad a_taina_ mu_sa_ wa ha_ru_nal furqa_na wa diya_ aw wa zikral lilmut taqin
49.	Al lazina yahsauna rab bahum bil gaibi wa hum minas sa_ati musfiqu_n
50.	Wa ha_za_ zikrum muba_rakun anzalna_h afa antum lahu_ munkiru_n
51.	Wa laqad a_taina_ ibra_hima rusdahu_ min qablu wa kun na_ bihi a_limin
52.	Iz qa_la li abihi wa qaumihi ma_ ha_zihit tama_silul lati antum laha_ a_kifu_n
53.	Qa_lu_ wajadna_ a_ba_ ana laha_ a_bidin
54.	Qa_la laqad kuntum antum wa a_ba_ ukum fi dala_lim mubin
55.	Qa_lu_ ajitana_ bil haq qi am anta minal la_ibin
56.	Qa_la bar rab bukum rab bus sama_wa_ti wal ardil lazi fatarahun na wa ama ala_ za_likum minas sa_hidin
57.	Wa tal la_hi la akidan na asna_makum bada an tuwal lu_ mudbirin
58.	Faja'alahum juza_zan il la_ kabiral lahum la'al lahum ilaihi yarjiu_n
59.	Qa_lu_ man fa'ala ha_za_a bi a_lihatina_ in nahu_ laminaz za_limin
60.	Qa_lu_ samina fatay yazkuru hum yuqa_lu lahu_ ibra_him
61.	Qa_lu_ fatu_ bihi ala_ ayunin na_si la'al lahum yashadu_n
62.	Qa_lu_ a anta fa'alta ha_za_ bi a_lihatina_ ya_ ibra_him
63.	Qa_la bal fa'alahu_ kabiruhum ha_za_ fas aluhum in ka_nu_ yantiqu_n
64.	Farajau_ ila_ anfusihim faqa_lu_ inakum antumuz za_limu_n
65.	Sum ma nukisu_ ala ru u_sihim laqad alimta ma_ ha_ ula_i yantiqu_n
66.	Qa_la afatabudu_na min du_nil la_hi ma_ la_ yanfaukum sai aw wa la_ yadur rukum
67.	Uf fil lakum wa lima_ tabudu_na min du_nil la_h afala_ taqilu_n
68.	Qa_lu_ har riqu_hu wan suru_ a_lihatakum in kuntum fa_ilin
69.	Qulna_ ya_ na_ru ku_ni bardaw wa sala_man ala_ ibra_him
70.	Wa ara_du bihi kaidan faja'alna_ humul ahsarin
71.	Wa naj jaina_hu wa lu_tan ilal ardil lati ba_rakna_ fiha_ lila_lamin
72.	Wa wahabna_ lahu_ is ha_q wa yaqu_ba na_filah wa kul lan ja'alna_ sa_lihin
73.	Wa ja'alna_hum a im matay yahdu_na bi amrina_ wa auhaina_ ilaihim filal haira_ti wa iqa_mas sala_ti wa ita_ az zaka_h wa ka_nu_ lana_ a_bidin
74.	Wa lu_tan a_taina_hu hukmaw wa ilmaw wa naj jaina_hu minal qaryatil lati ka_nat tamalul haba_ is in nahum ka_nu_ qauma sau in fa_siqin
75.	Wa adhalna_hu fi rahmatina_ in nahu_ minas sa_lihin
76.	Wa nu_han iz na_da_ min qablu fas tajabna_ lahu_ fanaj jaina_hu wa ah lahu_ minal karbil azim
77.	Wa nasarna_hu minal qaumil lazina kaz zabu_ bi a_ya_tina_ in nahum ka_nu_ qauma sau in fa agraqna_hum ajmain
78.	Wa da_wu_da wa sulaima_na iz yahkuma_ni fil harsi iz nafasat fihi ganamul qaum wa kun na_ lihukmihim sa_hidin
79.	Fatah hamna_ha_ sulaima_n wa kul lan a_taina_ hukmaw wa ilmaw wasah harna_ ma'a da_wu_dal hiba_la yusab bihna wat tair wa kuna_ fa_ilin
80.	Wa al lamna_hu sanata labu_sil lakum lituhsinakum min basikum fahal antum sa_kiru_n
81.	Wa lisulaima_nar riha a_sifatan tajri bi amrihi ilal ardhil lati ba_rakna_ fiha_ wa kun na_ bikul li sai in a_li min
82.	Wa minas saya_tini may yaghu_shu_na lahu_ wa ya'malu_na amalan du_na za_lik wa kun na_ lahum ha_fizin
83.	Wa ay yu_ba iz na_da_ rab bahu_ an ni mas saniyad dur ru wa anta arhamur ra_himin
84.	Fas tajabna_ lahu_ fakasyafna_ ma_ bihi min dur riw wa a_taina_hu ah lahu_ wa mitslahum ma'ahum rahmatam min 'indina_ wa zikra_ lil a_bidin
85.	Wa isma_ila wa idrisa wa zal kifl kul lum minas sa_birin
86.	Wa adkhalna_hum fi rahmatina_ in nahum minas sa_lihin
87.	Wa zan nu_ni iz zahaba mugha_dhiban fazhan na al lan naqdira alaihi fana_da_ fiz zuluma_ti al la_ ila_ha il la_ anta subha_naka in ni kuntu minaz za_limin
88.	Fas tajabna_ lahu_ wa naj jaina_hu minal gham wa kaza_lika nunjil mu'minin
89.	Wa zakariy ya_ iz na_da_ rab bahu_ rab bi la_ tadzarni fardaw wa anta hairul wa_risin
90.	Fas tajabna_ lah wa wahabna_ lahu_ yahya_ wa aslahna_ lahu_ zaujah in nahum ka_nu_ yusa_riu_na fil haira_ti wa yadu_nana_ raghabaw wa rahaba_ wa ka_nu_ lana_ ha_si'in
91.	Wal lati ahsanat farjaha_ fanafakna_ fiha_ mir ru_hina_ wa ja'alna_ha_ wab naha_ a_yatal lil'a_lamin
92.	In na ha_zihi um matukum um mataw wa_hidataw wa ana rab bukum fa'budu_n
93.	Wa taqat ta'u_ amrahum bainahum kul lun ilaina_ ra_ji'u_n
94.	Famay ya'mal minas sa_liha_ti wa huwa mu'minun fala_ kufra_na lisa'yih wa in na_ lahu_ ka_tibu_n
95.	Wa hara_mun 'ala_ qaryatin ahlakna_ha_ an nahum la_ yarji'u_n
96.	Hat ta_ iza_ futihat ya'ju_ju wa ma ju_ju wa hum min kul li badabiy yansilu_n
97.	Waq tarabal wa'dul haq qu fa iza_ hiya sa_khishatun absa_rul lazina kafaru_ ya_wailana_ qad kun na_ fi ghaflatim min ha_za_ bal kun na_ za_limin
98.	In nakum wa ma_ ta'budu_na min du_nil la_hi hashabu jahan nam antum laha_ wa_ridu_n
99.	Lau ka_na ha_ ula_i a_lihatam ma_ waradu_ha_ wa kul lun fiha_ kha_lidu_n
100.	Lahum fiha_ zafiruw wa hum fiha_ la_ yasma'u_n
101.	In nal lazina sabaqat lahum min nal husna_ ula_ ika 'anha_ mub'adu_n
102.	La_ yasma'u_na hasisaha_ wa hum fi mas tahat anfusuhum kha_lidu_n
103.	La_ yahzunuhumul faza'ul akbaru wa tatalaq qa_humul mala_ ikah ha_za_ yaumukumul lazi kuntum tu_'adu_n
104.	Yauma nathwis sama_ a kathay yis sijil li lilkutub kama_ badana_ aw wala khalqin nu'iduh wa dan 'alaina_ in na_ kun na_ fa_'ilin
105.	Wa laqad katabna_ fiz zabu_ri mim ba'diz zikri an nal arda yaritsuha_ iba_diyas sa_lihu_n
106.	In na fi ha_za_ labala_ghal liqaumin 'a_bidin
107.	Wa ma_ arsalna_ka il la_ rahmatal lil'a_lamin
108.	Qul in nama_ yu_ha_ ilay ya an nama_ ila_hukum ila_huw wa_hid fahal antum muslimu_n
109.	Fa in tawal lau faqul a_zantukum 'ala_ sawa_ in wa in adri aqaribun am ba'idum ma_ tu_'adu_n
110.	In nahu_ ya'lamul jahra minal qauli wa ya'lamu ma_ taktumu_n
111.	Wa in adri la'al lahu_ fitnatul lakum wa mata_'un ila_ hin
112.	Qa_la rab bih kum bil haq wa rab bunar rahma_nul musta'a_nu 'ala_ ma_ tashifu_n
.EndTopic
;_________________________________
.Topic qsAl-Haj  " 22. Al Haj"
1.	Ya_ ay yuhan na_sut taqu_ rab bakum in na zal zalatas sa_'ati sai un azim
2.	Yauma taraunaha_ tadzhalu kul lu murdi'atin am ma_ arda'at wa ta da'u kul lu za_ti hamlin hamlaha_ wa taran na_sa suka_ra_ wa ma_ hum bisuka_ra_ wa la-kin na 'aza_bal la_hi sadid  
3.	Wa minan na_si may yuja_dilu fil la_hi bighairi ilmiw wa yat tabi'u kul la saita_nim marid
4.	Kutiba alaihi an nahu_ man tawal la_hu fa an nahu_ yudhil luhu_ wa yahdihi ila_ aza_bis sa'ir
5.	Ya_ ay yuhan na_su in kuntum fi raibihim minal ba'tsi fa in na_ khalaqna_kum min tura_bin sum ma min nutfatin sum ma min alaqatin sum ma min mudghatim mukhal laqatiw wa gairi mukhal laqatil linubay yina lakum wa nuqir ru fil arha_mi ma_ nasya_ u ila_ ajalim musam man sum ma nukhrijukum thiflan sum ma litablughu_ asyud dakum wa minkum may yutawaf fa_ wa minkum may yurad du ila_ arzalil umuri likaila_ ya'lama min ba'di ilmin sai a_ wa taral arda ha_midatan fa iza_ anzalna_ alaihal ma_ ah taz zat wa rabat wa ambatat min kul li zaujin bahij
6.	Za_lika bi an nal la_ha huwal haq qu wa an nahu_ yuhyil mauta_ wa an nahu_ 'ala_ kul li sai in qadir
7.	Wa an nas sa_'ata a_tiyatul la_ raiba fiha_ wa an nal la_ha yab'atsu man fil qubu_r
8.	Wa minan na_si may yuja_dilu la_hi bigairi ilmiw wa la_ hudaw wa la_ kita_bim munir
9.	Sa_niya 'ithfihi liyudhil la an sabilil la_h lahu_ fid dun ya_ khizyuw wa nudziquhu_ yaumal qiya_mati aza_bal hariq
10.	Za_lika bima_ qad damat yada_ka wa an nal la_ha laisa bizhalla_mil lil'abid
11.	Wa minan na_si may ya'budul la_ha 'ala_ harf fa in asha_bahu_ khairunit ma an na bih wa in asha_bat hu fitnatunin qalaba 'ala_ wajhih khasirad dun ya_ wal a_khirah za_lika huwal khusra_nul mubin
12.	Yad'u_ min du_nil la_hi ma_ la_ yadur ruhu_ wa ma_ la_ yanfa'uh, za_lika huwad dala_lul ba'id
13.	Yad'u_ laman dar ruhu_ aqrabu min naf'ih labi'sal maula_ wa labi'sal asir
14.	In nal la_ha yudkhilul lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti jan na_tin tajri min tahtihal anha_r in nal la_ha yaf'alu ma_ yurid
15.	Man ka_na yazhun nu al lay yanshurahul la_hu fid dun ya_ wal a_khirati fal yamdud bisababin ilas sama_i sum mal yaqta falyanzur hal yuz hiban na kaiduhu_ ma_ yaghiz
16.	Wa kaza_lika anzalna_hu a_ya_tim bay yina_tiw wa an nal la_ha yahdil may yurid
17.	In nal lazina a_manu_ wal lazina ha_du_ was sa_bi ina wan nasha_ra_ wal maju_sa wal lazina asraku_ in nal la_ha yafshilu bainahum yaumal qiya_mah in nal la_ha 'ala_ kul li sai in sahid
18.	Alam tara an nal la_ha yasjudu lahu_ man fis sama_wa_ti wa man fil ardi was samsu wal qamaru wan nuju_ mu wal jiba_lu was sajaru wad dawa_b bu wa kasirum minan na_s wa kasirun haq qa 'alaihil aza_b wa may yuhinil la_hu fama_ lahu_ mim mukrim in nal la_ha yaf'alu ma_ yasya_
19.	Ha_za_ni hasma_nikh tashamu_ fi rab bihim fal lazina kafaru_ qut ti'at lahum siya_bum mina_riy yushab bu min fauqi ru u_sihimul hamim
20.	Yusharu bihi ma_ fi buthu_nihim wal julu_d
21.	Wa lahum maqa_mi'u min hadid
22.	Kul lama_ ara_du_ ay yakhruju_ minha_ min gham min u'idu_ fiha_ wa zu_qu_ aza_bal hariq
23.	In nal la_ha yudkhilul lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti jan na_tin tajri min tahtihal anha_ru yuhal launa fiha_ min asa_wira min zahabiw wa lu lu'a_ wa liba_suhum fiha_ harir
24.	Wa hudu_ ilat tay yibi minal qaul wa hudu_ ila_ sira_til hamid
25.	In nal lazina kafaru_ wa yashudu_na an sabilil la_hi wal masjidil hara_mil lazi ja'alna_hu lin na_si sawa_ anil 'a_kifu fihi wal ba_d wa may yurid fihi bi ilha_dim bizhulmin nudziqhu min 'aza_bin alim
26.	Wa iz baw wa'na_ li ibra_hima maka_nal baiti al la_ tusrik bi sai aw wa tah hir baitiya lit ta_ ifina wal qa_ imina war ruk ka'is suju_d
27.	Wa az zin fin na_si bil haj ji ya'tu_ka rija_law wa 'ala_ kul li da_miriy ya'tina min kul li faj jin amiq
28.	Liyasnadu_ mana_fi'a lahum wayazkurus mal la_hi fi ay ya_mim ma'lu_ma_tim 'ala_ ma_ razaqahum mimbahimatil an'a_mi fakulu_ minha_ wa at'imul ba_ isal faqir
29.	Sum mal yaqdu_ tafatsahum wal yu_fu_ nudzu_rahum walyat taw wafu_ bil baitil atiq
30.	Za_lika, wa may yu'az zhim huruma_til la_hi fahuwa hairul lahu_ indarab bihi wa uhil lat lakumul an'a_mi il la_ ma_ yutla_ alaikum fajtanibur rijsa minal autsa_ni wajtanibu_ qaulaz zu_r
31.	Hunafa_ a lil la_hi ghaira musrikina bihi wa may yusrik bil la_hi faka_an nama_ khar ra minas sama_i fatakhthafuhuth thairu au tahwi bihir rihu fi maka_nin sahiq
32.	Za_lika wa may yu'az zhim sa'a_iral la_hi fa in naha_ min taqwal qulu_b
33.	Lakum fiha_ mana_fi'u ila_ ajalim musam man sum ma mahil luha_ ilal baitil 'atiq
34.	Wa likul li um matin ja'alna_ mansakal liyazkurus mal la_hi 'ala_ ma_ razaqahum mim bahimatil an'a_m fa ila_ hukum ila_huw wa_hidun falahu_ aslimu_ wa bas siril mukhbitin
35.	Alazina iza_ zukiral la_hu wajilat qulu_buhum was sa_birina 'ala_ ma_ asha_bahum wal muqimis sala_ti wa mim ma_ razaqna_hum yunfiqu_n
36.	Wal budna ja'alna_ha_ lakum min sa'a_ril la_hi lakum fiha_ khairun fazkurus mal la_hi 'alaiha_ sawa_f fa iza_ wajabat junu_buha_ fakulu_ minha_ wa at'imul qa_ni'a wal mu'tar kaza_lika sakh kharna_ha_ lakum la'al lakum taskurun
37.	Lay yana_lal la_ha luhu_muha_ wa la_ dima_ uha_ wa la_kiy yana_luhut taqwa_ minkum kaza_lika sakh  kharaha_ lakum litukab birul la_ha 'ala_ ma_ hada_kum wa bas siril muhsinin
38.	In nal la_ha yuda_fi'u anil lazina a_manu_ in nal la_ha la_ yuhib bukul la khaw wa_nin kafu_r
39.	Uzina lil lazina yuqa_talu_na bi an nahum zulimu_ wa in nal la_ha 'ala_ nasrihim laqadir
40.	Nil lazina ukhriju_ min diya_rihim bigairi haq qin il la_ ay yaqu_lu_ rab bunal la_h wa laula_ daf'ul la_hin na_sa ba'dahum biba'dil lahud dimat sawa_mi'u wa biya'uw wa salawa_tuw wa masa_jidu yuzkaru fihas mul la_hi katsira_ wa layanshuran nal la_hu may yansuruh in nal la_ha laqawiy yun 'aziz
41.	Al lazina im mak kan na_hum fil ardi aqa_mus sala_ta wa a_tuz zaka_ta wa amaru_ bil ma'ru_fi wa nahau anil munkar wa lil la_hi 'a_qibatul umu_r
42.	Wa iy yukaz zibu_ka faqad kadzabat qablahum qaumu nu_hiw wa 'a_duw wa samu_d
43.	Wa qaumu ibra_hima wa qaumu lu_t
44.	Wa asha_bu mad yan wa kuz ziba mu_sa_ fa amlaitu lilka_firina sum ma akhaztuhum fakaifa ka_na nakir
45.	Faka ay yim min qaryatin ahlakna_ha_ wa hiya za_limatun fahiya kha_wiyatun 'ala_ uru_syiha_ wa bi'rim mu'at talatiw wa qasrim masyid
46.	Afalam yasiru_ fil ardi fataku_na lahum qulu_buy ya'qilu_na biha_ au a_za_nuy yasma'u_na biha_ fa in naha_ la_ ta'mal absa_ru wa la_kin ta'mal qulu_bul lati fis sudu_r
47.	Wa yasta'julu_naka bil'aza_bi wa lay yukhifal la_hu wa'dahu_ wa in na yauman 'inda rab bika ka alfi sanatim mim ma_ ta'ud du_n
48.	Wa ka ay yim min qaryatin amlaitu laha_ wa hiya za_limatun sum ma akhadztuha_ wa ilay yal masir
49.	Qul ya_ ay yuhan na_su in nama_ ana_ lakum nadzirum mubin
50.	Fal lazina a_manu_ wa 'amilus sa_liha_ti lahum magfiratuw wa rizqun karim
51.	Wal lazina sa'aufi a_ya_tina_ mu'a_jizina ula_ ika asha_bul jahim
52.	Wa ma_ arsalna_ min qablika mir rasu_liw wa la_ nabiy yin il la_ iza_ taman na_ alqas saitha_nu fi umniy yatih fayansakul la_hu ma_ yulqis saita_nu sum ma yukhimul lahu a_ya_tih wal la_hu 'alimun hakim
53.	Liyaj'ala ma_ yulqis saita_nu fit natal lil lazina fi qulu_bihim maraduw wal qa_siyati qulu_buhum wa in naz za_limina lafi siqa_qim ba'id
54.	Wa liya lamal lazina u_tul 'ilma an nahul haq qu mir rab bika fayu'minu_ bihi fatukbita lahu_ qulu_buhum wa in nal la_ha laha_dil lazina a_manu_ ila_ sira_tim mustaqim
55.	Wa la_ yaza_hul lazina kafaru_ fi miryatim minhu hat ta_ ta'tiyahumus sa_'atu bagtatan au ya'tiyahum 'aza_bu yaumin 'aqim
56.	Almulku yauma izil lil la_h yahkumu bainahum fal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti fi jan na_tin naim
57.	Wal lazina kafaru_ wa kaz zabu_ bi a_ya_tina_ fa ula_ ika lahum aza_bum muhin
58.	Wal lazina ha_jaru_ fi sabilil la_hi sum ma qutilu_ au ma_tu_ layarzuqan nahumul la_hu rizqan hasana_ wa in nal la_ha lahuwa hairur ra_ziqin
59.	Layudhilan nahum mudhalay yardaunahu_ wa in nal la_ha la'alimun halim
60.	Za_lika wa man 'a_qaba bimitsli ma_ 'u_qiba bihi sum ma bugiya 'alaihi layansuran nahul la_h in nal la_ha la'afuw wun gafu_r
61.	Za_lika bi an nal la_ha yu_lijul laila fin naha_ri wa yu_lijun naha_ra fil laili wa an nal la_ha sami'um basir
62.	Za_lika bi an nal la_ha huwal haq qu wa an na ma_ yad'u_na min du_nihi huwal ba_tilu wa an nal la_ha huwal 'aliy yul kabir
63.	Alam tara an nal la_ha abzala minas sama_i ma_ an fatusbihul ardu mukhdar rah in nal la_ha latifun habir
64.	Lahu_ ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ard wa in nal la_ha lahuwal ganiy yul hamid
65.	Alam tara an nal la_ha sak kara lakum ma_ fil ardi wal fulka tajri fil bahri bi amrihi wa yumsikus sama_ a an taqa'a 'alal ardi il la_ bi iznih in nal la_ha bin na_si lara u_fur rahim 
66.	Wa huwal lazi ahya_kum sum ma yumitukum sum ma yuhyikum in nal insa_na lakafu_r
67.	Likul li um matin ja'alna_ mansakan hum na_siku_hu fala_ yuna_zi un naka fil amri wad'u ila_ rab bik in naka la ala_ hudam mustaqim
68.	Wa in ja_dalu_ka faqulil la_hu a'lamu bima_ ta'malu_n
69.	Al la_hu yahkumu bainakum yaumal qiya_mati fima_ kuntum fihi tahtalifu_n
70.	Alam ta'lam an nal la_ha ya'lamu ma_ fis sama_i wal ardi in na za_lika fi kita_b in na za_lika 'alal la_hi yasir
71.	Wa ya'budu_na min du_nil la_hi ma_ lam yunaz zil bihi sulta_naw wa ma_ laisa lahum bihi 'ilm wa ma_ liz za_limina min nasir
72.	Wa iza_ tutla_ 'alaihim a_ya_tuna_ bay yina_tin ta'rifu fi wuju_hil lazina kafarul munkar yaka_du_na yastu_na bil lazina yatlu_na alaihim a_ya_tina_ qul afa unab bi ukum bisar rim min za_likum ana_r wa adahal la_hul lazina kafaru_ wa bisal masir
73.	Ya_ ay yuhan na_su duriba matsalun fastami'u_ lah in nal lazina tad'u_na min du_nil la_hi lay yahluqu_ zuba_baw wa lawij tama'u_ lah wa iy yaslubhumuz zuba_bu sai al la_ yastanqizu_hu min da'ufat ta_libu wal matlu_b
74.	Ma_ qadarul la_ha haq qa qadrih in nal la_ha laqawiy yun aziz
75.	Al la_hu yastafi minal mala_ ikati rusuluw wa minan na_s in nal la_ha sami'um basir
76.	Ya'lamu ma_ baina aidihim wa ma_ halfahum wa ilal la_hi turja'ul umu_r
77.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ ka'u_ was judu_ wa budu_ rab bakum waf 'alul haira la'al lakum tuflihu_n
78.	Wa ja_hidu_ fil la_hi haq qa jiha_dih huwaj taba_kum wa ma_ ja'ala 'alikum fid dini min haraj mil lata abikum ibra_him huwa sam ma_kumul muslimina min qablu wa fi ha_za_ liyaku_nar rasu_lu sahidan 'alaikum wa taku_nu_ suhada_ a 'alan na_s fa aqimus sala_ta wa a_tuz zaka_ta wa tasimu_ bil la_h huwa maula_kum fani'mal maula_ wa ni'man nasir
.EndTopic
