.Topic qsShad  " 38. Sha_d"
1.	Sa_d wal qur a_nizil dikir
2.	Balil lazina kafaru_ fi iz zatiw wa siqa_q
3.	Kam ahlakna_ min qablihim min qarnin fana_da wa la_ta hina mana_s
4.	Wa ajibu_ an ja_ ahum munzirum manhum wa qa_lal ka_firu_na ha_za_ sa_hirun kaz za_b
5.	Aja alal a_lihata ila_haw wa_hida_ in na ha_za_ lasyai uja_b
6.	Wantalaqal mala u minhum anim su_ wasbiru_ ala_ a_lihatikum in na ha_za_ lasyai uy yura_d
7.	Ma_ samina_ biha_za_ fil mil latil a_khirah in ha_za_ il lak tila_q
8.	A unzila alaihiz zikru min bainina_ bal hum fi sak kim min zikri bal lam ma_ yazu_qu_
9.	Am indahum khaza_ inu rahmati rab bikal azizil wah hab
10.	Am lahum mulkus sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa ma_ bainahuma_ fal yartaqu_ fil asba_b
11.	Jundum ma_ huna_lika mahzu_mum minal ahza_b
12.	Kaz zabat qablahum qaumu nu_hiw wa a_duw wa firaunu zul auta_d
13.	Wa samu_du wa qaumu lu_tiw wa asha_bul aikah ula_ ikal ahza_b
14.	In kul lun il la_ kaz zabar rusula fahaq qa iqa_b
15.	Wa ma_ yanzuru ha_ ula_ I il la_ saihataw wa_hidatam ma_ laha_ min fawa_q
16.	Wa qa_lu_ rab bana_ aj jil lana_ qitana_ qabla yaumil hisa_b
17.	Isbir ala_ ma_ yaqu_lu_na waz kur abdana_ da_wu_da zal aid in nahu_ aw wa_b
18.	In na_ sak karna_l jiba_la ma'ahu_ yusab bihna bil asyiy yi wal isra_q
19.	Wat taira mahsu_rah kul lul lahu_ aw wa_b
20.	Wa sadadna_ mulkahu_ wa a_taina_hul hikmata wa faslal khita_b
21.	Wa hal ata_ka naba ul hasmi iz ta saw warul mihra_b
22.	Iz dakalu_ ala_ da_wu_da fafazia minhum qa_lu_ la_ takhal hasma_ni baga_ baduna_ ala_  badin fahkum bainana_ bil haq qi wa la_ tustit wahdina_ ila_ sawa_ is sira_t
23.	In na ha_za_ akhi lahu_ tisuw wa tisu_na najataw waliya najatuw wa_ hidah fa qa_la akfilniha_ wa az zani fil khita_b
24.	Qa_la laqad zalamaka bisu a_li najatika ila_ nia_jih wain na katsiram minal hulata_i layabgi baduhum ala_ badin il lal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti wa qalilum ma_ hum wa zan na da_wu_du an nama_ fatan na_hufastagfara rab bahu_ wa khar ra ra_ki aw wa ana_h
25.	Faghafarna_ lahu_ za_lik wa in na lahu_ indana_ lazulfa_ wa husna_ ma a_b
26.	Ya_ da_wu_du in na_ ja'alna_ka kalifatan fil ardi fahkum bainan na_si bil haq qi wa la_ tat tabi il hawa_ fayudil laka an sabilil la_h in nal lazina yadil lu_na an sabilil la_hi lahum aza_bun sadidun  bima_ na su_ yaumal hisa_b
27.	Wa ma_ khalaqnas sama_ a wal arda wa ma_ bainahuma_ ba_tila_ za_lika zan nul lazina kafaru_ fawailul lil lazina kafaru_ minan na_r
28.	Am najalul lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti kal mufsidina fil ard am najalul mut taqina kal fuj ja_r
29.	Kita_bun anzalna_hu ilaika muba_rakul liyad dab baru_ a_ya_tihi wa liyatazak kara ulul alba_b
30.	Wa wahabna_ lida_wu_da sulaima_n nimal abd in nahu_ aw wa_b
31.	Iz urida alaihi bil asyiy yis sa_fina_tul jiya_d
32.	Faqa_la in ni ahbabtu hub bal khairi an zikri rab bi hat ta_ tawa_rat bil hija_b
33.	Rud du_ha_ alay fatafiqa mas ham bis su_qi wal ana_q
34.	Wa laqad fatan na_ sulaima_na wa al qaina_ ala_ kursiy yihi jasadan sum ma ana_b
35.	Qa_la rab bigfir li wa hab li mulkal la_ yan bagi li ahadim min badi in naka antal wah ha_b
36.	Fasak karna_ lahur riha tajri bi am rihi ruka_ an haitsu asha_b
37.	Was saya_tina kul la ban na_ iw wa gaw wa_s
38.	Wa a_khirina muqar ranina fil asfa_d
39.	Ha_za_ ata_ una_ famnun au amsik bigairi hisa_b
40.	Wa in na lahu_ indana_ lazulfa_ wa husna ma a_b
41.	Wazkur abdana_ ay yu_b iz na_da_ rab bahu_ an ni mas saniyas saita_nu binusbiw wa aza_b
42.	Urkud birijlik ha_za_ mugtasalun ba_riduw wa sara_b
43.	Wa wahabna_ lahu_ ahlahu_ wa mitslahum maahum rahmatam min na_ wa zikra_ li ulil alba_b
44.	Wa kuz biyadika digsan fadrib bihi wa la_ takhnats in na_ wajadna_hu sa_bira_ nimal abdu in nahu_ aw wa_b
45.	Wazkur iba_dana_ ibra_hima wa isha_q wa yaqu_ba ulil aidi wal absa_r
46.	In na_ akhlasna_hum bikha_lisatin zikrad da_r
47.	Wa in nahum indana_ laminal mustafainal akhya_r
48.	Wazkur isma_ila wal yasaa wa zal kif wa kul lum minal akhya_r
49.	Ha_za_ zikr wa in na lilmut taqina lahusnu ma a_b
50.	Jan na_ti adnim mufat tahatal lahumul abwa_b
51.	Mut taki na fiha_ yadu_na fiha_ bifa_kihatin katsiratiw wa sara_b
52.	Wa indahum qa_sira_tut tarfi atra_b
53.	Ha_za_ ma_ tu_adu_na liyaumi hisa_b
54.	In na ha_za_ larizquna_ ma_ lahu_ min nafa_d
55.	Ha_za_ wa in na lit ta_ghina lasar ra ma a_b
56.	Jahan nam yaslaunaha_ fabisal miha_d
57.	Ha_za_ falyazu_qu_hu hamimuw wa gas sa_q
58.	Wa a_kharu min saklihi azwa_j
59.	Ha_za_ faijum muqtahimum maakum la_ marhaban bihim in nahum sa_lun na_r
60.	Qa_lu_ bal antum la_ marhaban bikum antum qad damtumu_hu lana_ fabisal qara_r
61.	Qa_lu_ rab bana_ man qad dama lana_ ha_za_ fazid hu aza_ban difan fin na_r
62.	Wa qa_lu_ ma_ lana_ nara_ rija_lan kun na_ naud duhum minal asra_r
63.	At takazna_hum sikriy yan am za_gat anhumul absa_r
64.	In na za_lika lahaq qun taka_shumu ahlin na_r
65.	Qul in nama_ ana munziruw wa ma_ min ila_hin il lal la_hul wa_hidul qaha_r
66.	Rab bus sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa ma_ bainahumal azizul gaf fa_r
67.	Qul huwa naba un azim
68.	Antum anhu muridu_n
69.	Ma_ ka_na liya min ilmin bil mala il ala_ iz yahtasimu_n
70.	Iy yuha_ ilay ya il la_ an nama_ ana nazirum mubin
71.	Iz qa_la rab buka lilmala_ ikati in ni kha_liqun basyaram min tin
72.	Fa iza_ saw waituhu_ wa nafaktu fihi mir ru_hi faqau_ lahu_ sa_jidin
73.	Fasajadal mala_ ikatu kul luhum ajmau_n
74.	Il la_ iblis istakbara wa ka_na minal ka_firin
75.	Qa_la ya_ iblisu ma_ manaaka an tasjuda lima_ khalaqtu biyaday ya astakbarta am kunta minal a_lin
76.	Qa_la ana_ khairum minhu khalaqtani min na_riw wa khalaqtahu_ min tin
77.	Qa_la fakruj minha fa in naka rajim
78.	Wa in na alaika lanati ila_ yaumid din
79.	Qa_la rab bi fa anirni ila_ yaumi yub atsu_n
80.	Qa_la fa in naka minal munzarin
81.	Ila_ yaumil waqtil malu_m
82.	Qa_la fabiiz zatika la ugwiyan nahum ajmain
83.	Il la_ iba_daka minhumul muklasin
84.	Qa_la fal haq qu wal haq qa aqu_l
85.	La amla an na jahan nama minka wa mim man tabiaka minhum ajmain
86.	Qul ma_ as alukum alaihi min ajriw wa ma_ ana minal mutakal lifin
87.	In huwa il la_ zikrul lil a_lamin
88.	Wa latalamun na naba ahu_ bada hin
.EndTopic
;_____________________________
.Topic qsAz-Zumar  " 39. Az Zumar"
1.	Tanzilul kita_bi minal la_hil azizil hakim
2.	In na anzalna_ ilaikal kita_ba bil  haqi fa budil la_ha mukhlisal lahud din
3.	Ala_ lil la_hid dinul ha_lis wal lazinat takhazu_ min du_nihi auliya_ a ma_ nabuduhum il la_ liyuqar ribu_na_ ilal la_hi zulfa_ in nal la_ha yahkumu bainahum fi ma_ hum fihi yahtalifu_n in nal la_ha la_ yahdi man huwa ka_zibun kaf fa_r
4.	Lau ara_dal la_hu ay yat takhiza wa ladal lastafa_ mim ma_ yakhluqu ma_ yasya_ u subha_nah huwal la_hul wa_hidul qah ha_r
5.	Halaqas sama_wa_ti wal arda bil haq yukaw wirul laila Qalan naha_ri wa yukaw wirun naha_ra alal laili wa sah haras samsa wal qamar kul luy yajri li ajalim musam ma_ ala_ huwal azizul gaf fa_r
6.	Halaqakum min nafsiw wa_hidatin sum ma ja'ala minha_ zaujaha_ wa anzala lakum minal ana_mi sama_niyata azwa_j yahlukuqum fi butu_ni ummaha_tikum halqam min badi halqin fi zuluma_tin sala_ts za_likumul la_hu rab bukum lahul mulku la_ ila_ha il la_ huw fa an na_ tusrafu_n
7.	In takfuru_ fa in nal la_ha ganiy yun ankum wa la_ yarda_ liiba_dihil kufr wa in taskuru_ yardahu lakum wa la_ taziru wa_ziratuw wizra ukha_ sum ma ila_ rab bikum marjiukum fayunab bi ukum bima_ kuntum tamalu_na in nahu_ alimun biza_tis sudu_r
8.	Wa iza_ masal insa_na dur run daa_ rab bahu_ muniban ilaihi sum ma iza_ haw wa lahu_ nimatam minhu nasiya ma_ ka_na yadu_ ilaihi min qablu wa ja'ala lil la_hi anda_dal liyudil la an sabilih qul tamat bikufrika qalilan in naka min as ha_bin na_r
9.	Am man huwa qa_nitun a_na_ al laili sa_jidaw waqa_ imay yah zarul a_hirata wa yarju_ rahmata rab bih qul hal yastaw lazina yalamu_na wal lazina la yalamu_n in nama_ yatazak karu ulul alba_b
10.	Qul ya_ iba_dil lazina a_manut taqu_ rab bakum lil lazina ahsanu_ fi ha_zihid dun ya_ hasanah wa ardul la_hi wa_siah in nama_ yuwaf fas sabiru_na ajrahum bigairi hisa_b
11.	Qul in ni umirtu an abudal la_ha muhlisal lahud din
12.	Wa umirtu li an aku_na aw walal muslimin
13.	Qul in ni akha_fu in ashaitu rab bi aza_ba yaumin azim
14.	Qulil la_hi abudu muhlisal lahu_ dini
15.	Fabudu_ ma_ situm min du_nih qul in nal ha_sirinal lazina hasiru_ anfusahum wa ahlihim yaumal qiya_mah ala_ za_lika huwal husra_nul mubin
16.	Lahum min fauqihim zulalum minan na_ri wa min tahtihim zulal za_lika yukaw wiful la_hu bihi iba_dah ya_ iba_di fat taqu_n
17.	Wal lazinaj tanabut ta_gu_ta ay yabudu_ha_ wa ana_bu_ ilal la_hi la humul busra_ fabas sir iba_d
18.	Al lazina yastamiu_nal qaula fayat tbiu_na ahsanah ula_ ikal lazina hada_humul la_hu wa ula_ ika hum ulul alba_b
19.	Afaman haq qa alaihi kalimatul aza_b afa anta tunqizu man fin na_r
20.	La_kinil lazinat rab bahum lahum gurafum min fauqiha_ gurafum mabniy yatun tajri min tahtihal anha_ru wadal la_h la_ yuhliful la_hul mia_d
21.	Alam tara an nal la_ha anzala minas sama_ i ma_ an fasalakahu_ yana_bia fil ardi sum ma yuhriju bihi zaram muhtalifan alwa_nuhu_ sum ma yahiju fatara_hu musfar ran sum ma yajaluhu_ huta_man in na fi za_lika lazikra_ li ulil alba_b
22.	Afaman sarahal la_hu sadrahu_ lil isla_mi fahuwa ala_ nu_rim mir rabih fawailul lilqa_siyati qulu_buhum min zikril la_h ula_ ika fi dala_lim mubin
23.	Al la_hu naz zala ahsanal hadisi kita_bam mutasa_biham matsa_ niyataq sa ir ru minhu julu_dul lazina yahsauna rab bahum sum ma talinu julu_duhum wa qulu_buhum ila_ zikril la_h za_lika hudal la_hi yahdi bihi may yasya_ wa man yudlilil la_hu fama_ lahu_ min ha_d
24.	Afamay yat taqi biwajihi su_ al aza_bi yaumal qiya_mati wa qila liz za_limina zu_qu_ ma_ kuntum taksibu_n
25.	Kaz zabal lazina min qablihim fa_ta_humul aza_bu min haitsu la_ yasuru_n
26.	Fa aza_qahumul la_hul hizya fil haya_tid dun ya_ wa la'aza_bul a_hirati akbar lau ka_nu_ yalamu_n
27.	Wa laqad darabna_ lin na_si fi haa_zal qur a_ni min kul li matsalil la al lahum yatazak karu_n
28.	Qur a_nan arabiy yan gaira zi iwajil la'al lahum yat taqu_n
29.	Darabal la_hu matsaral rajulan fihi suraka_ u mutasa_kisu_na wa rajulan salamal lirajulin hal yastawiya_ni matsalan alhamdu lil la_h bal aksaruhum la_ yalamu_n
30.	In naka may yituw wa in nahum may yitu_n
31.	Sum ma in nakum yaumal qiya_mati inda rab bikum taktasimu_n
32.	Faman azhlamu mim man kazaba alal la_hi wa kaz zaba bis sidiq iz ja_ ah alaisa fi jahan nama matswal lilka_firin
33.	Wal lazi ja_ a bis sidiq qa sad daqa bihi ula_ ika humul mut taqu_n
34.	Lahum ma_ yasya_ u_na inda rab bihim za_lika jaza_ ul muhsinin
35.	Liyukaf firal lahu anhum aswa al lazi amilu wa yajziyahum ajrahum bi ahsani lazi ka_nu_ yamalu_n
36.	Alaisal la_hu bika_fin abdah wa yukaw wifu_naka bil lazina min du_nih wa may yudlilil la_hu fama_ lahu_ min ha_d
37.	Wa may yahdil la_hu lama_ lahu_ mim mudil alaisal la_hu biazizin zintiqa_m
38.	Wa la in sa altahum man halaqas sama_wa_ti wal arda layaqu_lun nal la_h qul afara aitum ma_ tadu_na min du_nil la_hi in ara_daniyal la_hu bidur rin hal hun na ka_sifa_tu dur rihi au ara_dani birahmatin hal hun na mumsika_turahmatih qul hasbiyal la_h alaihi yatakwak kalul mutawak kilu_n
39.	Qul ya_ qaumimalu_ ala_ maka_natikum in ni a_milun fasaufa talamu_n
40.	May yatihi aza_buy yukhzihi wa wa yahil lu alaihi aza_bun muqim
41.	In na_ anzalna_ alaikal kita_ba lin na_ si bil haq famanih tada_ falinafsih wa man dal la fa in nama_ yadil lu alaiha_ wa ma_ anta alaihin biwakil
42.	Al la_hu yatawaf fal anfusa hina mautiha_ wal lati lam tamut fi mana_miha_ fayumsikul lati qada_ alaihal mauta wa yursilul ukhra_ ila_ ajalin musam ma_ in na fi za_lika la a_ya_til liqaumiy yatafak karu_n
43.	Amit takhazu_ min du_nil la_hi sufa a_ qul awalau ka_nu_ la_ yamiliku_na sai aw wa la_ yaqilu_n
44.	Qul lil la_his safa_ atu jami a_ lahu_ mulkus sama_wa_ti wal ard sum ma ilaihi turja u_n
45.	Wa iza_ zukiral la_hu wahsahus ma az zat qulu_bul lazina la_ yuminu_na bil a_khirah wa iza_ zukiral lazina min du_nihi iza_ hum yastabsiru_n
46.	Qulil la_hum ma fa_tiras sama_wa_ti wal ard a_limal gaibi was saha_dati anta tahkumu baina fiba_dika fima_ ka_nu_ fihi yakhtalifu_n
47.	Wa lau an na lil lazina zalamu_ ma_ fil ardi jamiaw mitslahu_ maahu_ laftadau bihi min su_il aza_bi yaumai qiya_mah wa bada_lahum minal la_hi ma_ lam yaku_nu_ yahtasibu_n
48.	Wa bada_lahum say yi a_tu ma_ kasabu_ wa ha_qa bihim ma_ ka_nu_ bihi yastahzi u_n
49.	Fa iza_ mas sam insa_na dur run daa_na_ sum ma iza_ khaw walna_hu nima_tam min na_ qa_la in nama_ u_tituhu_ ala_ ilm bal hiya fitnatuw wa la_kin na aksarahum la_ yalamu_n
50.	Qad da_lahal lazina min qablihim fama_ agna_ anhum ma_ ka_nu_ yaksibu_n
51.	Fa asha_bahum say yi a_tu ma_ kasabu_ wal lazina zalamu_ min ha_ula_ I sayusibihim say yi a_tu ma_ kasabu_ wa ma_ hum bimujizin
52.	Awalam yalamu_ an nal la_ha yabsuthur rijqa limay yasya_ u wa yaqdir in na fi za_lika la a_ya_til liqaumiy yuminu_n
53.	Qul ya_ iba_diyal lazina asrafu_ ala_ anfusihim la_ taqnatu_ mir rahmatil la_h in nal la_h in nal la_ha yagfiruz zunu_ba jamia_ in nahu_ huwal gafu_rur rahim
54.	Wa anibu_ ila_ rab bikum wa aslimu_ lahu_ min qabli ay yatiyakumul aza_bu sum ma la_ tunsaru_n
55.	Wat tabiu_ ahsana ma_ unzila ilaikum mir rab bikum min qabli ay yatiyakumul aza_bu bagtataw wa antum la_ tasuru_n
56.	An taqu_la nafsuy ya_ hasrata_ ala_ ma_ far rathu fi jan bil la_hi wa in kuntu laminas sa_hirin
57.	An taqu_la lau an nal la_ha hada_ni lakuntu la_ minal mut taqin
58.	Au taqu_la hina taral aza_ba lau an na li kar ratan fa aku_na minal muhsinin
59.	Bala_ qad ja_ atka a_ya_ti fakaz zabta biha_ wastakbarta wa kunta minal ka_firin
60.	Wa yaumal qiya_mati taral lazina kazabu_ alal la_hi wuju_huhum mus wad dah alaisa fi jahan nama matswal lil mutakab birin
61.	Wa yunaj jil la_hul lazinat taqau bimafa_zatihim la_ yamas suhumus su_ u wa la_ hum yahzanu_n
62.	Al la_hu kha_liqu kul li sai iw wa huwa ala_ kuli sai iw wakil
63.	Lahu_ maqa_lidus sama_wa_ti wal ard wal lazina kafaru_ bi a_ya_til la_hi ula_ ika humul kha_siru_n
64.	Qul afaghairal la_hi tamuru_n ni abudu ay yuhal ja_hilu_n
65.	Wa laqad u_hiya ilaika wa ilal lazina min qablik la in asrakta layahbatana amaluka wa lataku_nan na minal kha_sirin
66.	Balil la_ha fabud wa kum minas sa_kirin
67.	Wa ma_ qadarul la_ha haq qa qadrihi wal ardu jamian qabdatuhu_ yaumal qiya_mati was sama_wa_tu matwiy ya_tun biyaminih subha_nahu wataa_la_ am ma_ yusriku_n
68.	Wa nufikha fis su_ri fashaiqa man fis sama_wati wa man fil ardi il la_ man sa_ al la_h sum ma nufikha fihi ukhra_ fa iza_ hum qiya_muy yanzhuru_n
69.	Wa asraqatil ardu binu_ri rab biha_ wa wudial kita_bu wa ji a bin nabiyina was suhada_ I wa qudiya bainahum bil haq qi wa hum la_ yuzlamu_n
70.	Wa wuf fiyat kul lu nafsim ma_ amilat wa huwa alamu bima_ yafalu_n
71.	Wa siqal lazina kafaru_ ila_ jahanama zumara_ hat ta_ iza_ ja_ u_ha_ futihat abwa_buha_ wa qa_la lahum khazanatuha_ alam yatikum rusulum minkum yatlu_na alaikum a_ya_ti rab bikum wa yunziru_nakum liqa_ a yaumikum ha_za_qa_lu_ bala_ wa la_kin haq qat kalimatul aza_bi alal ka_firin
72.	Qilad khulu_ azwa_ba jahan nama kha_lidina fiha_ fabisa matswal mutakab birin
73.	Wa siqal lazinat taqau rab bahum ilal jan nati zumara_ hat ta_ iza_ ja_ u_ha_ wa futihat abwa_buha_ wa qa_la lahum khazanatuha_ sala_mun alaikum tibtum fad khulu_ha_ kha_lidin
74.	Wa qa_lul hamdu lil la_hil lazi sadaqana_ wadahu_ wa auratsanal arda natabaw wa u minal jan na_ti haitsu nasya_ u fanima ajrul a_milin
75.	Wa taral mala_ikata ha_f fina min haulil arsi yusab bihu_na bihamdi rab bihim wa qudiya bainahum bil haq qi wa qilal hamdu lil la_hi rab bil a_lamin
.EndTopic
;______________________________________
.Topic qsAl-Mukmin  " 40. Al Mukmin"
1.	Ha_ mim
2.	Tanzilul kita_bi minal la_hil azizil alim
3.	Gha_fariz zan bi wa qa_bilit taubi sadidil iqa_bi zit taul la_ il la_ha il la_ huw wlaihil masir
4.	Ma_ yuja_dilu fi a_ya_til la_hi il lal lazina kafaru_ fala_ yagrurka taqalubuhum fil bila_d
5.	Kaz zabat qablahum qaumu nu_hiw wal ahza_bu min badihim wa hamat kul lu um matin birasu_lihim liyakhuzu_hu wa ja_dalu_ bil ba_tili liyud hidu_ bihil haq qa fa akhaz tuhum fakaifa ka_na iqa_b
6.	Wa kaza_lika haq qat kalimatu rab bika alal lazina kafaru_ an nahum asha_bun na_r
7.	Al lazina yahmilu_nal arsa wa man haulahu_ yusab bihu_na bihamdi rabihim wa yuminu_na bihi wa yastagfiru_na lil lazina a_manu_ rabana_ wa sita kul la sai ir rahmataw wa ilman tagfir lil lazina ta_bu_wat tabau_ sabilaka waqihim aza_bal jahim
8.	Rab bana_ wa adkhilhum jan na_ti adnil lati wa adtahum wa man salaha min a_ba ihim wa azwa_jihim wa zur riy ya_tihim in naka antal azizul hakim
9.	Wa qihimus say yi a_t wa man taqis say yi a_ti yauma izin faqad rahimtah wa za_lika huwal fauzul azhim
10.	In nal lazina kafaru_ yuna_da una lamaqtul la_hi akbaru mim maqtikum anfusakum iz tadauna ilal ima_ni fatakfuru_n
11.	Qa_lu_ rab bana_ amat tanats nataini wa ahyaitanats nataini fatarafna_ bizunu_bina_ fahal ila_ khuru_jim min sabil
12.	Za_likum bi an nahu_ iza_ duiyal lahu wahdahu_ kafartum wa iy yusy rak bihi tuminu_ falhukmu lil la_hil aliy yil kabir
13.	Huwal lazi yurikum a_ya_tihi wa yunaz zilu lakum minas sama_i rizqa_ wa ma_ yatazak karu il la_ may yunib
14.	Fadul la_ha muklisina lahud dina walau karihal ka_firu_n
15.	Rafiud daraja_ti zul arsy yulqiru_ha min amrihi ala_ may yasya_ u min iba_dihi liyunzira yaumat tala_q
16.	Yauma hum ba_rizu_na la yakta_ alal la_hi minhum sai limanil mulkul yaum lil la_hil wa_hidil qah ha_r
17.	Alyauma tujza_ kul lu nafsin bima_ kasabat la_ zulmal yaum in nal la_ha sariul hisa_b
18.	Wa anzirhum yaumal a_zifati izil qulu_bu ladal hana_jiri ka_zimin ma_ liz za_limina min hami miw wa la_ safiiy yuta_
19.	Yalamu kha_ inatal ayuni wa ma_ tukhfis sudu_r
20.	Wal la_hu yaqdi bil haq wal lazina yadu_na min du_nihi la_ yaqdu_na bisai in nal la_ha huwas samiul basir
21.	Awalam yasuru_ fil ardi fayanzuru_ kaifa ka_na qa_qibatul lazina ka_nu_ min qablihim ka_nu_ hum asyad damin hum quw wataw wa a_tsaran fil ardi fa akazahumul la_hu bizunu_bihim wa ma_ ka_na lahum minal la_hi miw wa_q
22.	Za_lika bi an nahum ka_nat tatihim rusuluhum bil bay yina_ti fakafaru_ fa akazahumul la_h in nahu_ qawiy yun sadidul iqa_b
23.	Wa laqad arsalna_ mu_sa_ bi a_ya_tina_ wa sulta_nim mubin
24.	Ila_ firauna wa ha_ma_na wa qa_ru_na taqa_lu_ sa_hirun kaz za_b
25.	Falam ma_ ja_ ahum bil haq qi min indina_ qa_luqtulu_ abna_ al lazina a_manu_ maahu_ wastahyu_ nisa_ ahum wa ma_ kaidul ka_firina il la_ fi dala_l
26.	Wa qa_la firaunu zaru_ni aqtul mu_sa walyadu rab bah in ni akha_fu ay yubad dila dinakum au ay yuzhira fil ardil fasa_d
27.	Wa qa_la mu_sa_ in ni uztu birab bi wa rab bikum min kul li mutakab biril la_ yuminu biyaumil hisa_b
28.	Wa qa_la rajulum muminum min a_li firauna yaktumu ima_nahu_ ataqtulu_na rajulan ay yaqu_la rab biyal la_hu wa qad ja_ akum bil bay yina_ti mir rab bikum wa iy yaku ka_ziban fa'alaihi kazibuh wa iy yaku sa_diquy yushibkum badul lazi yaidukum in nal la_ha la_ yahdi man huwa musrifun kaz za_b
29.	Ya_ qaumi lakumul mulkul yauma za_hirina fil ardi famay yansuruna_ min basil la_hi in ja_ ana_ qa_la firauna ma_ urikum il la_ ma_ ara_ wa ma_ ahdikum il la_ sabilar rasya_d
30.	Wa qa_lal lazi a_mana ya_ qaumi in ni akha_fu alaikum mitsla yaumil ahza_b
31.	Mitsla dabi qaumi nu_hiw waa_diw wa samu_da wal lazina min badihim wa mal la_hu yuridu zulmal liliba_d
32.	Wa ya_ qaumi in ni akha_fu alaikum yaumat tana_d
33.	Yauma tuwal lu_na mudbirina ma_ lakum minal la_hi min asim wa may yudlilil la_hu fama_ lahu_ min ha_d
34.	Wa laqad ja_akum yu_sufu min qablu bil bay yina_ti fama_ ziltum fi sakim mim ma_ ja_ akum bih hat ta_ iza_ halaka qultum lay yab atsal la_hu min badihi rasu_la_ kaza_lika yudil lul la_hu man huwa musrifum murta_b
35.	Al lazina yuja_dilu_na fi a_ya_til la_hi bigairi sulta_nin ata_hum kabura maqtan indal la_hi wa indal lazina a_manu_ kaza_lika yatbaul la_hu ala_ kul li qabli mutakab birin jab ba_r
36.	Wa qa_la firaunu ya_ ha_ma_nubni li sarhal la al li ablugul asba_b
37.	Asba_bas sama_wa_ti fa at talia ila_ ila_hi mu_sa_ wa in ni la azun nuhu_ kaziba_ wa kaza_lika zuy yina li firauna su_ u amalihi wa sud da anis sabil wa ma_ kaidu firauna il la_ fi taba_b
38.	Wa qa_lal lazi a_mana ya_ qaumit tabiu_ni ahdikum sabilar rasya_d
39.	Ya_ qaumi in nama_ ha_zihil haya_tud dun ya_ mata_uw wa in nal a_khirata hiya da_rul qara_r
40.	Man amila say yi atan fala_ yujza_ il la_ mitslaha_ wa man amila sa_lihan min zakarin au unsa_ wa huwa muminun fa ula_ ika yadhulu_nal jan nata yurzaqu_na fiha_ bigairi hisa_b
41.	Wa ya_ qaumi ma_li adu_kum ilan naja_ti wa tadu_nani ilan na_r
42.	Tadu_nani li akfura bil la_hi wa usrika bihi ma_ laisa li bihi ilmuw wa ana_ adu_kum ilal azizil gaf fa_r
43.	La_ jarama an nama_ tadu_nani ilaihi laisa lahu_ dawatun fid dun ya_ wa la_ fil a_khirati wa an na marad dana_ ilal la_hi wa an nal musrifina hum asha_bun na_r
44.	Fasatazkuru_na ma_ aqu_lu lakum wa ufaw widu amri ilal la_h in nal la_ha basirun bil iba_d
45.	Fawaqa_hul la_hu say yi a_ti ma_ makaru_ wa ha_qa bi a_li firauna su_ ul aza_b
46.	An na_ru yuradu_na alaiha_ guduw waw wa asyiy ya_ wa yauma taqu_mus sa_atu adkhilu_ a_la firauna asyad dal aza_b
47.	Wa iz yataha_j ju_na fin na_ri fayaqu_lud duafa_ u lil lazinas takbaru_ in na_ kun na_ lakum tabaan fahal antum mugnu_na an na_ nasibam minan na_r
48.	Qa_lal lazina takbaru_ in na_ kul lun fiha_ in nal la_ha qad hakama bainal iba_d
49.	Wa qa_lal lazina fin na_r likhazanati jahan namadu_ rab bakum yukhaf fif an na_ yaumam minal aza_b
50.	Qa_lu_ awalam taku tatikum rusulukum bil bay yina_t qa_lu bala_ qa_lu_ fadu_ wa ma_ du'a_ ul ka_firina il la_ fi dala_l
51.	Ina_lanansuru rusulana_ wal lazina a_manu_ fil haya_tid dun ya_ wa yauma yaqu_mul asha_d
52.	Yauma la_ yanfauz za_limina maziratuhum wa lahumul lanatu wa lahum su_ ud da_r
53.	Wa laqad a_taina_ mu_sal huda_ wa  auratsna_ bani isra_ilal kita_b
54.	Hudaw wa zikra li ulil lalba_b
55.	Fasbir in na wadal la_hi haq quw was tagfir lizan bika wa sab bih bihamdi rab bika bil asiy yi wal ibka_r
56.	In nal lazina yuja_dilu_na fi a_ya_til la_hi bigairi sulta_nin ata_hum in fi sudu_rihim il la_ kibrum ma_ hum bi ba_ligihi fastaiz bil la_h in nahu_ huwas samiul basir
57.	Lakhalqus sama_wa_ti wal ardi akbaru min khalqin na_si wa la_kin na aksaran na_si la_ yalamu_n
58.	Wa ma_ yastawil ama_ wal basiru wal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti wa lal musi qalilam ma_ tatazak karu_n
59.	In nas sa_ata la a_tiyatul la_ raiba fiha_ wala_kin na aksaran na_si la_ yuminu_n
60.	Wa qa_la rab bukumud u_ni astajib lakum in nal lazina yastakbiru_na an iba_dati sayadkhulu_na jahan na ma_ da_khirin
61.	Al la_hul lazi jaala lakumul laila litas kunu_ fihi wan naha_ra mubsira_ in nala la_ha lazu_ fadlin alan na_si wa la_kin na aksaran na_si la_ yaskuru_n
62.	Za_likumul la_hu rab bukum kha_liqukul li sai la_ ila_ha il la_ huwa fa ana_ tufaku_n
63.	Kaza_lika yufakul lazina ka_nu_ bi a_ya_til la_hi yajhadu_n
64.	Al la_hul lazi jaala lakumul arda qara_raw was sama_ abina_ aw wasaw warakum fa ahsana suwarakum wa razaqakum minat tay yiba_t za_likumul la_hu rab bukum fataba_rakal la_hu rab bul a_lamin
65.	Huwal hay yu la_ ila_ha il la_ huwa fadu_hu muklisina lahud din alhamdu lil la_hi rab bil  a_lamin
66.	Qul in ni an abudal lazina tadu_na min du_nil la_hi lam ma_ ja_ aniyal bay yina_tu mir rab bi wa umirtu an uslima li rab bil a_lamin
67.	Huwal lazi khalaqakum min tura_bin sum ma min nutfatin sum ma min alaqatin sum ma yukhrijukum tiflan sum ma litablugu_ asyud dakum sum ma litaku_nu_ suyu_kha_ wa minkum may yutawaf fa_ min qablu wa litablugu_ ajalam musam ma_ wa la al lakum taqilu_n
68.	Huwal lazi yuhyi wa yumitu faiza_ qadha_ amran fa in nama_ yaqu_lu lahu_ kun fayaku_n
69.	Alam tara ilal lazina yuja_dilu_na fi a_ya_til la_h an na_ yusrafu_n
70.	Al lazina kaz zabu_ bi kita_bi wa bima_ arsalna_ bihi rusulana_ fasaufa yalamu_n
71.	Izil agla_lu fi ana_qihim was sala_sil yushabu_n
72.	Fil hamimi sum ma fin na_ri yusjaru_n
73.	Sum ma qila lahum ainama_ kuntum tusriku_n
74.	Min du_nil la_h qa_lu_ dal lau_ ana_ bal lam nakun nadu_ min qablu sai a_ kaza_lika yudil lul la_hul ka_firin
75.	Za_likum bima_ kuntum tafrahu_na fil ardi bigairil haq qi wa bima_ kuntum tamrahu_n
76.	Udkhulu_ abwa_ba jahan nama kha_lidina fiha_ fa bisa matswal mutakabirin
77.	Fasbir in na wadal la_hi haq qun faim ma_ nuriyan naka badal lazi naiduhum au natawaf fayan naka fa ilaina_ yurjau_n
78.	Wa laqad arsalna_ rusula min qablika minhum man qasasna_ alaika wa minhum mal lam naq sus alaika wa ma_ ka_na lirasu_lin ay yatiya bi a_yatin il la_ bi iznil la_hi fa iza_ ja_ a amrul la_hi qudiya bil haq qi wakasira huna_ likal mubtilu_n
79.	Al la_hul lazi ja'ala lakumul ana_ma litarkabu_ minha_ wa minha_ takulu_n
80.	Wa lakum fiha_ mana_fiu wa litablugu_ alaiha_ ha_jatan fi sudu_rikum wa alaiha_ wa alal fulki tuh malu_n
81.	Wa yurikum a_ya_tihi fa ay ya a_ya_til la_hi tunkiru_n
82.	Afalam yasiru_ fil ardi fayanzuru_ kaifa ka_na a_qibatul lazina min qablihim ka_nu_ aksara min hum wa asyad da quw wataw wa a_tsa_ran fil ardi fama_ agna_ anhum ma_ ka_nu_ yaksibu_n
83.	Falam ma_ ja_ at hum rusuluhum bil bay yina_ti farihu_ bima_ indahum minal ilmi wa ha_qa_ bihim ma_ ka_nu_ bihi yastahzi u_n
84.	Falam ma_ ra au basana_ qa_lu_ a_man na_ bil la_hi wahdahu_ wa kafarna_ bima_ kun na_ bihi musrikin
85.	Falam yaku yanfauhum ima_nuhum lam ma_ ra au basana_ sun natal la_hil lati qad khalat fi iba_dihi wa khasira huna_likal ka_firu_n
.EndTopic
;____________________________________
.Topic qsFush-Shilat  " 41. Fush Shilat"
1.	Ha_ mim
2.	Tanzilum minar rahma_nir rahim
3.	Kita_bun fus silat a_ya_tuhu_ qur a_nan arabiy yal liqaumiy yalamu_n
4.	Basiraw wa naziran fa arada aksaruhum fahum la_ yasmau_n
5.	Wa qa_lu_ qulu_buna_ fi akin natim mim ma_ tadu_na_ ilaihi wa fi a_za_nina_ waqruw wa min bainina_ wa bainika hija_bun famal in nana_ a_milu_n
6.	Qul in nama_ ana basarum mitslukum yu_ha_ ilay ya an nama_ ila_hukum ila_huw wa_hidun fastaqimu_ ilaihi was tagfiru_h wa wailul lil musrikin
7.	Al lazina a_ yutu_naz zaka_ta wa hum bil a_khiratihum ka_firu_n
8.	In nal lazina a_manu_ wa amilusa_liha_ti lahum ajrun gairu mamnu_n
9.	Qul ain nakum latakfu_runa bil lazi khalaqal arda fi yaumaini wa tajalu_na lahu_ asda_da_ za_lika rab bul a_lamin
10.	Wa ja'ala fiha_ rawa_siya min fauqiha_ wa ba_raka fiha_ wa qad dara fiha_ aqwa_taha_ fi arbaata ay ya_m sawa_ al lis sa_ ilin
11.	Sum mas tawa_ ilas sama_i wa hiya duka_nun faqa_la laha_ wa lil arditiya_ tauan au karha_ qa_lata_ ataina_ ta_ i in
12.	Faqada_hun na saba sama_wa_ti fi yaumaini wa auha_ fi kul li sama_ in amraha_ wa zay yan nas sama_ ad dun ya_ bi masa_biha wa hifza_ za_lika taqdirul azizil alim
13.	Fa in aradu_ faqul anzartukum sa_iqatam mitsla sa_iqati a_diw wa samu_d
14.	Iz ja_ at humur rusulu min baini aidihim wa min khalfihim al la_ tabudu_ ilal la_h qa_lu_ lau sa_ a rab buna_ la anzala mala_ikatan fa in na_ bima_ ursitum bihi ka_firu_n
15.	Fa am ma_ a_dun fastakbaru_ fil ardi bigairil haq qi wa qa_lu_ ma_ asyadu min na_ quw wah awalam yarau an nal la_hal lazi khalaqahum huwa asyad du minhum quw wah wa ka_nu_ bi a_ya_tina_ yajhadu_n
16.	Fa arsalna_ alaihim rihan sarsaran fi ay ya_min nahisa_til linuziqahum aza_bal khizyi fil haya_tid dun ya_ wa la'aza_bal a_khirati akhza_ wa hum la_ yunsaru_n
17.	Wa am ma_ samu_du fahadaina_hum fastahab bul ama_ alal huda_ fa akhazat hum sa_iqatu aza_bil hu_ ni bima_ ka_nu_ yaksibu_n
18.	Wanaj jainal lazina a_manu_ waka_nu_ yat taqu_n
19.	Wa yauma yuhsaru ada_ ul la_hi ilan na_ri fahum yu_za u_n
20.	Hat ta_ iza_ ma_ ja_ u_ha_ sahida alaihim samuhum wa absa_ruhum wa julu_duhum bima_ ka_nu_ yamalu_n
21.	Wa qa_lu_ li julu_dihim lima sahidtum alaina_ qa_lu_ antaqanal la_hul lazi antaqa kul la sai iw wa huwa khalaqkum aw wala mar ratiw wa ilaihi turjau_n
22.	Wa ma_ kuntum tastatiru_na ay yashada alaikum samukum wa la_ absa_rukum wa la_ julu_dukum wala_kin zanantum an nal la_ha la_ yalamu katsiram mim ma_ tamalu_n
23.	Wa za_likum zan nukumul lazi zanantum birab bikum arda_kum fasbahtum minal kha_sirin
24.	Fa iy yasbiru_ fan na_ru matswal lahum wa iy yastatibu_ fama_ hum minal mutabin
25.	Wa qay yadna_ lahum qurana_ a fa zaay yanu_ lahum ma_ baina aidihim wa ma_ khalfahum wa haq qa alaihimul qaulu fi umamin qad khalat min qablihim minal jin ni wal insi inahum ka_nu_ kha_sirin
26.	Wa qa_lal lazina kafaru_ la_ tasmau_ liha_zal qur a_ni wal gau fihi la'al lakum taglibu_n
27.	Falanuziqan nal lazina kafaru_ aza_ban sadidaw wa lanajziyan nahum aswa al lazi ka_nu_ yamalu_n
28.	Za_lika jaza_ u ada_ la_hin na_ru lahum fiha_ sa_rul khuld jaza_ an bima_ ka_nu_ bi a_ya_tina_ yajhadu_n
29.	Wa qa_lal lazina kafaru_ rab bana_ arinal lazzini adal la_na_ minal jin ni wal insi najalhuma_ tahta aqda_mina_ liyaku_na_ minal azfalin
30.	In nal lazina qa_lu_ rab bunal la_hu sum mas taqa_mu_ tatanaz zalu alaihimul mala_ ikatu al la_ takha_fu_ wa la_ tahzanu_ wa absyiru_ bil jan natil lati kuntum tu_adu_n
31.	Nahnu auliya_ ukum fil haya_tid dun ya_ wa fil a_khirati wa lakum fiha_ ma_ tastahi anfusukum wa lakum fi ha_ ma_ tad dau_n
32.	Nuzulam min gafu_rir rahim
33.	Wa man ahsanu qaulam mim man daa_ ilal la_hi wa amila sa_lihaw wa qa_la in nani minal muslimin
34.	Wa la_ tastawil hasanatu wa las say yi ah idfa bil lati hiya ahsanu fa izal lazi bainaka wa bainahu_ ada_watun ka an nahu_ waliy yun hamim
35.	Wa ma_ yulaq qa_ha_ ilal lazina sabaru_ wa ma_ yulaq qa_ha_ il la_ zu_haz zin azim
36.	Wa im ma_ yanzagan naka minas saita_ni nazgun fastaiz bil la_h in nahu_ huwas saul alim
37.	Wa min a_ya_tihil lailu wan naha_ru was samsu wal qamar la_ tasjudu_ lis samsi wa la_ lilqamari was judu_ lil la_hil lazi khalaqahun na in kuntum iy ya_hu tabudu_n
38.	Fa inis takbaru_ fal lazina inda rab bika yusab bihu_na lahu_ bil laili wan naha_ri wa hum la_ yas amu_n
39.	Wa min a_ya_tihi an naka taral arda kha_siatan fa iza_ anzalna_ alaihal ma_ ajtaz zat wa rabat in nal lazi ahya_ha_  lamuhyil mauta_ in nahu_ ala_ kul li sai in qadir
40.	In nal lazina yulhidu_na fi a_ya_tina_ la_ yakhfauna alaina_ afmay yulqa_ fin na_ri khairun am may yati a_minay yaumal qiya_mah imalu_ ma_ situm inahu_ bima_ tamalu_na basir
41.	In nal lazina kafaru_ biz zikri lama_ ja_ ahum wa in nahu_ lakita_bun aziz
42.	La_ yatihil ba_tilu mim baini yasaihi wa la_ min khalif tanzilum min hakimin hamid
43.	Ma_ yuqa_lu laka il la_ ma_ qad qila lir rusuli min qablik in na rab baka lazu_ magfiratiw wa zu_ iqa_bin alim
44.	Wa lau jaalna_hu qur a_nan ajamiy yal laqa_lu_ lau la_ fus silat a_ya_tuh a ajamiy a_manu_ hudaw wa sifa_ wal lazina la_ yuminu_na fi a_za_nihim waqruw wa huwa alaihim ama_ ula_ ika yuna_dauna mim maka_nin baid
45.	Wa laqad a_taina_ mu_sal kita_ba fakhtulifa fih wa lau la_ kalimatun sabaqat mir rab bika laqudiya bainahum wa in nahum lafi sak sim minhu murib
46.	Man amila sa_lihan falinafsihi wa man asa_ a fa'alaiha_ wa ma_ rab buka bi zal la_mil lil abid
47.	Ilaihi yurad du ilmus sa_ah wa ma_ takhruju min samara_tin min akma_miha wa ma_ tahmilu min unsa_ wa la_ tadau il la_ bi ilmih wa yauma yuna_dihim aina suraka_ I qa_lu_ a_zan na_ka ma_ min na_ min sahid
48.	Wa dal la anhum ma_ ka_nu_ yad u_na min qablu wa zan nu_ ma_ lahum mim mahis
49.	La_ yas amul insa_nu min dua_il khair wa im mas sahus sar ru fayau_sun qanu_th
50.	Wa la in adzaqna_hu rahmatam min na_ mim badi dar ra_ a mas sat hu layaqu_lan na ha_za_ li wa ma_ azhun nus sa_ ata qa_ imataw wa la ir rujitu ila_ rab bi in na li indahu_ lalhusna fa lanunab bi an nal lazina kafaru_ bima_ amilu_ wa lanuziqan nahum min aza_bin galiz
51.	Wa iza_ anamna_ alal insa_ni arada wa na a_ bija_nibih wa iza_ mas sahus sar ru fazu_ dua_in arid
52.	Qul ara aitum in ka_na min indil la_hi sum ma kafartum bihi man adhal lu mim man huwa fi siqa_qin baid
53.	Sanurihim a_ya_tina_ fil a_fa_qi wa fi anfusihim hat ta_ yatabay yana lahum an nahul haq awalam yakfi birab bika an nahu_ ala_ kul li sai in sahid
54.	Ala_ in nahum fi miryatim mil liqa_i rab bihim ala_ in nahu_ bikuli sai im muhit
.EndTopic
;___________________________________
.Topic qsAsy-Syura  " 42. Asy Syura"
1.	Ha_ mim
2.	Ain Sin Qa_f
3.	Kaza_lika yu_hi ilaika wa ilal lazina min qablikal la_hul azizul hakim
4.	Lahu_ ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ard wa huwal aliy yul azim
5.	Taka_dus sama_wa_ti yatafat tarnamin faiqihin na wal mala_ikatu yusab bihu_na bihamdi rab bihim wa yastagfiru_na liman fil ard ala_ inal la_ha huwal gafu_rur rahim
6.	Wal lazinat takazu_ min du_nihi auliya_ al la_hu hafizun alaihim wa ma_ anta alaihim biwakil
7.	Wa kaza_lika auhaina_ ilaika qur a_nan arabiy yal lituzira um mal qu ra_ wa man haulaha_ wa tunzira yaumal jami la_ raiba fih fariqun fil jan nati wa fariqun fis sair
8.	Wa lau sa_ al la_hu lajaalahum umataw wa_hidataw wa la_kiy yudkhilu may yasya_u fi rahmatih waz za_limu_na ma_ lahum miw waliy yiw wa la_ nasir
9.	Amit takazu_ min du_nihi auliya_ fal la_hu huwal waliy yu wa huwa yuhyil mauta_ wa huwa ala_ kul li sai in qadir
10.	Wa mak talaftum fihi min sai in fahukmuhu_ ilal la_h za_likumul la_hu rab bi alaihi tawak kaltu wa ilaihi unib
11.	Fa_tirus sama_wa_ti wal ard jaala lakum min anfusikum azwa_jaw wa minal ana_mi aswa_ja_ yazra ukum fih laisa kamitlihi sai uw wa huwas samiul basir
12.	Lahu_ maqa_lidus sama_wa_ti wal ard yabsutur rizqa limay yasya_u wa yaqdir in nahu_ bikul li sai in alim
13.	Sara'a lakum minad dini ma_ wasa_ bihi nu_haw wal lazi auhaina_ ilaika wa ma_ was saina_ bihi ibra_hima wa mu_sa_ wa isa_ an aqimud dina wa la_ tatafar raqu_ fih kabura alal musrikina ma tadu_hum ilaih al la_hu yajtabi ilaihi may yasya_u wa yahdi ilaihi may yunib
14.	Wa ma_ tafar raqu_ il la_ min badi ma_ ja_ ahumul ilmu bagyan bainahum wa lau la_ kalimatun sabaqat mir rab bika ila_ ajalim musam mal faqudiya bainahum wa in nal lazina u_ritsul kita_ba min badihim lati sakim imnu murib
15.	Fa liza_lika fadu wastaqim kama_ umirta wa la_ tat tabi ahwa_ ahum wa qul a_mantu bima_ anzalal la_hu min kita_b wa umirtu li adila bainakum al la_hu rab buna_ wa rab bukum lana_ ama_luna_ wa lakum ama_lukum la_ huj jata bainana_ wa bainakum al la_hu yajmau bainana_ wa ilaihil masir
16.	Wal lazina yuha_j ju_na fil la_hi mim badi mastujiba lahu_ huj jatuhum da_hidatun inda rab bihim wa alaihim gadabuw wa lahum aza_bun sadid
17.	Al la_hul lazi anzalal kita_ba bil haqi wal miza_n wa ma_ yudrika la'alas sa_ata qarib
18.	Yastajilu bihal lazina la_ yuminu_na biha_ wal lazina a_manu_ musfiqu_na minha_ wa yalamu_na an nahal haq ala_ in nal lazina yuma_ru_na fis sa_ati lafi sala_lin baid
19.	Al la_hu latifun biiba_dihi yarzuqu may yasya_ wa huwal qawiy yul aziz
20.	Man ka_na yuridu hartsal a_khirati nazid lahu_ fi hartsihi wa man ka_na yuridu harsad dun ya_ nutihi minha_ wa ma_ lahu_ fil a_khirati min nasib
21.	Am lahum suraka_ u sarau_ lahum minad dini ma_ lam yazan bihil la_hu wa lau la_ kalimatul fasli la qudiya bainahum wa in naz za_limina lahum aza_bun alim
22.	Taraz za_limina musfiqina mim ma_ kasabu_ wa huwa wa_qiun bihim wal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_lihati fi rauda_til jan na_t lahum ma_ yasya_ u_na inda rab bihim za_lika huwal fadul kabir
23.	Za_likal lazi yubas sirul la_hu iba_dahul lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_t qul la_ as alukum alihi ajran il lal mawad data fil qurba_ wa may yaqtarif hasanatan nazid lahu_ fiha_ hus na_ in nal la_ha gafu_run saku_r
24.	Am yaqu_lu_naf tara_ alal lahi kazina_ fa iy yasya il la_hu yaktim ala_ qalbik wa yamhul la_hul ba_tila wa yuhiq qul haq qa bikalima_tih in nahu_ alimu_n biza_tis sudu_r
25.	Wa huwal lazi yaqbalut taubata an iba_dihi wa yafu_ anis say yi a_ti wa yalamu ma_ tafalu_n
26.	Wa yastajibul lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti wa yaziduhum min fadlih wal ka_firu_na lahum aza_bun sadid
27.	Walau basatal la_hur razqa liiba_dihi labagau fil ardi wa la_kiy yunaz zilu biqadarim ma_ yasya_ in nahu_ bi iba_dihi kabirun basir
28.	Wa huwal lazi yunaz zilul gaitsa mim badi ma_ qanathu_ wa yansyuru rahmatah wa huwal waliy yul hamid
29.	Wa min a_ya_tihi halqus sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa ma_ bat sa fihima_ min da_b bah wa huwa ala_ jamihim iza_ yasya_ u qadir
30.	Wa ma_ asha_bakum mim musibatin fa bima_ kasabat aidikum wa yafu_ an katsi
31.	Wa ma_ antum bimujizina fil ardi wa ma_ lakum min du_nil la_hi miw waliy yiw wa la_ nasir
32.	Wamin a_ya_tihil jawa_ri fil bahri kal ala_m
33.	Iy yasya yuskinir riha fayazalna rawa_kida ala_ zahrir in na fi za_lika la a_ya_til likul li sab ba_rin saku_r
34.	Au yu_bigun na bima_ kasabu_ wa yafu an katsir
35.	Wa yalamal lazina yuja_dilu_na fi a_ya_tina_ ma_ lahum mim mahis
36.	Fama_ u_titum min sai in famata_ul haya_tid dun ya_ wa ma_ indal la_hi khairuw wa abqa_ lil lazina a_manu_ wa ala_ rab bihim yatawak kalu_n
37.	Wal lazina yajtanibu_na kaba_ iral ismi wal fawa_hisya wa iza_ ma_ gadibu_hum yagfiru_n
38.	Wal lazinas taja_bu_ lirab bihim wa aqa_mus sala_h wa amruhum su_ra_ bainahum wa mim ma_ razaqna_hum yunfiqu_n
39.	Wal lazina iza_ asha_bahumul bagyu hum yantasiru_n
40.	Wa jaza_u say yi atin say yi atum mitsluha_ faman afa_ wa aslaha fa ajruhu_ alal la_h in nahu_ la_ yuhib buz za_limin
41.	Wa lamanin tasara bada zulmihi fa ula_ ika ma_ alaihim min sabil
42.	In namas sabilu alal lazina yazlimu_nan na_sa wa yabgu_na fil ardi bigairil haq ula_ ika lahum aza_bun alim
43.	Wa laman sabara wa gafara in na za_lika lamin azmil umu_r
44.	Wa may yudlilil la_hu fama_ lahu_ miw waliy yim min badih wa taraz za_limina lam ma_ ra awul aza_ba yaqu_lu_na hal ila_ marad dim min sabil
45.	Wa tara_hum yuradu_na alaiha_ ha_siina minaz zul li yanzuru_na min tarfin hafiy wa qa_lal lazina a_manu_ in nal ka_sirinal lazina kasiru_ anfusahum wa ahlihim yaumal qiya_mah ala_ in naz za_limina fi aza_bim muqim
46.	Wa ma_ ka_na lahum min auliya_ a yansuru_nahum min du_nil la_h wa may yudlilil la_hu fama_ lahu_ min sabil
47.	Istajibu_ lirab bikum min qabli ay yatiya yaumul la_ marad da lahu_ minal la_h ma_ lakum mim malja iy yauma iziw wa ma_ lakum min nakir
48.	Fa in aradu_ fama_ arsalna_ka alaihim hafizan in alaika il lal bala_g wa in na_ iza_ adzaqnal insa_na min na_ rahmatan fariha biha_ wa in tusibum say yi atun bima_ qad damat aidihim fa in nal insa_na kafu_r
49.	Lil la_hi mulkus sama_wa_ti wal ard yakluqu ma_ yasya u yahabu limay yasya_u ina_tsaw wa yahabu limay yasya_ uz zuku_r
50.	Au yuzaw wijuhum zukra_naw wa ina_sa_ wa yajalu may yasya_ u aqima in nahu_ alimun qadir
51.	Wa ma_ ka_na libasarin ay yukal limahul la_hu wahyan au miw wara_i hija_bin au yursila rasu_lan fayu_hiya bi iznihi ma_ yasya_ inahu_ aliy yun hakim
52.	Wa kaza_lika auhaina_ ilaika ru_ham min amrina_ ma_ kunta tadri mal kita_bu wa lal ima_nu wa la_kin jaalna_hu nu_ran nahdi bihi man nasa_u min iba_dina_ wa in naka_ la tahdil ila_ sira_tim mustaqim
53.	Sira_til la_hil lazi lahu_ ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ard ala_ ilal la_hi tasirul umu_r
.EndTopic
;____________________________________
.Topic qsAz-Zukhruf  " 43. Az Zukhruf"
1.	Ha_ mim
2.	Wal kita_bil mubin
3.	In na_ ja'alna_hu qur a_nan arabiy yal la al lakum taqilu_n
4.	Wa in nahu_ fi um mil kita_bi ladaina_ la'aliy yun hakim
5.	Afanadribu ankumuz zikra safhan an kuntum qaumam musrifin
6.	Wa kam arsalna_ min nabiy yin fil aw walin
7.	Wa ma_ yatihim min nabiy yin il la_ ka_nu_ bihi yastahzi u_n
8.	Fa ahlakna_ asyad da minhum batsaw wa mada_ matsalul aw walin
9.	Wa la in sa altahum man halaqas sama_wa_ti wal arda layaqu_lun na halaqahun nal azizul alim
10.	Al lazi ja'ala lakumul arda mahdaw wa jaala lakum fiha_ subulal la al lakum tahtadu_n
11.	Wal lazi naz zala minas sama_i ma_ an biqadar fa ansarna_ bihi baldatam maita_ kaza_lika tukraju_n
12.	Wal lazi halaqal azwa_ja kul laha_ wa ja ala lakum minal fulki wal an a_mi ma_ tarkabu_n
13.	Litastawu_ ala_ zuhu_rihi sum ma tazkuru_ nimata rab bikum izas tawaitum alaihi wa taqu_lu_ subna_nal lazi sak kara lana_ ha_za_ wa man kun na_ lahu_ muqrinin
14.	Wa in na_ ila_ rab bina_ lamunqalibu_n
15.	Wa ja'alu_ lahu_ min iba_dihi juz a_ in nal insana_ lakafu_rum mubin
16.	Amit takaza mim ma_ yakluqu bana_tiw wa asfa_kum bil banin
17.	Wa iza bus sira ahaduhum bima_ daraba lir rahma_ni matsalan zal la wajuhu_ muswad daw wa huwa kazim
18.	Awa may yunas sa u fil hilyati wa huwa fil hisa_mi gairu mubin
19.	Wa ja'alul mala_ ikatal lazina hum iba_dur rahma_ni ina_tsa_ asyahidu_ halqahum satuktabu saha_datuhum wa yus alu_n
20.	Wa qa_lu_ lau sa_ ar rahma_nu ma_ abadna_hum ma_ lahum biza_lika min ilmin in hum il la_ yakrusu_n
21.	Am a_taina_hum kita_bam min qablihi fahum bihi mustamsiku_n
22.	Bal qa_lu_ in na_ wajadna_ a_ba_ ana_ ala_ um matiw wa in na_ ala_ a_tsa_rihim muhtadu_n
23.	Wa kaza_lika ma_ arsalna_ min qablika fi qaryatim min nazirin il la_ qa_la mutrafu_ha_ in na_ wa jadna_ a_ba_ ana_ ala_ um matiw wa in na_ ala_ a_tsa_rihim muqtadu_n
24.	Qa_la awalau jitukum bi ahda_ mim ma_ wajatum alihi a_ba_ akum qa_lu_ in na_ bima_ ursiltum bihi ka_firu_n
25.	Fantaqamna_ minhum fanzur kaifa ka_na a_qibatul mukaz zibin
26.	Wa iz qa_la ibra_himu li abihi wa qaumihi in nani bara_ um mim ma_ tabudu_n
27.	Il lal lazi fatarani fa in nahu_ sayahdin
28.	Wa jaalaha_ kalimatan ba_qiyatan fi aqibihi la al lahum yarjiu_n
29.	Bal mat tatu ha_ ula_i wa a_ba_ ahum hat ta_ ja_ ahumul haq qu wa rasu_lum mibin
30.	Wa lam ma_ ja_ ahumul haq qu qa_lu_ ha_za_ sihruw wa in na_ bihi ka_firu_n
31.	Wa qa_lu_ lau la_ nuz zila ha_zal qur a_nu ala_ rajulim minal qaryataini azim
32.	Ahum yaqsimu_na rahmata rab bika nahnu qasamna_ bainahum maisyatahum fil haya_tid dun ya_ wa rafana_ badahum fauqa badin daraja_til liyat takhiza baduhum badan sukriy ya_ wa rahmatu rab bika khairum mim ma_ yajmau_n
33.	Wa lau la_ ay yaku_nan na_su umataw wa_hidatal laja'alna_ limay yakfuru bir rahma_ni libuyu_tihim suqufam min fid datiw wa maa_rija alaiha_ yazharu_n
34.	Wa libuyu_tihim abwa_baw wa sururan alaiha_ yat taki u_n
35.	Wa zukrufa_ wa in kul lu za_lika lam ma_ mata_ul haya_tid dun ya_ wal a_khiratu inda rab bika lilmut taqin
36.	Wa may yasu an zikrir rahma_ni nuqay yid lahu_ saita_nan fahuwa lahu_ qarin
37.	Wa in nahum layasud du_nahum anis sabili wa yahsabu_na an nahum muhtadu_n
38.	Hat ta_ iza_ ja_ ana_ qa_la ya_laita baini wa bainaka budal masriqaini fabisal qarin
39.	Wa lay yanfakumul yauma iz zalamtum an nakum fil aza_bi mustariku_n
40.	Afa anta tusmius sum ma au tahdil umya wa man ka_na fi dala_lim mubin
41.	Fa im ma_ nazaban na bika fa in na_ minhum muntaqimu_n
42.	Au nuriyan nakal lazi wa adna_hum fa in na_ alaihim muqtadiru_n
43.	Fastamsik bil lazi u_hiya ilaik in naka ala_ sira_tim mustaqim
44.	Wa in nahu_ lazikrul laka wa laqaumika wa saufa tus alu_n
45.	Was al man arsalna_ min qablika mir rusulina_ aja'alna min du_nir rahma_ni a_lihatay yubadu_n
46.	Wa laqad arsalna_ mu_sa_ bi a_ya_tina_ ila_ firauna wamala_ ihi faqa_lain ni rasu_lu rab bil a_lamin
47.	Falam ma_ ja_ ahum bi a_ya_tina_ iza_ hum minha_ yadhaku_n
48.	Wa ma_ nurihim min a_yatin il la_ hiya akbaru min ukhtiha_ wa akhaz na_hum bil aza_bi la'al lahum yarjiu_n
49.	Wa qa_lu_ ya_ ay yuhas sa_hirudu lana_ rab baka bima_ ahida indak in nana_ lamuhtadu_n
50.	Falam ma_ kasyafna_ anhumul aza_ba iza_ hum yankutsu_n
51.	Wa na_da_ firaunu fi qaumihi qa_la ya_ qaumi alaisa li mulku misra wa ha_zihil anha_ru tajri min tahti afala_ tubsiru_n
52.	Am ana_khairum min ha_zal lazi huwa mahinuw wa la_ yaka_du yubin
53.	Falau la_ ulqiya alaihi aswiratum min zahabin au ja_ a ma'ahul mala_ikatu muqtarinin
54.	Fastakhaf fa qaumahu_ fa ata_u_h in nahum ka_nu_ qauman fa_siqin
55.	Falam ma_ a_safu_nan taqamna_ minhum fa agraqna_hum ajmain
56.	Faja'alna_hum salafaw wa matsalal lil a_khirina
57.	Wa lam ma_ duribabnu maryama matsalan iza_ qaumuka minhu yasidu_n
58.	Wa qa_lu_ a a_lihatuna_ khairun am hu ma_ darabu_hu laka il la_ jadala_ bal hum qaumun khasimu_n
59.	In huwa il la_ abdun an amna_ alaihi wa jaalna_hu matsalal libani isra_il
60.	Wa lau nasya_u lajaalna_ minkum mala_ikatan fil ardi yakhlufu_n
61.	Wa in nahu_ la ilmul lis sa_ati fala_ tamtarun na biha wat tabiu_n ha_za_ sira_tum mustaqim
62.	Wa la_ yasud dan nakumus saita_n in nahu_ lakum aduw wum mubin
63.	Wa lam ma_ ja_ aisa_ bil bay yina_ti qa_la qad jitukum bilhikmati wa li ubay yina lakum badal lazi taktalifu_na fih fat taqul la_ha wa atiu_n
64.	In nal la_ha huwa rab bi wa rab bukum fabudu_h ha_za_ sira_tum mustaqim
65.	Faktalafal ahza_bu min bainihim fa wailul lil lazina zalamu_ min aza_bi yaumin alim
66.	Hal yansuru_na il las sa_ata an tatiyahum bagtataw wa hum la_ yasuru_n
67.	Al akhil la_ u yauma izim baduhum libadin aduw wun il lal mutaqin
68.	Ya_ iba_di la_ kaufun alikumul yauma wa la_ antum tahzanu_n
69.	Al lazina a_manu_ bi a_ya_tina_ wa ka_nu_ muslimin
70.	Udkhulul jan nata antum wa azwa_jukum tuhbaru_n
71.	Yutha_fu alaihim bisiha_fim min zahabiw wa akwa_b wa fiha_ ma_ tastahihil anfusu wa talaz zul ayun wa antum fiha_ kha_lidu_n
72.	Wa tikal jan natul lati u_ritsumu_ha_ bima_ kuntum tamalu_n
73.	Lakum fiha_ fa_kihatun katsiratum minha_ takulu_n
74.	In nal mujrimina fi aza_bi jahanama kha_lidu_n
75.	La_ yufat taru anhum wa hum fihi mublisu_n
76.	Wa ma_ zalamna_hum wa la_kin ka_nu_ humuz za_limin
77.	Wa na_dau ya_ ma_liku liyaqdi alaina_ rab buk qa_la in nakum ma_kitsu_n
78.	Laqad jina_kum bil haq qi wa la_kina aksarakum lilhaq qi ka_rihu_n
79.	Am abramu_ amran fa in na_ mubrimu_n
80.	Am yahsabu_na an na_ la_ nasmau sir rahum wa najwa_hum bala_ wa rusuluna_ ladaihim yaktubu_n
81.	Qul in ka_na lir rahma_ni waladun fa ana aw walul a_bidin
82.	Subha_na rab bis sama_wa_ti wal ardi rab bil arsi am ma_ yasifun
83.	Fazarhum yakhu_du_ wa yal abu_ hat ta_ yula_qu_ yauma humul lazi yu_adu_n
84.	Wa huwal lazi fis sama_i ila_huw wa fil ardi ila_h wa huwal hakimul alim
85.	Wa taba_rakal lazi lahu_ mulkus sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa ma_ bainahuma_ wa indahu_ ilmus sa_ah wa ilaihi turjau_n
86.	Wa la_ yamlikul lazina yadu_na min du_nihis safa_ata il la_ man sahida bilhaq qi wa hum yalamu_n
87.	Wa la in sa altahum man khalaqahum layaqu_lun nal la_hu fa an na_ yufaku_n
88.	Wa qilihi ya_ rab bi in na ha_ ula_ I qaumul la_ yuminu_n
89.	Fasfah anhum wa qul sala_mun fa saufa yalamu_n
.EndTopic
;_____________________________________
.Topic qsAdDukhan  " 44. Ad Dukha_n"
1.	Ha_ mim
2.	Wal kita_bil mubin
3.	In na_ anzalna_hu fi lailatim muba_ rakatin in na_ kun na_ munzirin
4.	Fiha_ yufraqu kul lu amrin hakim
5.	Amram min indina_ in na_ kun na_ mursilin
6.	Rahmatam mir rab bik in nahu_ huwas samiul alim
7.	Rab bis sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa ma_ bainahuma_ in kuntum mu_qinin
8.	La_ ila_ha il la_ huwa yuhyil wa yumit rab bukum wa rab bu a_ba_i kumul aw walin
9.	Bal hum fi sak kiy yalabu_n
10.	Fartaqib yauma tatis sama_u bidu kha_nim mubin
11.	Yagsan na_s ha_za_ aza_bun alim
12.	Rab banaksif an nal aza_ba in na_ muminu_n
13.	An na_ lahumuz zakra_ wa qad ja_ ahum rasu_lum mubin
14.	Sum ma tawal lau anhu wa qa_lu_ mual lamum majnu_n
15.	In na_ ka_siful aza_bi qalilan in nakum a_ idu_n
16.	Yauma nabtisul batsatal kubra_ in na_ muntaqimu_n
17.	Wa laqad fatan na_ qablahum qauma firauna wa ja_ ahum rasu_lun karim
18.	An ad du_ ilay ya iba_dal la_h in ni lakum rasu_lun amin
19.	Wa al la_ talu_ alal la_h in ni a_tikum bisul ta_nim mubin
20.	Wa in ni uztu birab bi wa rab bikum an tarjumu_n
21.	Wa il lam tuminu_ lil fatazilu_n
22.	Fadaa_ rab bahu_ an na ha_ ula_ I qaumum mujrimu_n
23.	Fa asri biiba_dil lailan in nakum mut tabau_n
24.	Watrukil bahra rahwa_ in nahum jundum mugraqu_n
25.	Kam taraku_ min jan na_tiw wa uyu_n
26.	Wa zuru_iw wa maqa_min karim
27.	Wa namatin ka_nu_ fiha_ fa_kihin
28.	Kaza_lika wa auratsna_ha_ qauman a_kharin
29.	Fama_ bakat alaihimus sama_u wal ardu wa ma_ ka_nu_ munzarin
30.	Wa laqad naj jaina_ bani isra_ il minal aza_bil muhin
31.	Min firaun in nahu_ ka_na a_liyam minal musrifin
32.	Wa laqadih tarna_hum ala_ ilmin alal a_lamin
33.	Wa a_taina_hum minal a_ya_ti ma_ fihi bala_ um mubin
34.	In na ha_ ula_ I layaqu_lu_n
35.	In hiya il la_ mautatunal u_la_ wa ma_ nahnu bimunsarin
36.	Fatu_ bi a_ba_ ina_ in kuntum sa_diqin
37.	Ahum khairun am qaumu tub baiw wal lazina min qablihim ahlakna_hum in nahum ka_nu_ mujrimin
38.	Wa ma_ khalaqnas sama_wa_ti wal arda wa ma_ bainahuma_ la_ibin
39.	Ma_ khalaqna_huma_ il la_ bilhaq qi wa la_kin na_ aksarahum la_ yalamu_n
40.	In na yaumal fasli miqa_tuhum ajmain
41.	Yauma la_ yugni maulan am maulan sai aw wa la_ hum yunsaru_n
42.	Il la_ mar rahimal la_h in nahu_ huwal azizur rahim
43.	In na_ syajarataz zaq qu_m
44.	Taa_mul atsim
45.	Kal muhli yagi fi butu_n
46.	Kaghalyil hamim
47.	Khuzu_hu fatilu_hu ila_ sawa_ il jahim
48.	Sum ma sub bu_ fauqa rasihi min aza_bil hamim
49.	Zuq in naka antal azizul karim
50.	In naha_za_ ma_ kuntum bihi tamtaru_n
51.	In nal mut taqina fi maqa_min amin
52.	Fi jan na_tiw wa uyu_n
53.	Yalbasu_na min sundusiw wa istabraqim mutaqa_bilin
54.	Kaza_lika wa zaw wajna_hum bihu_rin in
55.	Yadu_na fiha_ bikul li fa_kihatin a_minin
56.	La_ yazu_qu_na fihal mauta il lal mautatal u_la_ wa waqa_hum aza_bal jahim
57.	Fadlam mir rab bik za_lika huwal fauzul azim
58.	Fa in nama_ yas sarna_hu bilisa_nika la'al lahum yatazak karu_n
59.	Fai taqib in nahum murtaqibu_n
.EndTopic
;____________________________________
.Topic qsAl-Jatsiyah  " 45. Al Jatsiyah"
1.	Ha_ mim
2.	Tan zilul kita_bi minal la_hil azizil hakim
3.	In na fis sama_wa_ti wal ardi la a_ya_til lilmuminin
4.	Wa fi khalqikum wa ma_ yabuts sumin da_b batin a_ya_tul liqaumiy yu_qinu_n
5.	Wakhtila_fil laili wan naha_ri wa ma_ anzalal la_hu minas sama_i mir rizqin fa ahya_ bihil arda bada mautiha_ wa tasrifir riya_hi a_ya_tul liqaumiy yaqilu_n
6.	Tilka a_ya_tul la_hi natlu_ha_ alaika bil haq qi fabi ay yi hadisim badal la_hi wa a_ya_tihi yuminu_n
7.	Wailul likul li af fa_kin asim
8.	Yasmau a_ya_til la_hi tutla_ alaihi sum ma yusir ru mustakbiran ka al lam yasmaha_ fabas sirhu biaza_bin alim
9.	Wa iza_ alima min a_ya_tina_ saianit takazaha_ huzuwa_ ula_ ika lahum aza_bum muhin
10.	Miw wara_ ihim jahan nam wa la_ yugni anhum ma_ kasabu_ sai aw wa la_ mat takazu_ min du_nil la_hi auliya_ wa lahum aza_bun azim
11.	Ha_za_ huda_ wal lazina kafaru_ bi a_ya_ti rab bihim lahum aza_bum mir rijzin alim
12.	Al la_hul lazi sak kara lakumul bahra litajriyal fulku fihi bi amrihi wa litabtagu_ min fadlihi wa la al lakum taskuru_n
13.	Wa sak kara lakum ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ardi jamiam min in na fi za_lika la a_ya_til liaqumiy yatafak karu_n
14.	Qul lil lazina a_manu_ yagfiru lil lazina la_ yarju_na ay ya_mal la_hi liyajziya qaumam bima_ ka_nu_ yaksibu_n
15.	Man amila sa_lihan falinafsih wa man asa_ a fa'alaiha_ sum ma ila_ rab bikum turjau_n
16.	Wa laqad a_taina_ bani isra_ ilal kita_ba wal hukma wan nubuw wata wa razaqna_hum minat tay yiba_ti wa fad dalna_hum alal a_lamin
17.	Wa a_taina_hum bay yina_tim minal amr famaktalafu_ il la_ mim badi ma_ ja_ a humul ilmu bagyan bainahum in na rab baka yaqdi bainahum yaumal qiya_mati fima_ ka_nu_ fihi yakhtalifu_n
18.	Sum ma jaalna_ka ala_ sari atim minal amri fat tabiha_ wa la_ tat tabiahwa_ al lazina la_ yalamu_n
19.	In nahum lay yugnu_ anka minal la_hi sai a_ wa in naz za_limina baduhum auliya_ u badiw wal la_hu waliy yul mut taqin
20.	Ha_za_ basa_ iru lin na_si wa hudaw wa rahmatul liqaumiy yu_qinu_n
21.	Am hasibal lazinaj tarahus say yi a_ti an naj alahum kal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti sawa_ am mahya_hum wa mama_tuhum sa_ a ma_ yahkumu_n
22.	Wa khalaqal la_hus sama_wa_ti wal arda bil haq qi wa litujza_ kul lu nafsin bima_ kasabat wa hum la_ yuzlamu_n
23.	Afara aita manit takaza ila_hahu_ hawa_hu wa adal lahul la_hu ala_ ilmiw wa khatama ala_ samiihi wa qalbihi wa ja'ala ala_ basarihi gisa_wah famay yahdihi min nadil la_h afala_ tazak karu_n
24.	Wa qa_lu_ ma_ hiya il la_ haya_tunad dun ya_ namu_tu wa nahya_ wa ma_ yuhlikuna_ il lad dah wa ma_ lahum biza_lika min ilmin in hum il la_ yahzun nu_n
25.	Wa iza_ tutla_ alaihim a_ya_tuna_ bay yina_tim ma_ ka_na huj jatahum il la_ an qa_lu tu_ bi a_ba_ ina_ in kuntum sa_diqin
26.	Qulil la_hu yuhyikum sum ma yumitukum sum ma yajmaukum ila_ yaumil qiya_matil la_ raiba fihi wa la_kin na aksaran na_si la_ yalamu_n
27.	Wa lil la_hi mulkus sama_wa_ti wal ard wa yauma taqu_mus sa_atu yaumaiziy yakhsarul mubtilu_n
28.	Wa tara_ kul la um matin ja_tsiyah kul lu um matin tud da_ ila_ kita_biha_ alyauma tujzauna ma_ kuntum tamalu_n
29.	Ha_za_ kita_buna_ yantiqu alaikum bil haq in na_ kun na_ nastansiku ma_ kuntum tamalu_n
30.	Fa am mal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti fayudkiluhum rab buhum fi rahmatih za_lika huwal fauzul mubin
31.	Wa am mal lazina kafaru_ afalam takun a_ya_ti tutla_ alaikum fastak bartum wa kuntum qaumam mujrimin
32.	Wa iza_ qila in na wadal la_hi haquw was sa_atu la_ raiba fiha_ qultum ma_ nadri mas sa_atu in nazun nu il la_ zan naw wa ma_ nahnu bimustaiqinin
33.	Wa bada_ lahum say yi a_tu ma_ amilu_ wa ha_qa bihim ma_ ka_nu bihi yastahzi u_n
34.	Wa qilal yauma nansa_kum kama_ nasitum liqa_ a yaumikun ha_za_ wa mawa_kumun na_ru wa ma_ lakum min na_sirin
35.	Za_likum bi an nakumut takhaztum a_ya_til la_hi huzuwaw wa gar ratkumul haya_tud dun ya_ fal yauma la_ yukhraju_na minha_ wa la_ hum yustatabu_n
36.	Falil la_hil hamdu rab bis sama_wa_ti wa rab bil ardi rab bil a_lamin
37.	Wa lahul kibriya_ u fis sama_wa_ti wal ardi wahuwal azizul hakim
.EndTopic
;___________________________________
.Topic qsAl-Ahqa_f  " 46. Al Ahqa_f"
1.	Ha_ mim
2.	Tanzilul kita_bi minal la_hil azizil hakim
3.	Ma_ halaqnas sama_wa_ti wal arda wa ma_ bainahuma_ il la_ bil haq qi wa ajalim musam ma_ wal lazina kafaru_ am ma_ unziru_ muridu_n
4.	Qul ara aitum ma_ tadu_na min du_nil la_hi aru_ni ma_za_ halaqu_ minal ardi am lahum sirkun fis sama_wa_ti lu_ni bikita_bim min qabli ha_za_ au atsa_ratim min ilmin in kuntum sa_diqin
5.	Wa man adhal lu mim may yadu_ min du_nil la_hi mal la_ yastajibu lahu_ ila_ yaumil qiya_mati wa hum an du a_ ihim ga_filu_n
6.	Wa iza_ husyiran na_su ka_nu_ lahum ada_ aw wa ka_nu_ biiba_datihim ka_firin
7.	Wa iza_ tutla_ alaihim a_ya_tuna_ bay yina_tin qa_lal lazina kafaru_ lilhaq qi lam ma_ ja_ ahum ha_za_ sihrum mubin
8.	Am yaqu_lu_naf tara_h qul inif taraituhu_ fala_ tamiku_na li minal la_hi sai a_ huwa alamu bima_ tufidu_na fih kafa_ bihi sahidan bainu wa bainakum wa huwal gafu_rur rahim
9.	Qul ma_ kuntu bidam minar rusuli wa ma_ adri ma_ yufalu bi wa la_ bikum in at tabiu il la_ ma_ yu_ha_ ilay ya wa ma_ ana il la_ nazirum mubin
10.	Qul ara aitum in ka_na min indil la_hi wa kafartum bihi wa sahida sa_hidum min bani isra_ila ala_ mitslihi fa a_mana wastakbartum in nal la_ha la_yahdil qaumaz za_linin
11.	Wa qa_lal lazina kafaru_ lil lazina a_manu_ lau ka_na kairam ma_ sabaqu_na ilaih wa iz lam yahtadu_ bihi fayaqu_lu_na ha_za_ ifkun qadim
12.	Wa min qablihi kita_bu mu_sa_ ima_maw wa rahmah wa ha_za_ kita_bum mushad diqul lisa_nan arabiy yal liyunziral lazina zalamu_ wa busra_ lilmuhsinin
13.	In nal lazina qa_lu_ rab bunal la_hu sum mas taqa_mu_ fala_ kaufun alaihim wa la_ hum yahzanu_n
14.	Ula_ika asha_bul jan nati ha_lidina fiha_ jaza_an bima_ ka_nu_ yamalu_n
15.	Wa was sainal insa_na biwa_lidaihi ihsa_na_ hamalat hu um muhu_ kurhaw wa wadaathu kurha_ wa hamluhu_ wa fisa_luhu sala_su_na sahra_ hat ta_ iza_ balaga asyudahu_ wa balaga arbaina sanatan qa_la rab bi auzini an askura nimatakal lati anamta alay ya wa ala_ wa_liday ya wa an amala sa_lihan tarda_hu wa aslih li fi zur riy yati in ni tubtu ilaika wa in ni minal muslimin
16.	Ula_ ikal lazina nataqab balu anhum ahsana ma_ amilu_ wa nataja_wazu an say yi a_tihim fi asha_bil jan nah wadas sidqil lazi ka_nu_ yu_adu_n
17.	Wal lazi qa_la liwa_lidaihi uf fil lakuma_ ataida_nini an uhraja wa qad halatil quru_nu min qabli wa huma_ yastagnitsa_nil la_ha wailaka a_min in na wadal la_hi haq qun fayaqu_lu ma_ ha_za_ il la_ asa_tirul aw walin
18.	Ula_ ikal lazina haq qa alaihimul qaulu fi umamin qad halat min qablihim minal jin ni wal ins in nahum ka_nu_ ha_sirin
19.	Wa likul lin daraja_tum mim ma_ amilu_ wa liyuwaf fiyahum ama_lahum wa hum la_ yuzlamu_n
20.	Wa yauma yuradul lazina kafaru_ alan na_ri az habtum tay yiba_tikum fi haya_tikumud dun ya_ wastamtatum biha_ fal yauma tujzauna aza_bal hu_ni bima_ kuntum tastak biru_na fil ardi bigairil haq qi wa bima_ kuntum tafsuqu_n
21.	Wazkur akha_ a_d iz anzara qau mahu_ bil ahqa_fi wa qad halatin nuzuru min baini yadaihi wa min halfihi al la_ tabudu_ ilal la_h in ni akha_fu  alaikum aza_ba yaumin azim
22.	Qa_lu_ ajitana_ litafikana_ an a_lihatina_ fatina_ bima_ taiduna_ in kunta minas sa_diqin
23.	Qa_la in namal ilmu indal la_hi wa ubal ligukum ma_ ursiltu bihi wa la_kin ni ara_kum qauman tajhalu_n
24.	Falam ma_ ra auhu aridam mustaqbila audiyatihim qa_lu_ ha_za_ a_ridum mumtiruna_ hal huwa mastajaltum bihi rihun fiha_ aza_bun alim
25.	Tudam miru kul la sai in ni amri ra biha_ fa asbahu_ la_ yura_ il la_ masa_kinuhum kaza_lika najzil qaumal mujrimin
26.	Wa laqad mak kan na_hum fima im mak kan na_kum fihi wa ja'alna_ lahum samaw wa absa_raw wa af idah fama_ agna_ anhum samuhum wa la_ absa_ruhum wa la_ af idatuhum min sai in iz ka_nu_ yajhadu_na bi a_ya_til la_hi wa ha_qa bihim ma_ ka_nu_ bihi yastahziu_n
27.	Wa laqad ahlakna_ ma_ haulakum minal qura_ wa sar rafnal a_ya_til la alahum yarjiu_n
28.	Falaula_ nasarahumul lazinat takhazu_ min du_nil la_hi qurba_nan a_lihah bal dal lu_ anhum wa za_lika ifkuhum wa ma_ ka_nu_ yaftaru_n
29.	Wa iz zarafna_ ilaika nafaram minal jin ni yastamiu_nal qur a_n falam ma_ hadaru_hu qa_lu_ ansitu_ falam ma_ qudiya wal lau ila_ qaimihim munzirin
30.	Qa_lu_ ya_ qaumana_ in na_ samina_ kita_ban unzila min badi mu_sa_ mushad diqal lima_ baina yadaihi yahdi ilal haq qi wa ila_ tariqim mustaqim
31.	Ya_ qaumana_ ajibu_ da_iyal la_hi wa a_minu_ bihi yagfir lakum min zunu_bikum wa yujirkum min aza_ bin alim
32.	Wa mal la_ yujib da_ iyal la_hi falaisa bimujizin fil ardi wa laisa lahu_ min du_nihi auliya_ uka_ika fi dala_lim mubin
33.	Awalam yarau an nal la_hal lazi halaqas sama_wa_ti wal arda wa lam yaya bikalqihin na biqa_dirin ala_ ay yuhyiyal mauta_ bala_ in nahu_ ala_ kul li sai in qadir
34.	Wa yauma yuradul lazina kafaru_ alan na_r alaisa ha_za_ bil haq qa_lu_ bala_ wa rab bina_ qa_la fazu_qul aza_ba_ bima_ kuntum takfuru_n
35.	Fasbir kama_ sabara ulul azmi minar rusuli wa la_ tasta jil lahum ka an nahum yauma yarauna ma_ yu_adu_na lam yalbatsu_ il la_ sa_atam min naha_r bala_gun fahal yuhlaku il lal qaumul fa_siqu_n
.EndTopic
;______________________________________
.Topic qsMuhammad  " 47. Muhammad"
1. 	Al lazina kafaru_ wa sad du_ an sabilil la_hi adhal la ama_lahum
2. 	Wal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti wa a_manu_ bima_ nuzila ala_ muham madiw wa huwal haq qu mir rab bihim kaf fara anhum say yi a_tihim wa aslaha ba_lahum
3. 	Za_lika bi an nal lazina kafarut ta baul ba_tila wa an nal lazina a_manut tabaul haq qa mir rab bihim kaza_lika yadribul la_hu lin na_si amsa_lahum
4. 	Fa iza_ laqitumul lazina kafaru_ fadarbar riqa_b hat ta_ iza_ atskantumu_hum fasyud dul watsa_qa fa im ma_ man nan badu wa im ma_ fida_ an hat ta_ tadaal harbu auza_ raha_ za_lik wa lau yasya_ ul la_hu lan tashara minhum wa la_kil liyabluwa badakum bibadh wal lazina qutilu_ fi sabililla_hi falay yudil la ama_lahum
5. 	Sayahdihim wa yuslihu ba_lahum
6. 	Wa yudhiluhumul jan nata ar rafaha_ lahum
7. 	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ in tansurul la_ha yansurkum wa yutsab bit aqda_makum
8. 	Wal lazina kafaru_ fatasal lahum wa adhal la ama_lahum
9. 	Za_lika bi an nahum karihu_ ma_anzalal la_hu fa_hbata ama_lahum
10.	Afalam yasiru fil ardi fayanzuru_ kaifa ka_na a_qibatul lazina min qablihim dam maral la_hu alaihim wa lilka_firina amsa_luha_
11.	Za_lika bi an nal la_ha maulal lazina a_manu_ wa an nal ka_firina la_ maula_ lahum
12.	In nal la_ha yudhilul lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti jan na_tin tajri min tahtihal anha_r wal lazina kafaru_ yatamat tau_na wa yakulu_na kama_ takulul ana_mu wan na_ru matswal lahum
13.	Wa ka ay yim min qaryatin hiya asyadu quw watam min qaryatikal lati akhrajatka ahlakna_hum fala_ na_sira lahum
14.	Afaman ka_na ala_ bay yinatim mir rab bihi kaman zuy yina lahu_ su_u amalihi wat tabau_ ahwa_ ahum
15.	Matsalul jan natil lati wuidal mut taqu_n fiha_ anha_rum mim ma_in gairi a_sin wa anha_rum mil labanil lam yatagay yar tamuhu_ wa anha_rum min kamril laz zatil lis sa_ribin wa anha_rum min asalim mushaf fa_ wa lahum fiha_ min kulits samara_ti wa magfiratum mir rab bihim kaman huwakha_lidun fin na_ri wa suqu_ ma_ an hamiman faqat ta'a am a_ ahum
16.	Wa minhum may yastamiu ilaik hat ta_ iza_ haraju_ min indika qa_lu_ lil lazina u_tul ilma ma_za_ qa_la a_nifa_ ula_ikal lazina tabaal la_hu ala_ qulu_bihim wat tabau_ ahwa_ ahum
17.	Wal lazina tadau za_dahum hudaw wa a_ta_hum taqwa_hum
18.	Fahal yanzuru_na il las sa_ata an tatiyahum bagtatan faqad ja_a asra_tuha_ fa an na_ lahum iza_ ja_athum zikra_hum
19.	Falam an nahu_ la_ ila_ha il lal la_hu wastagfir lizan bika wa lil muminina wal mumina_t wal la_hu yalamu mutaqal labakum wa matswa_kum
20.	Wa yaqu_lul lazina a_manu_ laula_ nuz zilat su_rah fa iza_ unzilat su_ratum muhkamatuw wa zukira fihal qita_lu ra aital lazina fi qulu_bihim maraduy yanzuru_na ilaika nazaral magsiy yi alaihi minal maut fa au la_ lahum
21.	Ta_atuw wa qaulum maru_fun fa iza_ azamal amru falau sadaqul la_ha laka_na hairal lahum
22.	Fahal asaitum in tawal laitum an tufsidu_ fil ardi wa tuqath tiu_ arha_makum
23.	Ula_ikal lazina laanahumul la_hu fa asham mahum wa ama_ absa_rahum
24.	Afala_ yatadab baru_nal qur a_na am ala_ qulu_bin aqfa_luha_
25.	In nal lazinar tad du_ ala_ adba_rihim min badi ma_ tabay yana lahumul hudas saita_nu saw wala lahum wa amla_ lahum
26.	Za_lika bi an nahum qa_lu_ lil lazina kahiru_ ma_ naz zalal la_hu sabutiukum fi badil amri wal la_hu yalamu isra_rahum
27.	Fakaifa iza_ tawaf fat humul mala_ikatu yadribu_na wuju_hahum wa adba_rahum
28.	Za_lika bi an nahumut tabau_ ma_ askatal la_ha wa karihu_ ridwa_nahu_ fa ahbata ama_lahum
29.	Am hasibal lazina fi qulu_bihim maradun al lay yukrijal la_hu adga_nahum
30.	Wa lau nasya_u la araina_kahum falaaraftahum bisima_hum wa latarifan nahum fi lahnil qaul wal la_hu yalamu ama_lakum
31.	Wa lanabluwan nakum hat ta_ nalamal muja_hidina minkum was sa_binina wa nabluwa akba_rakum
32.	In nal lazina kafaru_ wa sad du_ an sabilil la_hi wa sa_q qur rasu_la min badi ma_ tabay yana lahumul huda_ lay yadur rul la_ha sai a_ wa sayuhbitu ama_lahum
33.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ atiul la_ha wa atiur rasu_la wa la_ tubtilu_ ama_lakum
34.	In nal lazina kafaru_ wa sad du_an sabilil la_hi sum ma ma_tu_ wa hum kuf fa_run falay yagfiral la_hu lahum
35.	Fala_ tahinu_ wa tadu_ ilas salmi wa antumul alauna wal la_hu maakum wa lay yatirakum ama_lakum
36.	In namal haya_tud dun ya_ laibuw wa lahw wa in tuminu_ wa tat taqu_ yutikum uju_rakum wa la_ yas alkum amwa_lakum
37.	Iy yas alkumu_ha_ fayuhfikum tabkhalu_ wa yukhrij adga_nakum
38.	Ha_ antum ha_ ula_i tadauna litunfiqu_ fi sabilil la_h fa minkum may yabkhalu wa may yabkhal fa in nama_ yabkhalu an nafsih wal la_hul ganiyu wa antumul fuqara_u wa in yastabdil qauman gairakum suma la_ yaku_nu_amsa_lakum
.Endtopic
;______________________________
.Topic qsAl-Fath  " 48. Al Fath"
1.	In na_ fatahna_ laka fat ham mubina_
2.	Liyagfira lakal la_hu ma_ taqad dama min zanbika wa ma_ ta ak kara wa yutim ma nimatahu_ alaika wa yahdiyaka sira_tam mustaqima_
3.	Wa yansurakal la_hu nasran aziza_
4.	Huwal lazi anzalas sakinata fi qulu_bil muminina liyazda_du_ ima_nam maa ima_nihim wa lil la_hi junu_dus sama_wa_ti wal ard wa ka_nal la_hu aliman hakima_
5.	Liyudhilal muminina wal mumina_ti jan na_tin tajri min tahtihal anha_ru ha_lidina fiha_ wa yukaf fira anhum say yi a_tihim wa ka_na za_lika indal la_hi fauzan azhima_
6.	Wa yuaz zibal muna_fiqina wal muna_fiqa_ti wal musrikina wal musrika_tiz za_n nina bil la_hi zan nas sau-i alaihim da_iratus sau-i wa gadibal la_hu alaihim wa laanahum wa a'ad da lahum jahan nam wa sa_at masira_
7.	Wa lil la_hi junu_dus sama_wa_ti wal ard wa ka_nal la_hu azizan hakima_
8.	In na_ arsalna_ka sa_hidaw wa mubas siraw wa nazira_
9.	Lituminu_ bil la_hi wa rasu_lihi wa tuaz ziru_hu wa tuwaq qiru_h wa tusab bihu_hu bukrataw wa asila_
10.	In nal lazina yuba_yiu_naka in na ma_ yuba_yiu_nal la_h yadul la_hi fauqa aidihim faman nakatsa fa in nama_ yankutsu ala_ nafsihi wa man aufa_ bima_ a_hada alaihul la_ha fasayutihi ajran azima_
11.	Sayaqu_lu lakal mukhal lafu_na minal ara_bi sagalatna_ amwa_luna_ wa ahlu_na_ fastagfir lana_ yaqu_lu_na bi alsinatihim ma_ laisa fi qulu_bihim qul famay yamliku lakum minal la_hi sai an in ara_da bikum dar ran au ara_da bikum nafa_ bal ka_nal la_hu bima_ tamalu_na khabira_
12.	Bal zanantum al lay yanqalibar rasu_lu wal muminu_na ila_ ahlihim abadaw wa zuy yina za_lika fi qulu_bikum wa zanantum zan nas sau-i wa kuntum qauman bu_ra_
13.	Wa mal lam yumin bil la_hi wa rasu_lihi fa in na_ atadna_ lilka_firina saira_
14.	Wa lil la_hi mulkus sama_wa_ti wal ard yahgfiru limay yasya_u wa yuaz zibu may yasya_ wa ka_nal la_hu gafu_rar rahima_
15.	Sayaqu_lu mukal lafu_na izan talaqtum ila_ maga_nima litakuzu_ ha_ zaru_na_ nat tabikum yuridu_na ay yubad dilu_ kala_mal la_h qulan tat tabiu_na_ kaza_likum qa_lal la_hu min qablu fasayaqu_lu_na bal tahsu_dunana_ bal ka_nu_ la_ yafqahu_na il la_ qalila_
16.	Qul lilmukal lafina minal ara_bi satudauna ila_ qaumin uli basin sadidin tuqa_tilu_nahum au yuslimu_n fa in tutiu_ yutikumul la_hu ajran hasana_ wa in tatawal lau kama_ tawal laitum min qablu yuaz zibkum aza_ban alima_
17.	Laisa alal ama_ harajuw wa la_ alal araji harajuw wa la_ alal maridi haraj wa may yutiil la_ha wa rasu_lahu_ yudkhilhu jan na_tin tajri min tahtihal anha_r wa may yatawal la yuaz zibu aza_ban alima_
18.	Laqad radiyal la_hu anil muminina iz yuba_yiu_naka tahtas sajarati fa'alima ma_ fi qulu_bihim fa anzalas sakinata alaihim wa atsa_bahum fat han qariba_
19.	Wa magha_nima katsiratay yakhuzu_naha_ wa ka_nal la_hu azizan hakima_
20.	Wa adakumul la_hu magha_nima katsiratan takhuzu_naha_ fa'aj jala lakum ha_zihi wa kaf fa aidiyan na_si ankum wa li taku_na a_ya_tal lilmuminina wa yahdiyakum sira_tam mustaqima_
21.	Wa ukhra_ lam taqdiru_ alaiha_ qad aha_tal la_hu biha_ wa ka_nal la_hu ala_ kuli sai in qadira_
22.	Wa lau qa_talakumul lazina kafaru_ lawal lawul adba_ra sum ma la_ yajidu_na waliy yaw wa la_ nasira_
23.	Sun natal la_hil lati qad khalat min qablu wa lan tajida lisun natil la_hi tabdila_
24.	Wa huwal lazi kaf fa aidiyahum ankum wa aidiyakum anhum bibatnikmak kata min badi an azfarakum alaihim wa ka_nal la_hu bima_ tamalu_na basira_
25.	Humul lazina kafaru_ wa sad du_kum anil masjidil hara_mi wal had ya maku_fan ay yabluga mahil lah wa laula_ rija_lum muminu_na wa nisa_um mumina_tul lam talamu_hum an tata u_hum fatusibakum minhum maar ratun bigairi ilm liyudhilal la_hu fi rahmatihi may yasya_-u lau tazay yalu_ la'az zabnal lazina kafaru_ minhum aza_ban alima_
26.	Iz ja'alal lazina kafaru_ fi qulubihimul hamiy yata hamiy yatal ja_hiliy yati fa anzalal la_hu sakinatahu_ ala_ rasu_lihi wa alal muminina wa alzamahum kalimatat taqwa_ wa ka_nu_ ahaq qa biha_ wa ahlaha_ wa ka_nal la_hu bikuli sai in alima_
27.	Laqad sadaqal la_hu rasu_lahur ruya_ bil haq la tadkhulan nal masjidal hara_ma in sa_ al la_hu a_minina muhal liqina ruu_sakum wa muqash sirina la_ takha_fu_n fa'alima ma_ lam talamu_ fajaala min du_ni za_lika fat hanqariba_
28.	Huwal lazi arsala rasu_lahu_ bil huda_ wa dinil haq qi liyuzhirahu_ alad dini kul lih wa kafa_ bil la_hi sahida_
29.	Muham madur rasu_lul la_h wal lazina maahu_ asyid da_u alal kuf fa_ri ruhama_u bainahum tara_hum ruk kaan suj jaday yabtagu_na fadlam minal la_hi wa ridwa_na_ sima_hum fi wuju_hihim min atsaris suju_d za_lika matsaluhum fit taura_ti wa matsaluhum fi injil jkazarin akhraja satahu_ fa a_zarahu_ fastaglaza fastawa_ ala_ su_qihi yujibuz zur ra_a liyagiza_ bihimul kuf fa_r waadal la_hul lazina a_manu_ wa amilush sa_liha_ti minhum magfirataw wa ajran azima_
.EndTopic
;___________________________________
.Topic qsAl-Hujarat  " 49. Al Hujurat"
1.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ la_ tuqad dimu_ baina yadayil la_hi wa rasu_lihi wat taqul la_h in nal la_ha samiun alim
2.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ la_ tarfau_ aswa_takum fauqa sautin nabiy yi wa la_ tajharu_ lahu_ bil qauli kajahri badikum libadin an tahbata ama_lukum wa antum la_ tasuru_n
3.	In nal lazina yaghud du_na aswa_tahum inda rasu_lil la_hi ula_ ikal lazinam tahanal la_hu qulu_bahum lit taqwa_ lahum magfiratuw wa ajrun azim
4.	In nal lazina yuna_du_naka miw wa ra_il hujura_ti aksaruhum la_ yaqilu_n
5.	Wa lau an nahum sabaru_ hat ta_ takhruja ilaihim laka_na khairal lahum wal la_hu gafu_rur rahim
6.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ in ja_akum fa_siqun binaba in fatabay yanu_ an tusibu_ qauman bijaha_latin fatusbihu_ ala_ ma_ faaltum na_dimin
7.	Wa lamu_ an na fikum rasu_lal la_h lau yu tiukum fi katsirim minal amri laanit tum wa la_kin nal la_ha hab baba ilaikumul ima_na wa zay yanahu_ fi qulu_bikum wa kar raha ilaikumul kufra wal fusu_qa walisya_n ula_ika humur ra_sidu_n
8.	Fadlam minal la_hi wa nimah wal la_hu alimun hakim
9.	Wa in ta_ifata_ni minal mumininaq tatalu_ fa aslihu_ bainahuma_ fa in bagat ihda_huma_ alal ukhra_ faqa_tilul lati tabgi hat ta_ tafi a ila_ amril la_h fa in fa_ at fa aslihu_ bainahuma_ bi adli wa aqsitu_ in nal la_ha yuhib bul muqsitin
10.	In namal muminu_na ikhwatun fa aslihu_ baina akhawaikum wat taqul la_ha la'al lakum turhamu_n
11.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ la_ yaskhar qaumum min qaumin asa_ ay yaku_nu_ khairam minhum wa la_ nisa_ um min nisa_in asa_ ay yakun na khairam minhun na wa la_ talmizu_ anfusakum wa la_ tana_bazu_ bil alqa_b bisal ismul fusu_qu badal ima_ni wa mal lam yatub fa ula_ ika humuz za_limu_n
12.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manuj tanibu_ katsiram minaz zan ni in na badaz zan ni itmuw wa la_ tajasasu_ wa la yagtab badukum bada_ ayuhib bu ahadukum ay yakula lahma akhihi maitan fakarihtumu_h wal taqul la_h in nal la_ha taw wa_bur rahim
13.	Ya_ ay yuhal na_su in na_ halaqna_kum min zakariw wa unsa_ wa ja'alna_kum suu_baw wa qaba_ ila litaa_rafu_ in na akramakum indal la_hi atqa_kum in nal la_ha alimun kabir
14.	Qa_ latil arabu a_man na_ qul lam tuminu_ wa la_kin qu_lu_ aslamna_ wa lam ma_ yadkulil ilma_nu fi qulu_bikum wa in tutiul la_ha wa rasu_lahu_ la_ yalitkum min ama_likum syar a_ in nal la_ha gafu_rur rahim
15.	In namal muminu_nal lazina a_manu_ bil la_hi wa rasu_lihi sum ma lam yarta_bu_ wa ja_hadu_ bi amwa_lihim wa anfusihim fi sabil la_h ula_ika humus sa_diqu_n
16.	Qul atual limu_nal la_ha bidinikum wal la_hu yalamu ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ard wal la_hu bikul li sai in alim
17.	Yamun nu_na alaika an aslamu_ qul la_ tamun nu_ alay ya isla_makum balil la_hu yamun nu alaikum an hada_kum lil ima_ni in kuntum sa_diqin
18.	In na la_ha yalamu gaibas sama_wa_ti wal ard wal la_hu basirun bima_ tamalu_n
.EndTopic
;________________________
.Topic qsQa_f  " 50. Qa_f"
1.	Qa_f wal qur a_nil majid
2.	Bal ajbu_ an ja_ ahum munzirum minhum faqa_lal ka_firu_na ha_za_ sai un ajib
3.	A iza_ mitna_ wa kun na_ tura_ban za_lika rajun baid
4.	Qad alimna_ ma_ tanqusul ardu minhum wa indana_ kita_bun hafiz
5.	Bal kaz zabu_ bil haq qi lam ma_ ja_ ahum fahum fi amrim marij
6.	Afalam yanzuru_ ilas sama_i fauqahum kaifa banaina_ha_ wa zay yana_ha_ wa ma_ laha_ min furu_j
7.	Wal arda madadna_ha_ wa alqaina_ fiha_ rawa_siya wa an batna_ fiha_ min kul li zaujin bahij
8.	Tabsirataw wa zikra_ likul li abdim munib
9.	Wa naz zalna_ minas sama_i ma_ am muba_rakan fa an batna_ bihi jan na_tiw wa hab bal hasid
10.	Wan nakhla ba_siqa_til laha_ talun nadid
11.	Rizqal lil iba_d wa ahyaina_ bihi bal datam maita_ kaza_likal khuru_j
12.	Kaz zabat qablahum qaumu nu_hiw wa asha_bur rasi wa samu_d
13.	Wa a_duw wa firauna wa ikhwa_nu lu_t
14.	Wa asha_bul aikati wa qaumu tub bain kul lun kaz zabar rusula fahaq qawaid
15.	Afa'ayina_ bil halqil aw wal bal hum fi labsim min halqin jadid
16.	Wa laqad halaqnal insa_na wa nalamu ma_ tuwaswisu bihi nafsuhu_ wa nahnu aqrabu ilaihi min hablil warid
17.	Iz yatalaq qal mutalaq qiya_ni anil yamini wa anis sima_li qaid
18.	Ma_ yalfizu min qaulin il la_ ladaihi raqibun atid
19.	Wa ja_ at sakratul mauti bil haq za_lika ma_ kunta minhu tahid
20.	Wa nufika fis su_r za_lika yaumul waid
21.	Wa ja_ at kul lu nafsim maaha_ sa_ I quw wa sahid
22.	Laqad kunta fi gaflatim min ha_za_ fakasyafna_ anka gita_ aka fabasarukal yauma hadid
23.	Wa qa_la qarinuhu_ ha_za_ ma_ laday yaatid
24.	Alqiya_ fi jahan nama kul la kaf fa_rin anid
25.	Man na_il lilkhairi mutadim murib
26.	Al lazi ja'ala maal la_hi ila_han a_khara fa alqiya_hu fil aza_bis sadid
27.	Qa_la qarinuhu_ rab bana_ ma_ atgaituhu_ wa la_kin ka_na fi dala_lin baid
28.	Qa_la la_ taktasimu_ laday ya waqad qad damtu ilaikum bil waid
29.	Ma_ yubad dalul qaulu laday ya wa ma_ ana bizal la_mil lil abid
30.	Yauma naqu_lu lijahan nama halim talati wa taqu_lu hal mim mazud
31.	Wa uzlifatil jan natu lilmut taqina gaira baid
32.	Ha_za_ ma_ tu_adu_na likul li awa_bin hafiz
33.	Man khasyiyar rahma_na bil gaibi wa ja_ a biqalbim munib
34.	Udkhulu_ha_ bisala_m za_lika yaumul khulu_d
35.	Lahum ma_ yasya_ u_na fiha_ wa ladaina_ mazid
36.	Wakam ahlakna_ qablahum min garnin hum asyad du minhum batsyan fanaq qabu_ fil bila_d hal mim mahis
37.	In na fi za_lika lazikra_ liman ka_na lahu_ qalbun au alqas sama wa huwa sahid
38.	Wa laqad halaqnas sama_wa_ti wal arda wa ma_ bainahuma_ fi sit tati ay ya_miw wa ma_ mas sana_ mil lugu_b
39.	Fasbir ala_ ma_ yaqu_lu_na wa sab bih bihamdi rab bika qabla tulu_is samsi wa qablal ghuru_b
40.	Wa minal laili fasab bih hu wa adba_ras suju_d
41.	Wastami yauma yuna_dil muna_di mim maka_nin qarib
42.	Yauma yasmau_nas saihata bil haq za_lika yaumul khuru_j
43.	In na_ nahnu nuhyi wa numitu wa ilainal masir
44.	Yauma tasyaq qaqul ardu anhum sira_a_ za_lika hasyrun alaina_ yasir
45.	Nahnu alamu bima_ yaqu_lu_na wa ma_ anta alaihim bijab ba_rin fazakir bil qur a_ni may yaka_fu wajid
.EndTopic

.Topic qsAl-Qamar  " 54. Al Qamar"
1.	Iqtarabatis sa_atu wansyaq qal qamar
2.	Wa iy yarau a_yatay yuridu_ wa yaqu_lu_ sihrum mustamir
3.	Wa kaz zabu_ wat tabau_ ahwa_ ahum wa kul lu amrim mustaqir
4.	Wa laqad ja_ ahum minal an ba_i ma_ fihi muzajar
5.	Hikmatun ba_ligatun fama_ tugnin nuzur
6.	Fatawal la anhum yauma yadud dai ila_ syai in nukur
7.	Kus syaan absa_ruhum yakruju_na minal ajda_tsi ka an nahum jara_dum muntasir
8.	Muhtiina ilad da_ yaqu_lul ka_firu_na ha_za_ yaumun Qasir
9.	Kaz zabat qablahum qaumu nu_hin fakaz zabu_ abdana_ wa qa_lu_ majnu_nuw waz dujir
10.	Fadaa_ rab bahu_ ani maglu_bun fantasir
11.	Fafatahna_ abwa_bas sama_i bima_ im munhamir
12.	Wa faj jarnal arda uyu_nan faltaqal ma_u ala_ amrin qad qudir
13.	Wa hamalna_hu ala_ za_ti alwa_hiw wa dusur
14.	Tajri bi ayunina_ jaza_ al liman ka_na kufir
15.	Wa laqad tarakna_ha_ a_yatan fahal mim mud dakir
16.	Fakaifa ka_na aza_bi wa nuzur
17.	Wa laqad yas sarnal qur a_na liz zikri fahal mim mud dakir
18.	Kaz zabat a_dun fakaifa ka_na aza_bi wa nuzur
19.	In na_ arsalna_ alaihim rihan sarsaran fi yaumi nafsim mustamir
20.	Tanziun na_sa ka an nahum aja_zu naklim munqair
21.	Fakaifa ka_na aza_bi wa nuzur
22.	Wa laqad yas sarnal qur a_na liz zikri fahal mim mud dakir
23.	Kaz zabat samu_du bin nuzur
24.	Faqa_lu_ abasyaram min na_ wa_hidan nat tabiuhu_ in na_ azal lafi dala_liw wa suur
25.	A ulqiyaz zikru alaihi min bainina_ bal huwa kaz za_bun asyir
26.	Sayalamu_na gadam manil kaz za_bul asyir
27.	In na_ mursilun na_qati fitnatal lahum far taqibum was tabir
28.	Wa nab bihum an nal ma_a qismatun bainahum kul lu sirbim muhtadar
29.	Fana_dau sa_hibahum fataa_ta_ faaqar
30.	Fakaifa ka_na aza_bi wa nuzur
31.	In na_ arsalna_ alaihim saihataw wa_hidatan faka_nu_ kahasimil muhtazir
32.	Wa laqad yas sarnal qur a_na liz zikri fahal mim mud dakir
33.	Kaz zabat qaumu lu_tin bin nuzur
34.	In na_ arsalna_ alaihim ha_siban il la_ a_la lu_t naj jaina_hum bisahar
35.	Nimatam min indina_ kaza_lika najzi man sakar
36.	Wa laqad anzarahum batsatana_ fatama_rau bin nuzur
37.	Wa laqad ra_wadu_hu an daifihi fatamasna_ ayunahum fazu_qu_ aza_bi wa nuzur
38.	Wa laqad sab bahahum bukratan aza_bum mustaqir
39.	Fazu_qu_ aza_bi wa nuzur
40.	Wa laqad yas sarnal qur a_na liz zikri fahal mim mud dakir
41.	Wa laqad ja_a a_la firaunan nuzur
42.	Kaz zabu_ bi a_ya_tina_ kul liha_ fa akhazna_hum akza azizim muqtadir
43.	Akuf fa_rukum kairum min ula_ikum am lakum bara_ atun fiz zubur
44.	Am yaqu_lu_na nahnu jamium mun tasir
45.	Sayuhzamul jamu wa yuwal lu_nad dubur
46.	Balis sa_atu mauiduhum was sa'atu ad ha_ wa amar
47.	In nal mujrimina fi dala_liw wasu'ur
48.	Yauma yus habu_na fin na_ri ala_ wuju_hihim zu_qu_ mas sa saqar
49.	In na_ kul la sai in halaqna_hu biqadar
50.	Wa ma_ amruna_ il la_ wa_hidatun kalamhin bil basar
51.	Wa laqad ahlakna_ asya_akum fahal mim mud dakir
52.	Wa kul lu sai in fa'alu_hu fiz zubur
53.	Wa kul lu sagiriw wa kabirim mustatar
54.	In nal mut taqina fi jan na_tiw wa nahar
55.	Fi maqadi sidqin inda malikim muqtadir
.EndTopic

66.	Fihima_ aina_ni nad da_hata_n
67.	Fabi ay yi a_la_ rab bikuma_ tukaziba_n
68.	Fihima_ fa_kihatuw wa nakhluw warum ma_n
69.	Fabi ay yi a_la_i rab bikuma_ tukaziba_n
70.	Fihin na haira_tun hisa_n
71.	Fabi ay yi a_la-i rab bikuma_ tukaziba_n
72.	Hu_rum maqsu_ratun fil kiya_m
73.	Fabi ay yi a_la_ rab bikuma_ tukaziba_n
74.	Lam yatmis hun na insun qablahum wa la_ ja_n
75.	Fabi ay yi a_la_i rab bikuma_ tukaziba_n
76.	Mutakina ala_ rafrafin kudriw wa abqariy yin hisa_n
77.	Fabi ay yi a_la_i rab bikuma_ tukaziba_n
78.	Taba_rakas mu rab bika zil jala_li wal ikra_m
.EndTopic
;_______________________________
.Topic qsAl-Waqiah  " 56. Al Waqiah"
1.	Iza_ waqaatil wa_qiah
2.	Laisa liwaqatiha_ ka_zibah
3.	Ka_fidatur ra_fiah
4.	Iza_ ruj jatil ardu raj ja_
5.	Ya bus satil jiba_lu bas sa_
