.Topic qsAl-Hadid  " 57. Al Hadid"
1.	Sab baha lil la_hi ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa huwal azizul hakim
2.	Lahu_ mulkus sama_wa_ti wal ardi yuhyi wa yumitu wa huwa ala_ kuli sai in qadir
3.	Huwal aw walu wal a_khiru waz za_hiru wal ba_tinu wa huwa bikul li sai in alim
4.	Huwal lazi halaqas sama_wa_ti wal arda fi sit tati aya ya_min sum mas tawa_ alal arsy yalamu ma_ yaliju fil ardhi wa ma_ yakhruju minha_ wa ma_ yanzilu minas sama_i wa ma_ yaruju fiha_ wa huwa ma'akum aina ma_ kuntum wal la_hu bima_ tamalu_na basir
5.	Lahu_ mulkus sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa ilal la_hi turjaul umu_r
6.	Yu_lijul laila fin naha_ri wa yu_lijun naha_ra fil lail wa huwa alimun biza_tis sudu_r
7.	A_minu_ bil la_hi wa rasu_lihi wa anfiqu_ mim ma_ ja'alakum mustaklafina fih fal lazina a_manu_ minkum wa anfaqu_ lahum ajrun kabir
8.	Wa ma_ lakum la_ tuminu_na bil la_hi war rasu_lu yadu_kum lituminu_ birab bikum wa qad akhaza misa_qakum in kuntum muminin
9.	Huwal lazi yunaz zilu ala_ abdihi a_ya_tim bay yina_til liyukrijakum minaz zuluma_ti ilan nu_r wa in nal la_ha bikum lara u_fur rahim
10.	Wa ma_ lakum al la_ tunfiqu_ sabilil la_hi wa lil la_hi mira_tsus sama_wa_ti wal ard la_ yastawil minkum man anfaqa min qablil fat hi wa qa_tal ula_ika azamu darajatam minal lazina anfaqu_ min badu wa qa_talu_ wa kul law wa'adal la_hul husna_ wal la_hu bima_ tamalu_na kabir
11.	Man zal lazi yuqridul la_ha qardan hasanan fayuda_ifahu_ lahu_ wa lahu_ ajrun karim
12.	Yauma taral muminina wal mumina_ti yasa_ nu_ruhum baina aidihim wa bi aima_nihim busra_kumul yauma jan na_tun tajri min tahtihal anha_ru ha_lidina fiha_ za_lika huwal fauzul azhim
13.	Yauma yaqu_lul muna_fiqu_na wal muna_fiqa_tu lil lazina a_manun zuru_na_ naqtabis min nu_rikum qilar jiu wara_akum fal tamisu_ nu_ran faduriba bainahum bisu_ril lahu_ ba_b ba_tinuhu_ fihir rahmatu wa za_hiruhu_ min qibalihil aza_b
14.	Yuna_du_nahum alam nakum maakum qa_lu_ bala_ wa la_kin nakum fatantum anfusakum wa tarab bastum war rabtum wa gar ratkumul ama_niy yu hat ta_ ja_a amrul la_hi wa gar rakum bil la_hil garu_r
15.	Falyauma la_ yukazu minkum fid yatuw wa la_ minal lazina kafaru_ mawa_kumun na_ri hiya maula_kum wa bisal mashir
16.	Alam yani lil lazina a_manu_ an takhsyaa qulu_buhum lizikril la_hi wa ma_ nazala minal haq qi wa la_ yaku_nu_ kal lazina u_tul kita_ba min qablu fatha_la alihimul amadu faqasat qulu_buhum wa katsirum minhum fa_siqu_n
17.	I lamu_ an anl la_ha yuhyil arda bada mautiha_ qad bay yan na_ lakumul a_ya_til la'al lakum taqilu_n
18.	Innal mus sadiqina wal mus sadiqa_ti wa aqrasul la_ha qardan hasanan yudha_afu lahum wa lahum ajrun karim
19.	Wal lazina a_manu_ bil la_hi wa rusulihi ula_ ika humus sidiqu_n was suhada_u inda rab bihim lahum ajruhum wa nu_ruhum wal lazina kafaru_ wa kaz zabu_ bi a_ya_tina_ ula_ika asha_bul jahim
20.	Ilamu_ an namal haya_tud dun ya_ laibuw wa lahwuw wa zinatuw tafa_khurun nainakum wa taka_tsurun fil amwa_li wal aula_d kamatsali gaisin ajabal kuf fa_ra naba_tuhu_ sum ma yahiju fatara_hu musfar ran suma yaku_nu huta_ma_ wa fil a_khirati aza_bun sadiduw wa magfiratum minal la_hi wa ridwa_n wa mal haya_tud dun ya_ il la_ mata_ul guru_r
21.	Sa_biqu_ ila_ magfiratim mir rab bikum wa jan natin arduha_ kaardis sama_i wal ardi uid dat lil lazina a_manu_ bil la_hi wa rusulih za_lika fadlul la_hi yutihi may yasya_u wal la_hu zul fadlil azim
22.	Ma_ asha_ba mim musibatin fil ardi wa la_ fi anfusikum il la_ fi kita_bim min qabli an nabra aha_ in na za_lika alal la_hi yasir
23.	Likaila_ tasau ala_ ma_ fa_takum wa la_ tafrahu_ bima_ a_ta_kum wal la_hu la_ yuhib bu kul la mukta_lin faku_r
24.	Al lazina yabkalu_na wa yamuru_nan na_sa bil bukl wa may yatawal la fa in nal la_ha huwal gainiy yul hamid
25.	Laqad arsalna_ rusulana_ bil bay yina_ti wa anzalna_ ma'ahumul kita_ba wal miza_na liyaqu_man na_su bil qisth wa anzalna hadida fihi basun sadiduw wa mana_fiu lin na_si wa liyalamal la_hu may yansuruhu_ wa rusulahu_ bil gaib in nal la_ha qawiy yun aziz
26.	Wa laqad arsalna_ nu_haw wa  ibra_hima wa ja'alna_ fi zur riy yatihi man nubuw wata wal kita_ba famin hum muhtad wa kasirum minhum fa_siqu_n
27.	Suma qaf faina_ ala_ a_tsa_rihim birusulina_ wa qaf faina_ biisabni maryama wa a_taina_hul injila wa ja'alna_ fi qulu_bil lazinat tabau_hu rafat aw wa rahmah wa rahba_niy yata nibtadau_ha_ ma_ katabna_ha_ alaihim il labtiga_a ridwa_nil la_hi fama_ ra'auha_ haq qa ri a_ya_tiha_ fa a_tainal lazina a_manu_ minhum ajrahum wa katsirum minhum fa_siqu_n
28.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manut taqul la_ha wa a_minu_ birasu_lihi yutikum kiflaini mir rahmatihi wa yajal lakum nu_ran tamsu_na bihi wa yagfir lakum wal la_hu gafu_rur rahim
29.	Li al la_ yalama ahlul kita_bi al la_ yaqdiru_na ala_ sai im min fadlil la_hi wa an nal fadla biyadil la_hi yutihi may yasya_ wal la_hu zulfadil azim
.EndTopic
;_________________________________
.Topic qsAl-Mujadilah  " 58. Al Mujadilah"
1.	Qad samial la_hu qaulal lati tuja_di luka fi zaujiha_ wa tastaki ilil la_hi wal la_hu yasmau taha_wurakuma_ in nal la_ha sam,iun basir
2.	Al lazina yuza_hiru_na minkum miin nisa_ihim ma_ hun na um maha_tihim in um maha_tuhum il lal la_i waladnahum wa in nahum laya qu_lu_na munkaram minal qauli wa zu_ra_ wa in nal la_ha laafuw wun gafu_r
3.	Wal lazina yuza_hiru_na min nisa_ ihim suma yau_du_na lima_ qa_lu_ fatariru raqabatim min qabli ay yatama_ sa_ za_likum tuazu_na bih wal la_hu bima_ tamalu_na kabir
4.	Famal lam yajid fasiya_mu sahraini mutata_biaini min qabli ay yatama_s sa_ famal lam yastati fa ita_mu sitina miskina za_lika lituminu_ bil la_hi wa rasu_lih wa tilka hudu_la_h wa lilka_firina aza_bun alim
5.	In nal lazina yuha_d du_nal la_ha wa rasu_lahu_ kubitu_ kama_ kubital lazina min qablihim wa qad anzalna_ a_ya_tim bay yina_t wa lilka_firina aza_bum muhin
6.	Yauma yabasuhumul la_hu jamian fayunab bi uhun bima_ Qamilu_ ahsa_hul la_hu wa nasu_h wal la_hu ala_ kuli sai in sahid
7.	Alam tara an nal la_ha yalamu ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ard ma_ yaku_nu min najwa_ sala_satin il la_ huwara_biuhum wa la_ hamsatin min za_lika wa la_ aksara il la_ huwa maahum ainama_ ka_nu suma yunab bi uhum bima_ amilu_ yaumal qiya_mah in nal la_ha bikuli sai in alim
8.	Alam tara ilil lazina nuhu_ anin najwa_ suma yau_du_na lima_ nuhu_ anhu wa yatana_jauna bil ismi wal udwa_ni wa masiyatir rasu_li wa iza_ ja_ u_ka hay yauka bima_ lam yuhay yika bihil la_hu wa yaqu_lu_na fi anfusihim lau la_yuaz zibunal la_hu bima_ naqu_l hasbuhum jahan namu yaslaunaha_ fabisal masir
9.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ iza tana_jaitum fala_ tatana_jau bil ismi wal udwa_ni wa masiyatir rasu_li wa tana_jau bil biri wat taqwa_ wat taqul la_hal lazi ilaihi tusyaru_n
10.	In naman najwa_ minas saita_ni liyahzunal lazina a_manu_ wa laisa bida_rihim sai in il la_ bi iznilla_h wa alal la_hi falyatawak kalil muminu_n
11.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ iza_ qila lakum tafas sahu_ fil maja_lisi fafsahu_ yafsahil la_hu lakum wa iza_ qilan suzu_ fan suzu_ yarfail la_hul lazina a_manu_ minkum wal lazina u_tul ilma daraja_t wal la_hu bima_ tamalu_na kabir
12.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ iza_ na_jaitumur rasu_la faqad dimu_ baina yadai najwa_ kum sadaqah za_lika kairul rahim
13.	A asfaqtum an tuqad dimu_ baina yadai najwa_kum sadaqa_t fa izlam tafalu_ wa ta_bal la_hu alaikum fa aqimus sala_ta wa a_tuz zaka_ta wa atiul la_ha wa rasu_lah wal la_hu kabirun bima_ tamalu_n
14.	Alam tara ilil lazina tawal lau qauman gadibal la_hu alaihim ma_hum minkum wa la_ minhum wa yahlifu_na alal kazibi wa hum yalamu_n
15.	Aad dal la_hu lahum aza_ban sadida_ in nahum sa_a ma_ ka_nu_ yalamu_n
16.	It takazu_ aima_nahum jun natan fasad du_ an sabilil la_hi falahum aza_bum muhin
17.	Lan tugniya anhum amwa_luhum wa la_ aula_duhum minal la_hi saia_ ula_ika asha_bun na_r hum fiha_ ha_lidu_n
18.	Yauma yabatsuhumul la_hu jamian fayahlifu_na lahu_ kama_ yahlifu_na lakum wa yahsabu_na an nahum ala_ sai ala_ in nahum humul ka_zibu_n
19.	Istahwaza alaihimus saita_nu fa ansa_hum zikral la_h ula_ika hizbus saita_n ala_ in na hizbay saita_ni humul kha_siru_n
20.	In nal lazina yuha_d du_nal la_ha wa rasu_lahu_ ula_ika fil azal lin
21.	Katabal la_hu la agliban na ana wa rusuli in nal la_ha qawiy yun aziz
22.	La_ tajidu qaumay yuminu_na bil la_hi wal yaumil a_khiri yuwa_d du_na man ha_d dal la_ha wa rasu_lahu_ wa lau ka_nu_ a_ba_ahum au abna_ ahum au ikhwa_nahum au asyiratahum ula_ika kataba fi qulu_bihimul ima_na wa ay yadahum biru_him min wa yudkiluhum jan na_tin tajri min tahtihal anha_ruka_lidina fiha_ radiyal la_hu anhum wa radu_ an ula_ika hizbul la_h ala_ in na hizbal la_hi humul muflihu_n
.EndTopic
;_________________________________
.Topic qsAl-Hasyr  " 59. Al Hasyr"
1.	Sab baha_ lil la_hi ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ardi wa huwal azizul hakim
2.	Huwal lazi akhrajal lazina kafaru_ min ahlil kita_bi mindiya_rihim li aw walil hasyr ma_ zanantum ay yakhruju_ wa zan nu_ an nahum ma_nia tuhum hushu_nuhum minal la_hi fa ata_humul la_hu min haitsu lam yah tasibu_ wa qazafa fi qulu_bihimur ruba yukhribu_na buyu_tahum bi aidihim wa aidil muminima fatabiru_ ya_ ulil absa_r
3.	Wa lau la_ an katabal la_hu alaihimul jala_a la'az zabahum fid dun ya_ wa lahum fil a_khirati aza_bun nar
4.	Za_lika bi an nahum sa_q qul la_ha wa rasu_lahu_ wa may yusya_q qil la_ha fa in nal la_ha sadidul iqa_b
5.	Ma_ qatatum mil linatin au taraktumu_ha_ qa_ imatan ala_ ushu_liha_ fabi iznil la_hi wa liyukziyal fa_siqin
6.	Wa ma_ afa_al la_hu ala_ rasu_lihi minhum fama_ aujaftum alaihi min hailiw wa la_ rika_biw wa la_kin nal la_ha yusal lithu rusulahu_ ala_ may yasya_ wal la_hu ala_ kuli sai in qadir
7.	Ma afa_ al la_hu ala_ rasu_lihi min ahlil qura_ falil la_hi wa lir rasu_li walizil qurba_ wal yata_ma_ wal masa_kini wab nis sabili kaila_ yaku_na du_latambainal agniya_i minkum wa ma_ a_ta_kumur rasu_lu fakuzu_ hu wa ma_naha_kum anhu fantahu_ wataqul la_h in nal la_ha sadidul iqa_b
8.	Lilfuqara_ il muha_jirinal lazina ukhriju_ min diya_rihim wa amwa_lihim yabtaghu_na fadlam minal la_hi wa ridwa_naw wa yansuru_nal la_ha wa rasu_luh ula_ika humus sa_diqun
9.	Wal lazina tabaw wa ud da_ra wal ima_na min qablihim yuhib bu_na man ha_jara ilaihim wa la_ yajidu_na fi sudu_rihim ha_jatam mim ma_ u_tu_ wa yusiru_na ala_ anfusihim wa lau ka_na bihim kasa_sah wa may yu_qa suhanafsihi fa ula_ika humul muflihu_n
10.	Wal lazina ja_u_ min badihim ya qu_lu_na rab banagfir lana_ wali ikwa_ninal lazina sabaqu_na_ bil ima_ni wa la_ tajal fi qulu_bina_ gilal lil lazina a_manu_ rab bana_ in naka rau_fur rahim
11.	Alam tara ilal lazina na_faqu ya qu_lu_na li ikhwa_nihimul lazina kafaru_ min ahlil kita_bi la in ukhrijtum lanakru jan na maakum wa la_ nutiu fikum ahadan abadaw wa in qu_tiltum lanansuran nakum wal la_hu yashadu un nahum laka_zibu_n
12.	La in ukhriju_ la_ yakhruju_na maahum wa la in qu_tilu_ la_ yansuru_ nahum wa la in nasharu_hum layu wal lun nal adba_ra sum ma la_ yun saru_n
13.	La antum asyad du rahbatan fi sudu_rinhim minal la_h za_lika bi an nahum qaumul la_ yafqahu_n
14.	La_ yuqa_tilu_nakum jamian il la_ fi quram muhas sanatin au miw wara_i judur basuhum bainahum sadid tahsabuhum jamiaw wa qulu_ buhum sat ta_ za_lika bi an nahum qaumul la_ yaqilu_n
15.	Kamatsalil lazina min qablihim qariban za_qu_ waba_la amrihim wa lahum aza_bun alim
16.	Kamatsalis saita_ni qa_la lil insa_nikfur falam ma_ kafara qa_la in ni barium minka in ni akha_ful la_ha rab bal a_lamin
17.	Faka_na a_qibatahuma_ an nahuma_ fin na_ri ha_lidaini fiha_ wa za_lika  jaza_ uz za_limin
18.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_t taqul la_ha wal tanzhur nafsum ma_ qad damat ligadin wat taqul la_h in nal la_ha habirum bima_ tamalu_n
19.	Wa la_ taku_nu_ kal lazina nasul la_ha fa ansa_hum anfusahum ula_ika humul fa_siqu_n
20.	La_ yastawi asha_bun na_ri wa asha_bul jan nah asha_bul jan nati humul fa_izu_n
21.	Lau anzalna_ ha_zal qur a_na ala_ jabalil lara aitahu_ kha_sian mutasad diam min khasyatil la_h wa tilkal amsa_lu nadribuha_ lin na_si la'al lahum yatafak karu_n
22.	Huwal la_hul lazi la_ ila_ha il la_ huwa a_limul gaibi was saha_dati huwar rahma_nur rahim
23.	Huwal la_hul lazi la_ ila_ha huwal almalikul qud du_sus sala_mul muminul muhaiminul azizul jab ba_rul mutakab bir subha_nal la_hi am ma_ yusriku_n
24.	Huwal la_hul ha_liqul ba_ri ul musaw wiru lahul asma_ ul husna_ yu sab bihu lahu_ ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa huwal azizul hakim
.EndTopic
;_____________________________________________
.Topic qsAl-Mumtahanah  " 60. Al Mumtahanah"
1.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ la_ tat takhizu_ aduw wi wa aduw wakum auliya_a tulqu_na ilaihim bilmawad dati wa qad kafaru_ bima_ ja_akum minal haq yukhriju_nar rasu_la wa iy ya_kum an tuminu_ bil la_hi rab bikum in kuntum harajtum jiha_dan fi sabili wabtiga_a marda_ti tusir ru_na ilaihim bilmawad dah wa ana alamu bima_ akhfaitum wa ma_ alan tum wa may yafalhu minkum faqad dala sawa_ as sabil
2.	Iy yasqafu_kum yaku_nu_ lakum ada_ aw wa yabsutu_ ilaikum aidiyahum wa alsinatahum bis su_i wa wad du_ lau takfuru_n
3.	Lan tanfa'akum arha_mukum wa la_ aula_dukum yaumal qiya_mah yafsilu bainakum wal la_hu bima_ tamalu_na basir
4.	Qad ka_nat lakum uswatun hasanatun fi ibra_hima wal lazina maahu_ iz qa_lu liqaumihim in na_ bura_u minkum wa mim ma_ tabudu_na min du_nil la_hi kafarna_bikum wa bada_ bainana_ wa bainakumul ada_watu wal bagda_u abadan hat ta_ tuminu_ bil la_hi wahdahu_ il la_ qaula ibra_hima li abihi la astagfiran na laka wa ma_ amliku laka minal la_hi min sayi ran bana_ alaika tawak kalna_ wa ilaika anabna_ wa ilaikal masir
5.	Rab bana_ la_ tajalna_ fitnatal lazina kafaru_ wagfirlana_ rab bana_ in naka antal azizul hakim
6.	Laqad ka_na lakum fihim uswatun hasanatul liman ka_na yarjul la_ha wal yaumal a_khir wa may yatawal la fain nal la_ha huwal ganiy yul hamid
7.	Asal la_hu ay yajala bainakum wa bainal lazina a_daitum minhum mawad dah wal la_hu qadir wal la_hu gafu_rur rahim
8.	La_ yanha_kumul la_hu anil lazina lam yuqa_tilu_kum fid dini wa lam yuhkriju_kum min diya_rikum an tabar ru_hum wa tuqsitu_ ilaihim in nal la_ha yuhib bul muqsitin
9.	In nama_ yanha_kumul la_hu anil lazina qa_talu_kum fid dini wa akhraju_kum min diya_rikum wa zaharu_ may yatawal lahum fa ula_ika humuz za_limu_n
10.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ iza_ ja_ akumul mumina_tu muha_jira_tin famtahinu_hun al la_hu alamu bi ima_nihin fa in alimtumu_hun na mumina_tin fala_ tarjiu_hun na ilal kuf fa_r la_ hun na hil lul lahum wa lahum yahil lu_na lahun wa a_tu_ hum ma_ anfa_qu_ wa la_ juna_ha alaikum an tankihu_hun na iza_ a_ taitumu_hun na uju_rahun wa la_ tumsiku bi ishamil kawa_firi was alu_ ma_ anfaqtum wal yas alu_ ma_ anfaqu_ za_likum hukmul la_h yah kumu bainakum wal la_hu alimun hakim
11.	Wa in fa_takum saium min azwa_jikum ilal kuf fa_ri fa a_qabatum fa a_tul lazina zahabat azwa_juhum mitslama_ anfaqu_ wat taqul la_hal lazi antum bihi muminu_n
12.	Ya_ ay yuhan nabiyu iza ja_ akal mumina_tu yuba_yinaka ala_ al la_ yusrikna bil la_hi sai aw wa la_ yasriqna wa la_ yaznina wa la_ yaqtulna aula_dahun na wa la_ yatina bibuhta_niy yaftarinahu_ baina aidihin na wa arjulihin na wa la_ yasinaka fi maru_fin faba_yihun na wastagfir lahun nal la_h in nal la_ha gafu_rur rahim
13.	Ya_ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ la_ ta tawal lau qauman gadibal la_hu alaihim qad ya isu_ minal a_khirati kama_ ya isal kuf fa_ru min asha_bil qubu_r
.EndTopic
;________________________________
.Topic qsAs-Shaff  " 61. As Shaff"
1.	Sab baha lil la_hi ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ardi wa huwal azizul hakim
2.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ lima taqu_lu_na ma_ la_ tafalu_n
3.	Kabura maqtan indal la_hi an taqu_lu_ ma_ la_ tafalu_n
4.	In nal la_ha yuhib bul lazina yuqa_tilu_na fi sabilihi saf fan ka an nahum bun ya_num marsu_s
5.	Wa iz qa_la mu_sa_ liqaumihi ya_ qaumi lima tuzu_nani wa qad talamu_na an ni rasu_lul la_hi ilaikum, falam ma_ za_ghu_ aza_gal la_hu qulu_bahum wal la_hu la_ yahdil qaumal fa_siqin
6.	Wa iz qa_la isabnu maryama ya_ bani isra_ ila ini rasu_lul la_hi ilaikum mushad diqal lima_ baina yaday ya minat taura_ti wa mubas siran birasu_liy yail min badis muhu_ ahmad falam ma_ ja_ahum bil bay yina_ti qa_lu_ ha_za_ sihrum mubin
7.	Wa man azhlamu min manif tara_ alal la_hil kaziba wa huwa yuda_ ilal isla_m wal la_hu la_ yahdil qaumaz za_limin
8.	Yuridu_na liyuthfi u nu_ral la_hi bi afwa_hihim wal la_hu mutim mu nu_rihi wa lau karihal ka_firu_n
9.	Huwal lazi arsala rasu_lahu_ bil huda_ wa dinil haq qi liyuzhirahu_ alad dini kul lihi wa lau karihal musyriku_n
10.	Ya ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ hal adul lukum ala_ tija_ratin tunjikum min aza_bin alim
11.	Tuminu_na bil la_hi wa rasulihi wa tuja_hidu_na fi sabilil la_hi bi amwa_likum wa anfusikum, za_likum khairul lakum in kuntum talamu_n
12.	Yagfir lakum zunu_bakum wa yudkilkum jan na_tin tajri min tahtihal anha_ru wa masa_kina tay yibatan fi jan na_ti and, za_likal fauzul azim
13.	Wa ukhra_ tuhib bu_naha_ nasrum minal la_hi wa fat hun qarib wa basiril muminin
14.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ ku_nu_ ansha_ral la_hi kama_ qa_la isabnu maryama lilhawa_riy yina man ansa_ri ilal la_h qa_lal hawa_riy yu_na nahnu ansha_rul la_hi fa a_manat ta_ifa fum min bani isra_ila wa kafarat ta_ifah fa ay yadnal lazina a_manu_ ala_ aduw wihim fa ashbahu_ za_hirin
.EndTopic
;____________________________________
.Topic qsAl-Jumuah  " 62. Al Jumuah"
1.	Yusab bihu lil la_hi ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ardi malikil qud du_sil azizil hakim
2.	Huwal lazi baatsa fil um miy yina rasu_lam minhum yatlu_ alaihim a_ya_tihi wa yuzak kihim wa yual limuhumul kita_ba wal hikmah wa in ka_nu_ min qablu lafi dala_lim mubin
3.	Wa a_kharina minhum lam ma_ yalhaqu_ bihim wa huwal azizul hakim
4.	Za_lika fadul la_hi yutihi may yasya wal la_hu zul fadhil azhim
5.	Matsalul lazina hum milut taura_ta suma ma lam yahmilu_ha_ kamatsalil hima_ri yahmilu asfa_ra_ bisa matsalul qaumil lazina kaz zabu_ bia_ya_til la_h wal la_hu la_ yahdil qaumaz za_limin
6.	Qul ya_ ay yuhal lazina ha_du_ in zaantum an nakum auliya_u lil la_hi min du_nin na_si fa taman nawul mauta in kuntum sa_diqin
7.	Wa la_ yataman naunahu_ abadan bima_ qad damat aidihim wal la_hu alimun biz za_limin
8.	Qul in nal mautal lazi tafir ru_na minhu fa in nahu_ mula_qikum suma turad du_na ila_ a_limil gaibi was saha_dati fayunab bi ukum bima_ kuntum tamalu_n
9.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ iza_ nu_diya lis sala_ti miy yaumil jumuati fasau ila_ zikril la_hi wa zarul baia za_likum hairul lakum in kuntum talamu_n
10.	Fa iza_ qudiyatish sala_tu fantasyiru_ fil ardi wabtaghu_ min fadlil la_hi wazkurul la_ha katsiral la al lakum tuflihu_n
11.	Wa iza_ ra au tija_ratan au lahwanin fad du_ ilaiha_ wa taraku_ka qa_ima_ qul ma_ indal la_hi kairum minal lahwi wa minat tija_rah wal la_hu kairuf ra_ziqin
.EndTopic
;_________________________________________
.Topic qsAl-Munafiqun  " 63. Al Munafiqun"
1.	Iza_ ja_akal muna_fiqu_na qa_lu_ nashadu in naka larasu_lul la_h wal la_hu yalamu in naka larasu_luh wal la_hu yas hadu in nal muna_fiqina taka_zibu_n
2.	It takazu_ aima_nahum jun natan fasad du_ an sabilil la_h in nahum sa_a ma_ ka_nu yamalu_n
3.	Za_lika bi an nahum a_manu_ sum ma kafaru_ fatubia ala_ qulu_bihim fahum la_ yafqahu_n
4.	Wa iza_ ra aitahum tujibuka ajsa_muhum wa iy yaqu_lu_ tasma liqaulihim ka an nahum husubum musan nadatun yabsabu_na kul la saihatin alaihim humul aduw wu fahzarhum qa_talahumul la_hu an na_ yufaku_n
5.	Wa iza_ qila lahum taa_lau yastagfir lakum rasu_lul la_hi law wau ru u_sahum wa ra aitahum yashud du_na wahum mustakbiru_n
6.	Sawa_un alaihim astagfarta lahum am lam tastagfi lahum lay yagfiral la_hu lahum in nal la_ha la_ yahdil qaumal la_siqin
7.	Humul lazina yaqu_lu_na la_ tunfiqu_ ala_ man inda rasu_lil la_hi hata_ yanfadu du_ wa lil la_hi haza_inus sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa la_kinal muna_fiqina la_ yafqahu_n
8.	Yaqu_lu_na la ir rajana_l ilal madinati layukhrijan nal a'az zu minhal azal wal lil la_hil iz zatu wa lirasu_lihi wa lilmuminina wa la_kin nal muna_fiqina la_ yalamu_n
9.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ la_ tulhikum amwa_lukum wa la_ aula_dukum an zikril la_hi wa may yafal za_lika fa ula_ ika humul ha_siru_n
10.	Wa anfiqu_ mim ma_ razaqna_kum min qabli ay yatiya ahadakumul mautu layaqu_la rab bi lau la_ akh karta mi ila_ ajalin qaribin fa as sad daqa qa akum minas sa_lihin
11.	Wa lay yu akhiral la_hu nafsan iza_ ja_ a ajaluha_ wal la_hu habi un bima_ tamalu_n
.EndTopic
;_______________________________________
.Topic qsAt-Taghabun  " 64. At Taghabun"
1. 	Yusabihu lil la_hi ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ardhi lahul hamdu wa huwa ala_ ku li syai in qadir
2. 	Huwal ladzi khalaqakum laminkum ka_firuw wa minkum mumin wal la_hu bima_ tamalu_na bashir
3. 	Khalaqasa_ma_wa_ti wal ardha bil haq qi wa shaw warakum fa ahsana shuwa rakum wa ilaihil mashur
4. 	Ya lamu ma_  fis sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa yalamu ma_ tusu ru_na wa ma_ tulinu_n wal la_hu alimun biza_ tisudu_n
5. 	Alam yatikum naba ul lazina kafaru_ min qablu faza_qu_ wa ba_la amrihim wa lahum aza_bun alim
6. 	Zalika bi an nahu_ ka_nat tatihim rusuluhum bil bay yina_ti faqa_lu_ abasaru yahdu_nana_ fakafaru_ wa tawal lau wa istagnal la_h wal la_hu ganiy yun hamid
7. 	Za'amal lazina kafaru_ ahay yub atsu_ qul bala_ wa rab bu la tub atsun na sum ma latunab ba un na bima_ amiltum wa za_lika alal la_hi yasur
8. 	Fa a_minu_ bil la_hi wa rasu_lihi wan nu_ril lazi anzalna_ wal la_hu bima_ tamalu_na kabir
9. 	Yauma yajmaukum layaumil jami za_lika yaumut taga_hun wa may yumin bil la_hi wa yamal sa_lihay yukal fir anhu say yi a_tihi wa yud hilku jan na_tin taji min tahtihal anha_ru ha_lidina fiha_ abada_ za_likal fauzul azhim
10.	Wal lazina kafaru_ wa kaz zabu_ bi a_ya_tina_ ula_ika asha_bun na_ri ha_lidina fiha_ wa bisal masi
11.	Ma_ asha_ba mim musibatin il la_ bi iznil la_h wa may yumin bil la_hi yahdi qalbahu_ wal la_hu bikul li sai in alim
12.	Wa atiul la_ha wa athiur rasu_la fa in tawal laitum fa in nama_ ala_ rasu_linal balagul mubin
13.	Al la_hu la_ ila_ha il la_ huw wa alal la_hi falyatawak kalil muminu_n
14.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ in na min azwa_jikum wa aula_dikum aduw wal lakum fahzaru_hum wa in tafu_ wa tasfahu_ wa tagfiru_ fa in nal la_ha gafu_rur rahim
15.	In nama_ amwa_lukum wa aula_dukum fitnah wal la_hu indahu_ ajrun azim
16.	Fat taqul la_ha mastata tum wasmau_ wa atiu_ wa unfiqu_ khairal li anfisukum wa may yu_qa suh ha nafsihi fa ula_ika humul muflihu_n
17.	In tuqridul la_ha qardan hasanay yuda_ifhu lakum wa yagfir lakum wal la_hu saku_run halim
18.	A_limul gaibi was saha_datil azizul hakim 
.EndTopic
;__________________________________
.Topic qsAt-Thalaq  " 65. At Thalaq"
1.	Ya_ ayuhan nabiy yu idza_ thal laq tumun nisa_ a fathal liqu_hun na li id datihin na wa ahshul id data wat taqul la_ha rab bakum la_ yakhrujna il la_ ay yatina bifa_hisyatim mubay yinah, wa tilka hudu_dul la_h, wa may yata'ad da hudu_dal la_hi faqad zhalama nafsahu_dal la_ha yuhditsu bada dza_lika amra_
2.	Fa iza_ balagna ajalahun na fa amsi ku_hun na bimaru_fin au fa_riqu_hun na bimaru_fiwwa ashidu_ zawai adlim minkum wa aqimus saha_data lil la_hi zalikum yu_azhubihi man ka_na yuminu bil la_hi wal yaumil a_khir wa may yat taqil la_ha yajal lahu_ makhraja_
3.	Wa yarzuqhu min haitsu la_ yahtasib, wa may yatakwak kal alal la_hi fa huwa hasbuh in nal la_ha ba_ligu amrih qad ja'alal la_hu likul li sai in qadra_
4.	Wal la_i ya isna minal mahidi min nisa_ ikum inir tabtum faid datuhun na sala_tsatu ashuriw wal la_i lam yahidn wa ula_tul ahma_li ajalahuna ay yadana hamlahun wa may yat taqil la_ha yajal lahu_ min amrihi yusra_
5.	Za_lika amrul la_hi anzalahu_ ilaikum wa may yat taqil la_ha yukaf fir anhu say yi a_tihi wa yuzim lahu_ ajra_
6.	Askinu_hun na min haitsu sakantum miw wujdikum wa la_ tudha_r ru_huna lituday yiqu_ alihin wa in kun na_ ula_ti hamlin fa anfiqu_ alaihin na hat ta_ yadana hamlahun na fa in ardana lakum fa a_tu_huna uju_rahun na wa tamiru_ bainakum bimaru_fiw wa in taa_sartum fasaturdiu lahu_ ukhra_
7.	Liyunfiq zu_ saatim min saatih wa man qudira alaihi rizquhu_ falyunfiq mim ma_ a_ta_hul la_h la_ yukal lifulla_hu nafsan il la_ ma_ a_ta_ha_ sayajalul la_hu bada usriy yusra_
8.	Wa ka ay yim min qaryatin atat an amri rab biha_ wa rusulihi faha_sabna_ha_ hisa_ban sadidaw wa azzabna_ha_ aza_ban nukra_
9.	Faza_qat waba_la amriha_ wa ka_na a_qibatu amriha_ khusra_
10.	A'ad dal la_hu lahum aza_ban sadidan fat taqul la_ha ya_ ulil alba_bil lazina a_manu_ qad anzalal la_hu ilaikum zikra_
11.	Rasu_lay yatlu_ alaikum a_ya_til la_hi mubay yina_til liyukrijal lazina a_manu_ wa amilush sa_liha_ti minaz zuluma_ti ilan nu_r wa may yumin bil la_hi wa yamal sa_lihay yudkilhu jan na_tin tajri min tahtihal anha_ru ka_lidina fiha_ abada_ qad ahsanal la_hu  lahu_ rizqa_
12.	Al la_hul lazi halaqa saba sama_wa_tiw wa minal ardi mitslahun yatanaz zalul amru bainahuna litalamu_ an nal la_ha ala_ kul li syai in qadiruw wa an nal la_ha qad aha_ta bikuli sai in ilma_
.EndTopic
;___________________________________
.Topic qsAt-Tahrim  " 66. At Tahrim"
1.	Ya_ ay yuhan nabiyu lima tuhar rimu ma_ ahal lal la_hu laka tabtagi marda_ta azwa_jik wal la_hu gafu_rur rahim
2.	Qad faradal la_hu lakum tahil lata aima_nikum wal la_hu maula_kum wa huwal alimul hakim
3.	Wa iz asar ran nabiyu ila_ badi azwa_jihi hadistsa falam ma_ nab ba at bihi wa azharahul la_hu alaihi ar rafa badahu_ wa arada an badin falam ma_ nab ba ahabihi qa_lat man an ba aka ha_za_ qa_la nab ba aniyal alimul kabir
4.	In tatu_ba_ ilal la_hi faqad sagat qulu_bukuma_ wa in taza_hara_ alaihi la in nal la_ha huwa maula_hu wa jib rilu wa sa_lihul muminin wal mala_ ikatu bada za_lika zahir
5.	Asa_ rab buhu_ in tal laqakun na ay yubdilahu_ azwa_jan kairan minkuna muslima_tim mumina_tin qa_nita_tin ta_ iba_tin a_bida_tin sa_iha_tin say yibatiw wa abka_ra_
6.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ qu_ anfusakum wa ahlikum na_raw wa qu_duhan na_su wal hija_ratu alaiha_ mala_ ikatun gila_zun sida_dul la_ yasu_nal la_ha ma_ amarahum wa yafalu_na ma_ yumaru_n
7.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina kafaru_la_ tatazirul yaum in nama_ tujzauna ma_ kuntum tamalu_n
8.	Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ tu_bu_ ilal la_hi taubatan nasu_ha_ asa_ rabukum ay yukaf fira ankum say yia_tikum wa yudhilakum jan na_tin tajri min tahtihal anha_ru yauma la_ yukhzil la_hun nabiy ya wal lazina a_manu_ maahu_ nu_ruhum yasa_baina aidihim wa bi aima_nihim ya qu_lu_na rab bana_ atmim lana_ nu_ rana_ wagfir lana_ in naka ala_ kul li sai in qadir
9.	Ya ay yuhan nabiy yu ja_hidil kuf fa_ra wal muna_fiqina wagluz alaihim wa mawa_hum jahan nam wa bisal masir
10.	Darabal la_hu matsalal lil lazina kafarum ra ata nu_hiw wamra ata lu_t ka_nata_ tahta abdaini min iba_dina_ sa_lihaini fakha_nata_huma_ falam yughniya_ anhuma_ minal la_hi sai aw wa qilad kulan na_ra maad da_ hilin
11.	Wa  darabal la_hu matsalal lil lazina a_manum ra ata firaun iz qa_lat rabibni lil indaka baitan fil jan nati wa naj jini min firauna wa amalihi wa naj jini minal qaumiz za_limin
12.	Wa maryamab nata imra_nal latu ahsanat farjaha_ fanafahna_ fihi mir ru_hina_ wa sad daqat bikalima_ti rab iha_ wa kutubihi wa ka_nat minal qa_nitin
.EndTopic
;______________________________________
.Topic qsAl-Mulk  " 67. Al Mulk"
1.	Taba_rakal lazi biyadil mulku wahuwa ala_  syain qadir
2.	Alazi halakal mauta wal haya_ta liyab luwakumay yukum ahsanu ama la_ wa huwal azizul gafu_r
3.	Aflazi halaqa saba sama_wa_tin tiba_qa_, ma_ tara_ fi halqir rahma_ni min tafa_wut farjiil  basara hal tara_ min futu_r
4.	Sumar jiil basara karataini yankalib ilaikal basaru ka_sian wa huwa hasir
5.	Wa laqad zayan nas sama_ adun ya_ bimasa_biha wa ja'alna_ha_ ruju_mal lisyaya_tini wa atadna_ lahum aza_basair
6.	Wa lil lazina kafaru_ birabihim aza_bu jahanam wa bisal masir
7.	Iza ulqu_ fiha_ samiu_ laha_ sahiqaw wa hiya tafu_r
8.	Taka_du tama yazu minal gaiz kulama_ ulqiya fiha_ faujun sa alahum hazanatuha_ alam yatikum nazir.
9.	Qa_lu bala_ qad ja_ana_ nazirun fakaz zabna_ wa qulna_ ma_ naz zalal la_hu min syain in antum il la_ fi dala_lin kabir
10.	Wa qa_lu lau kun na_ nasmau au naqilu ma_ kun na_ fi asha_bi sair
11.	Fa tarafu_ bizan bihim fasuhqal liasha_bis sair
12.	Inal lazina yaksyauna rabahum bil gaibi lahum magfiratu wa ajrun kabir
13.	Wa asiru_ qaulakum awij haru_ bih, inahu_ alimun biza_tis sudu_r
14.	Ala_ yalamu man halaq wa huwal la tiful kabir
15.	Huwal lazi jaala lakumul arda zalu_lan famsu_ fi mana_kibiha_ wa kulu_ mir rizqi wa ilaihin nusu_r
16.	A amitum man fisama_i ay yahsifa bikumul arda faiza_ hiya tamu_r
17.	Am amintum man fis sama_i ay yursi la alaikum ha_siba_ fasatalamu_na kaifa nazir
18.	Wa laqad kazabal lazina min qablihim fakaifa ka_na nakir
19.	Awalam yarau ilat tairi fauqahum sa_f fatiw wa yaqbidin ma_ yumsikuhun na il lar rahma_n in nahu_ bi kuli sai in basir
20.	Am man ha_dzal ladzi huwa jundul lakum yanshurukum min du_nir rah ma_n inil ka_firu_na il la_ fi ghuru_r
21.	Am man ha_dzal ladzi  yarzuqukum in amsaka rizqahu_ bal laj ju_fi utuw wiw wa nufu_r
22.	Afamay yamsyi mukib ban ala_ waj hihi ahda_ am may yamsyi sawiy yan ala_ shira_thim mustaqim
23.	Qul huwal ladzi ansya akum wa ja'ala lakumus sama wal absha_ra wal af I dah,qalilam ma_ tasykuru_n
24.	Qul huwal ladzi dzara akum fil ardhi wa ilaihi tuhsyaru_n
25.	Wa yaqu_lu_na mata_ ha_dzal wadu in kuntum sha_diqin
26.	Qul in namal ilmu indal la_hi wa in nama_ ana nadzirum mubin
27.	Falam ma_ ra auhu zulfatan si at wuju_hul ladzina kafaru_ wa qila ha_dzal ladzi kuntum bihi tad dau_n
28.	Qul ara aitum in ahlakaniyal ta_hu wa mam maiya aurahimana_ famay yuji rul ka_firina min adza_bin alim
29.	Qul huwar rahma_nu a_man na_ bihi wa alaihi tawak kalna_ fasatalamu_na man huwa fi dhala_lim mubin
30.	Qul ara aitum in ashbana ma_ ukum ghauran famay yatikum bima_ im ma in
.EndTopic
;__________________________________
.Topic qsAl-Qalam  " 68. Al Qalam"
1.	Nu_n wal qalami wa ma_ yasthuru_n
2.	Ma_ anta binimati rab bika bimajnu_n
3.	Wa in na laka la airan ghaira mam nu_n
4.	Wa in naka la'ala_ khuluqin azhim
5.	Fasatubshiru wa yubshiru_n
6.	Bi ay yikumul maftu_n
7.	In na rab baka huwa alamu biman dhal la an sahilih wa huwa alamu bil muhtadin
8.	Fala_ tuthiil mukadz dzibin
9.	Wad du_ lau tud hinu fayud hinu_n
10.	Wa  la_ tuthikul la hal la_fim mahin
11.	Ham ma_zim  masy sya_in binamim
12.	Man na_il likhairi mutadin atsim
13.	Utul lin bada dza_lika zanim
14.	An ka_na dza_ ma_liw wa banin
15.	Idza_ tutla_ alaihi a_ya_tuna_ qa_la asa_thirul aw walim
16.	Sanasimuhu_ alal khurthu_m
17.	In na_ balauna_hum kama_ balauna_ ashha_bal jan nati idz aqsamu_ layash rimun naha_ mushbihin
18.	Wa la_ yastatsnu_n
19.	Fatha_fa alaiha_ tha_ ifum mir rab bika wa hum na_ imu_n
20.	Fa ashbahat kash sharim
21.	Fatana_dau mushbihim
22.	Anighdu_ ala_ hartssikum in kuntum sha_rimin
23.	Fanthalaqu_ wa hum yatakha_fatu_n
24.	Al la_ yadkhulan nahal yauma alai kum miskin
25.	Wa ghadau ala_ hardin qa_dinin
26.	Falam ma_ ra auha_ qa_lu_ in na_ la dha_l lu_n
27.	Bal nahnu mahru_mu_n
28.	Qa_la ausathuhum alam aqul lakum lau la_ tusab bihu_n
29.	Qa_lu_ subha_na rab bina_ in na_kun na_za_limin
30.	Fa aqbala baduhum ala_ badiy ya tal a_wamu_n
31.	Qa_lu_ ya_ wailana_ ina_ kun na_ ta_gin
32.	Asa_ rabuna_ ayubdilana_ hairam minha_ in na_ ila_ rabina_ ra_gibu_n
33.	Kaza_likal aza_b wa laaza_bul a_khirati akbar lau ka_nu_ yalamu_n
34.	Ina lilmut taqina inda rabihim jan na_tin naim
35.	Afanajalul muslimina kal mujrimin
36.	Ma_ lakum kaifa tahkumu_n
37.	Am lakum kita_bun fihi tadrusu_n
38.	Ina lakum fihi lama_ takhay yaru_n
39.	Am lakum aima_nun alina a_ ba_ligatun ila_ yaumil qiya_mati in na lakum lama_ tahkumu_n
40.	Salhum ay yuhum biza_lika zaim
41.	Am lahum suraka_u falyatu_ bi suraka_ ihim in ka_nu_ sa_diqin
42.	Yauma yuksafu an sa_qiw wa yudauna ilas suju_di fala_ yastathiu_n
43.	Ka_siatan absa_ruhum tarhaquhum zilah wa qad ka_nu_ yudauna ilas suju_di wa hum sa_limu_n
44.	Fazami wa may yukaz zibu biha_zal hadis sanastadrijuhum min haisu la_ yalamu_n
45.	Wa umli lahum in na kaidimatin
46.	Am tas aluhum ajran fahum mim magramim mustaqalu_n
47.	Am indahumul gaibu fahum yaktubu_n
48.	Fasbirlihukmi rabika wa la_ takun kasa_hibil hu_t iz na_da_ wa huwa makzu_m
49.	Lau la_ an tada_rakahu_ nimatum mir rabihi lanubiza bil ara_ I wa huwa mazmu_m
50.	Faj taba_hu rab buhu_ fajaalahu_ minas sa_lihin
51.	Wa iy yaka_dul lazina kafaru_ layuz liqu_naka bi absa_rihim la ma_ samiuz zikra wa yaqu_lu_na in nahu_ lamajnu_n
52.	Wa ma_ huwa ila_ zikrul lil a_lamin
.EndTopic

.Topic qsAl-Ha_qqah  " 69. Al Ha_qqah"
1.	Al ha_q qah
2.	Mal ha_q qah
3.	Wa ma_ adra_ka mal ha_q qah
4.	Kazabat samu_du wa a_dum bilqa_riah
5.	Fa am ma_ samu_du fa uhiku_ bita_giyah
6.	Wa am ma_ a_dun fa uhliku_ birihin sarsarin a_tiyah
7.	Sakaraha_ alaihim saba laya_liw wa sama_niyata ay ya_min husu_man fataral qauma fiha_ sara_ ka an nahum aja_zu naklin ka_wiyah
8.	Fahal tara_ lahum min ba_qiyah
9.	Wa ja_ a firaunu wa man qablahu_ wal mutafika_tu bil ha_tiah
10.	Fa'asau rasu_la rabihim fa ahazahum ahzatar ra_biyah
11.	In na_ lam ma_ taghal ma_u hamal na_kum fil ja_riyah
12.	Linajalaha_ lakum tazkirataw taiyaha_ uzunuw wa_iyah
13.	Fa iza nufika fisuri nafkatuw wa_hidah
14.	Wa humilatil ardu wal jiba_lu faduk kata_ daktawa wa_hidah
15.	Fayauma iziwaqiatil wa_qiah
16.	Wansaq qatis sama_ u fa hiya yauma iziw wa_hiyah
17.	Wal malaku ala_  arja_ iha_  wa yahmilu arsa rabika fauqahum yauma izin sama_niyah
18.	Yauma izin turadu_na la_ takfa_ minkum ka_fiyah
19.	Fa am ma_ man u_tiya kita_bahu_ biyaminihi fayaqu_lu ha_ umuqra u_ kita_biyah
20.	Ini zanantu an ni mula_qin hisa_biyah
21.	Fahuwa fi isyatir ra_diyah
22.	Fi janatin a_liyah
23.	Quthu_fuha_ da_niyah
24.	Kulu_ wasrabu_ hani am bima_ aslafatum fil aya_mil ha_liyah
25.	Wa am ma_ man u_tiya kitabahu_ bisima_lihi fayaqu_lu ya_ laitani lam u_ta kita_biyah
26.	Wa lam adri ma_ hisa_biyah
27.	Ya_ laitaha_ ka_natil qa_diyah
28.	Ma_ agna_ an ni ma_liyah
29.	Halaka an ni sulta_niyah
30.	Kuzu_hu fagul lu_h
31.	Sumal jahima salu_h
32.	Suma fi silsilatin zaruha_ sabu_na zira_an fasluku_h
33.	Inahu_ ka_na la_ yuminu bil la_hilazim
34.	Wa la_ yahudu ala_ taa_mil miskin
35.	Falisa lahul yauma ha_huna_ hamim
36.	Wa la_ taa_mun ila_ min gislin
37.	La_ ya;kuluhu_ ila ka_ti u_n
38.	Fala_ uqsimu bima_ tubsiru_n
39.	Wa ma_ la_ tubsiru_n
40.	In nahu_ laqaula rasu_lin karim
41.	Wa ma_ huwa biqauli sa_ir qalilam ma_ tuminu_n
42.	Wa la_ biqauli ka_hin, qalilam ma_ tazak karu_n
43.	Tanzilum mir rab bil a_lamin
44.	Wa lau taqaw wala alaina_ badal aqa_wil
45.	La akazna_ minhu bil yamin
46.	Suma laqatana_ minhul watin
47.	Fama_ minkum min ahadin anhu ha_jizin
48.	Wa in nahu_ latazkiratul lil mut taqin
49.	Wa in na_ lanalamu an na minkum mukaz zibin
50.	Wa in nahu_ lahasratun alal ka_firin
51.	Wa in nahu lahaq qul yaqin
52.	Fasab bih bismi rabikal azim
.EndTopic
;___________________________________
.Topic qsAl-Ma'a_rij  " 70. Al Ma'a_rij"
1.	Sa ala sa_ ilun biaza_biw wa_qi
2.	Lilka_firina laisa lahu_ da_fi
3.	Minal la_hi zil maa_rij
4.	Tarujul mala_ ikatu war ru_hu ilaihi fi yaumin ka_na miqda_ruhu_ hamsina alfa sanah
5.	Fasbir sabran jamila_
6.	In nahum yaraunahu_ baida_
7.	Wa narahu_ qariba_
8.	Yauma taku_nus sama_u kal muhl
9.	Wa taku_nul jiba_lu kalihn
10.	Wa la_ yas alu hamimun hamima_
11.	Yubas saru_nahum yawad dul mujrimu lau yaftadi min aza_bi yaumizin bibanih
12.	Wa sa_hibatihi wa akhih
13.	Wa fasilatihil lati tuwih
14.	Wa man fil ardi jamian suma yunjih
15.	Kal la_ in naha_ laza_
16.	Naz za_atal lis sawa_
17.	Tadu_ man adbara wa tawal la_
18.	Wa jamaa fa aua_
19.	In nal insa_na huliqa halu_a_
20.	Iza mas sahus sar ru jazu_a_
21.	Wa iza mas sahul hairu manu_a_
22.	Il lal musal lin
23.	Al lazinahum ala_ sala_tihim da_imu_n
24.	Wal lazina fi amwa_lihim haq qum malu_m
25.	Lis sa_ili wal mahru_m
26.	Wal lazina yushad diqu_na biyaumidin
27.	Wal lazina hum min aza_bi rabihim musfiqu_n
28.	In na aza_ba rab bihim gairu mamu_n
29.	Wal lazina hum lifu_rujihim ha_fizu_n
30.	Il la_ ala_ az wa_jihim au ma_  malaka aima_nuhum fa in nahum gairu malu_min
31.	Famanibtaga_ wara_a za_lika fa ula_ ika humul a_du_n
32.	Wal lazina hum li ama_na_tihim waahdihim ra_u_n
33.	Wal lazina hum bisaha_da_tihim qa_ imu_n
34.	Wal lazina hum ala_ sa_la_tihim yuha_fizu_n
35.	Ula_ ika fi jan na_tim mukramu_n
36.	Fama_lil lazina kafaru_ qibalaka mutiin
37.	Anil yamini wa anis sima_li izin
38.	Ayatmau kulumrim minhum ayudkala  jan nata maim
39.	Kal la_ in na_ halaqna_hum mim ma_ yalamu_n
40.	Fala_ uqsimu birab bil masaya_riqi wal magha_ribi in na_ laqadiru_n
41.	Ala_ an nubad dila kairam minhum wa ma_ nahnu bimasbu_qin
42.	Fazarhum yaku_du_ wa yalabu_ bat ta_ yula_qu_ yaumahumul lazi yu_adu_n
43.	Yauma yakhruju_na minal ajda_si sira_an ka an nahum ila_ nusubi yu_fidu_n
44.	Ka_siatan absa_ruhum tarquhum zilah za_likal yaumul lazi ka_nu_ yu_adu_n
.EndTopic

.Topic qsNuh  " 71. Nuh"
1.	In na_ arsalna_ nu_han ila_ qaumilhi an anzir qaumaka min qabil ay yatiyahum aza_bun alim
2.	Qa_la ya_ qaumi in ni lakum nazirum mubin
3.	Anibudul la_ha wat taqu_hu wa atiu_n
4.	Yagfir lakum min zunu_bikum wa yu akhirkum ila_ ajalim musama_ in na ajalal la_hi iza_ ja_ a la_ yuakhar lau kuntum talamu_n
5.	Qa_la rab bi in ni daautu qaumi lai law wa naha_ra_
6.	Falam yazidhum dua_ i il la_ fira_ra_
7.	Wa in ni kul lama_ daautuhum litagfira lahum ja'alu_ asha_biahum fi a_za_nihim wastagsau siya_bahum wa ashar ru_ wastakbaru_s tikba_ra_
8.	Suma in ni daautuhum jiha_ra_
9.	Suma in ni alantu lahum wa asrartu lahum isra_ra_
10.	Faqultus tagfiru_ rab bakum in nahu_ ka_na gaf fa_ra_
11.	Yursilis sama_a alaikum midra_ra_
12.	Wa yumdidkum bi amwa_liw wa banina wa yajal lakum jan na_tiw wa yaj al lakum anha_ra_
13.	Ma_ lakum la_ tarju_na lil la_hi wa qa_ra_
14.	Wa qad kalaqakum atwa_ra_
15.	Alam tarau kaifa halaqal la_hu saba sama_wa_tin tiba_qa_
16.	Wa ja'alal qamara fihin na nu_raw wa ja'alas samsa sira_ja_
17.	Wal la_hu ambatakum minal ardi naba_ta_
18.	Suma yuidukum fiha_ wa yukrijukum ikhra_ja_
19.	Wal la_hu jaala lakumul arda bisa_ta_
20.	Litasluku_ minha_ subulan fija_ja_
21.	Qa_la nu_hur rabi in nahum ashauni wat tabau_ mal lam yazid hu ma_luhu_ wa waladuhu_ il la_ hasa_ra_
22.	Wa makaru_ makran kub ba_ra_
23.	Wa qa_lu_ la_ tadzarun na a_laihatakum wa la_ tadzarun na wad daw wa la_ suwa_aw wa la_ yagu_tsa wa yau_qa wa nasra_
24.	Wa qad adal lu_ katsira_ wa la_ tazidih za_limina il la_ dala_la_
25.	Mim ma_ kati a_tihim ugriqu_ faudhilu_ na_ran falam yajidu_ lahum min du_nil la_hi ansa_ra_
26.	Wa qa_la nu_hur rab bi la_ tazar alal ardi minal ka_firina day ya_ra_
27.	In naka in tazarhum yudhil lu_ iba_daka wa la_ yalidu_ il la_ fa_jiran kafa_ra_
28.	Rabigfirli wa liwa_liday ya waliman dakhala baitiya muminaw wa lil muminina walmumina_t wa la_ tazidih za_limina ai la_ taba_ra_
.EndTopic
;____________________________
.Topic qsAl-Jin  " 72. Al Jin"
1.	Qul u_hiya ilay ya an nahustamaa nafarum minal jin ni faqa_lu_ in na_ samina_ qur a_nan ajaba_
2.	Yahdi ilar rusdi fa a_man na_ bih wa lan nusrika birab bina_ ahada_
3.	Wa an nahu_ taa_la_ jad du rab bina_ mat takhaza sa_hibataw wa la_ walada_
4.	Wa an nahu_ ka_na yaqu_lu safihuna_ alal la_hi satata_
5.	Wa an na_ zanan na_ al lan taqu_lal insu wal jin nu alal la_h kaziba_
6.	Wa an nahu_ ka_na rija_lum minal insi yau_zu_na birija_lim minal jin nifaza_du_hum rahaqa_
7.	Wa an nahum zan nu_ kama_ zanantum al lay yabasal lahu_ ahada_
8.	Wa an na_ lamasna sama_a fawajadna_ha_ muliat harasan sadidaw wa suhuba_
9.	Wa an na_ kun na_ naqudu minha_ maqa_ida lis sami famay yastami ila_na yajid lahu_ siha_bar rasa da_
10.	Wa an na_la_ nadri asyar run urida biman fil ardi am ara_da bihim rabuhum rasada_
11.	Wa an na_ min nas sa_lihu_na wamin na_ du_na za_lik kun na_ tara_iqa qida_da_
12.	Wa an na_ zanan na_ alan nuji zal la_ha fil ardi wa lan nujizahu_ haraba_
13.	Wa an na_ lam ma_ saminal huda_ a_man na_ bih famay yumin birabihi fala_ yaka_fu baksaw wa la_ rahaqa_
14.	Wa an na_ minal muslimu_na wa minnal qa_situ_n faman aslama fa ula_ika tahar rau hataba_
15.	Wa am mal qa_situ_na faka_nu_ lijahan nama hataba_
16.	Wa al lawistaqa_mu_ alat tariqatila asqaina_hum ma_ an gadaqa_
17.	Linsftinahum fih, wa may yuridh an dzikri rab bihi yasluk hu adza_ban sha'ada_
18.	Wa an nal masa_jida lil la_hi fala_ tadu_ mala_hi ahada_
19.	Wa an nahu_ lam ma_ qa_ma abdul la_hi yadu_hu  ka_du_ yaku_nu_na alaihi libada_
20.	Qul in nama_ adu_ rab bi wa la_ usyriku bihi ahada_
21.	Qul in ni la_ amliku lakum dhar raw wa la_ raswyada_
22.	Qul in ni lay yujirani minal la_hi aha duw wa lan ajida min du_nihi mul tahada_
23.	Il la_ bala_gham minal la_hi wa risa_ la_tih, wa may yashil la_ha wa rasu_ lahu_ fa in na lahu_ na_ra jahan nama kha_lidina fiha_ adada_
24.	Hat ta_ idza_ ra au ma_ yu_ adu_na fayalamu_na man adhafu na_shiraw wa aqal lu adada_
25.	Qul in adri aqaribum ma_ tu_adu_na am yajalu lahu_ rab bi  amada_
26.	A_limul ghaibi fala_ yuzhhiru ala_ ghaibihi ahada_
27.	Illa manirtadha_ mir rasu_lin fa in na hu_ yasluku min baini yadaihi wa min khalfihi rashada_
28.	Liyalama an qad ablaqhu_ risa_la_ti rab bihim wa ahatha bima_ ladaihim wa ahsha_kul la syai in adada_
.EndTopic
;______________________________________
.Topic qsAl-Muzamil  " 73. Al Muzamil"
1.	Ya_ ay yuhal muz zam mil
2.	Qumil laila il la_ qalila_
3.	Nishfahu_ awinqush minhu qalila_
4.	Au zid alaihi wa rat tili qur a_na tai tila_
5.	In na_ sanulqi alaika qaulan tsaqila_
6.	In na na_syi atal laili hiya asyad du wath aw aqwamu qila_
7.	In na fin naha_ri sabhan thawi la_
8.	Wadzkurisma rab bika wa tabat tal ilaihi tabtila_
9.	Rab bul masyriqi wal maghribi la_ ila_ ha il la_ huwa tat takhidz hu wakila_
10.	Washbir ala_ ma_ yaqu_lu_na wahjur hum hajran jamila_
11.	Wa dzami wal mukadz dzibina ulin namati wa mah hilhum qalila_
12.	In na ladaina_ anka_law wa jahima_
13.	Wa tha'a_man dza_ qhush shatiw wa adza_ban alima_
14.	Yauma tarjuful ardhu wal jiba_lu wa ka_natil jiba_lu katsibam mahila_
15.	In na_ arsalna_ ilaikum rasu_lan sya_ hidan alaikum kama_ arsalna_ firauna rasu_la_
16.	Fa'asha_ firaunur rasu_la fa akhadz na_hu akhdzaw wabila_
17.	Fakaifa tat taqu_na in kafartum yau may yajalul wilda_na syiha_
18.	As sama_ u munfathirun bih, ka_na waduhu_ mafu_la_
19.	In na ha_dzihi tadzkiratun faman sya_ at takhadza ila_ rab bihi sabila_
20.	In na rab baka yalamu an naka taqu_ mu adna_ min tsulutsayil laili wa nish fahu_ wa tsulutsahu_ wa tha_ ifatum minal ladzina maak, wal la_hu yu qad dirul laila wan naha_r, alima al lan tuhshu_hu fata_ba alaikum faqra u_ ma_ tayas sara minal qura_n, alima an sayaku_nu minkum mardha_ wa a_ kharu_na yadhribu_na fil ardhi yabta qhu_na min fadhlil la_hi wa a_kharu_ na yuqa_tilu_na fi sabilil la_h, faqra u_ ma_ taya sara minhu wa aqimush shala_fa wa a_tuz zaka_ta wa aqridhul la_ha qardhan hasana_, wa ma tuqad dimu_ li anfusikum min khairin tajidu_hu  indal la_hi huwa khairin wa azhama ajra_, wastagfirul la_h, in nal la_ha ghafu_ru_r rahim 
.EndTopic
;__________________________________________
.Topic qsAl-Muddatstsir  " 74. Al Muddatstsir"

Wa ma_ jaalna_ asha_ban na_ri il la_ mala_ikataw wa ma_ ja'alna_ id datahum il la_ fitnatal lil lazina kafaru_ liyastaiqinal lazina u_tul kita_ba wa yazda_dal lazina a_manu_ ima_naw wa la_ yarta_bal lazina u_tul kita_ba wal muminu_na wa liyaqu_lal lazina fi qulu_bihim maraduw wal ka_firu_na ma_za_ ara_dal la_hu biha_za_ masala_ kaza_lika yudhilul la_hu may yasya_u wa yahdi may yasya_  wa ma_ yalamu junu_da rab buka il la_ huw wa ma_ hiya il la_ zikra_ lilbasyar

38.	Kul lu nafsin bima_ kasabat rahinah
39.	Il la_ asha_bal yamin
40.	Fi jan na_tin yatasa_ alu_n
41.	Anil mujrimin
42.	Ma_ salakakum fi saqar

44.	Wa lam naku nutihumul miskin
45.	Wa kun na_ naku_du ma'al ka_idin
46.	Wa kun na_ nukaz zibu bi yaumidin
47.	Hat ta_ ata_nal yaqin
48.	Fama_ tanfauhum safa_'atus sa_fiin
49.	Fama_ lahum anit tazkirati muridin
50.	Ka an nahum humurum mustanfirah
51.	Far rat min qaswarah
52.	Bal yuridu kul lum ri in minhum ay yuta_ suhufam munas sarah
53.	Kal la_ bal la_ yakha_fu_nal a_khirah
54.	Kal la_ in nahu_ tazkirah
55.	Faman sa_ a zakarah
56.	Wa ma_ yazkuru_na il la_ ay yasya_ al la_h huwa ahlut taqwa_ wa ahlul magfirah
.EndTopic

.Topic qsAl-Qiya_mah  " 75. Al Qiya_mah"
1.	La_ uqsimu biyaumi qiya_mah
2.	Wa la_ uqsimu bin nafsil law wa_mah
3.	Ayahsabul insa_nu al lan najmaa iza_mah
4.	Bala_ qa_dirina ala_ an nusaw wiya bana_nah
5.	Bal yuridul insa_nu liyafjura ama_mah
6.	Yas alu ay ya_na yaumul qiya_mah
7.	Fa iza_ bariqal basar
8.	Wa kasafal qamar
9.	Wa jumias samsu wal qamar
10.	Yaqu_lul insa_nu yauma izin ainal mafar
11.	Kal la_ la_ wazar
12.	Ila_ rab bika yauma izinil mustaqar
13.	Yunab baul insa_nu yauma izin bi ma_ qad dama wa akhar
14.	Balil insa_nu ala_ nafsihi basirah
15.	Wa lau alqa_ maa_zirah
16.	La_ tuharik bihi lisa_naka litajalabih
17.	In na alaina_ jamahu_ wa qura_nah
18.	Fa iza_ qarana_hu fat tabi qur a_nah
19.	Suma in na alaina_ baya_nah
20.	Kal la_ bal tuhib bu_nal a_jilah
21.	Wa tazaru_nal a_khirah
22.	Wuju_huy yauma izin na_dirah
23.	Ila_ rab biha_ na_zirah
24.	Wa wuju_huy yauma izin
25.	Tazun nu ay yufala biha_ fa_qirah
26.	Kal la_ iza_ balagatit tara_qi
27.	Wa qila man ra_q
28.	Wa zana an nahul fira_q
29.	Wal taf fatis sa_qu bis sa_q
30.	Ila_ rab bika yauma izinil masa_q
31.	Fala_ sad daqa wa la_ sal la_
32.	Wa la_kin kaz zaba wa tawal la_
33.	Suma zahaba ila_ ahlihi yatamat ta_
34.	Aula_ laka fa aula_
35.	Suma aula_ laka fa aula_
36.	Ayahsabul insa_nu ay yutraka suda_
37.	Alam yaku nuthfatam mim maniy yiy yumna_
38.	Suma ka_na alaqatan fakalaqa fasaw wa_
39.	Faja'ala minhuz zaujainiz zakara wal unsa_
40.	Alaisa za_lika biqa_dirin ala_ ay yuhyiyal mauta_
.EndTopic
;________________________________
.Topic qsAl-Insa_n  " 76. Al Insa_n"
1.	Hal ata_ alal insa_ni himun minad dahri lam yakun saiam mazku_ra_
2.	In na_ halaqnal insa_na min nutfatin amsya_jin nabtalihi faja'alna_hu sami'an basira_
3.	In na_ hadaina_hus sabila im ma_ sya_ kiraw wa im ma_ kafu_ra_
4.	In na_ atadna_ lika_firina sala_sila wa aqhla_law wa saira_
5.	In nal abra_ra yasyrabu_na min kasin ka_na miza_juha_ ka_fu_ra_
6.	Ainay yasyrabu  biha_ iba_dul la_hi yufaj jiru_naha_ tafjira_
7.	Yu_funa bin nadzri wa yakha_funa yauman ka_na syar ruhu_ mustathira_
8.	Wa yuthimu_nath thaa_ma ala_ hub bihi miskinaw wa yatimaw wa asira_
9.	In nama_ nuthimukum liwajhil la_hi lanuridu minkum jaza_ aw wa la_ syuku_ra_
10.	In na_ nakha_fu mir rah bina_ yauman abu_san qamtharira_
11.	Fawaqa_humul la_hu syar ra dza_likal yaumi wa laq qa_hum nadhataw wa suru_ra_
12.	Wa jaza_hum bima_ sabaru_jan nataw wa harira_
13.	Mut taki ina fiha_ alal ara_ iki la_ yarauna fiha_ syamsaw wa la_ zamharira_
14.	Wa da_niyatan alaihim zila_luha_ wa zulilat qutufuha_ tazlila
15.	Wa yuta_fu alaihim bi a_niyatiw wa akwa_bin ka_nar  qawa_rira_
16.	Qawa_rira min fidatin qad daru_ha_ taqdira_
17.	Wa yusqauna fiha_ kasan ka_na miza_juha_ zanjabila_
18.	Ainan fiha_ tusam ma_ salsabila_
19.	Wa yatu_fu alaihim wilda_num mukal ladu_na iza_ ra aitahum hasibtahum luluam mansu_ra_
20.	Wa iza_ ra aita sam ma ra aita naimaw wa mulkan kabira_
21.	A_liyahum siya_bu sundusin hudruw wa istabraquw wa hul lu_ asa_wira min fid dah wa saqa_hum rab buhum sara_ban tahu_ra_
22.	In na ha_za_ ka_na lakum jaza_ aw wa ka_na sayukum masku_ra_
23.	In na_ nahnu naz zalna_ alaikal qur a_na tanzila_
24.	Fashbir lihukmi rab bika wa la_ tuthi minhum a_tsiman au kafu_ra_
25.	Wadzkurisma rab bika bukrataw wa ashila_
26.	Wa minal laili tasjud lahu_ wa sab bih hu lailan  thawila_
27.	In na ha_ ula_ I yuhub bu_nal a_jilata wa yadzaru_na wa ra_ ahum   yauman tsaqila_
28.	Nahnu khalaqna_hum wa syadadna_ asrahum wa idza_ syina bad dalna_ amtsa_lahum tabdila_
29.	In na ha_dzihi tadzkiratun faman sya_at takhadza ila_  rab bihi sabila
30.	Wa ma_ tsya_ u_na il la_ ay yasya_ al la_h, in nal la_ha ka_na aliman hakima_
31.	Yudkhilu may yasya_ u fi rahmatihi wazha_limina a'ad da  lahum adza_ ban alima_
.EndTopic
;_____________________________________
.Topic qsAl-Mursala_t  " 77. Al Mursala_t"

34.	Wailuy yauma izil lilmukaz zibin

44.	In na_ kaza_lika najzil muhsinin
45.	Wailuy yauma izil lilmukaz zibin
46.	Kulu_ wa tamat tau_ qalilan in nakum mujrimu_n
47.	Wailuy yauma izil limukaz zibin
48.	Wa iza_ qila lahumur kau_ la_ yarkau_n
49.	Wailuy yauma izin lilmukaz zibin
50.	Fabi ay yi hadisim badahu_ yuminu_n
.EndTopic

.Topic qsAl-Insyiqaq  " 84. Al Insyiqaq"

.Topic qsAl-Buruj  " 85. Al Buruj"
1.	Wa sama_i za_til buru_j
2. 	Wal yaumul mauu_d
3. 	Wa sya_hidi wa masyhu_d
4. 	Qutila asha_bul ukhdu_d
5. 	An na_ri za_til waqu_d
6. 	Izhum alaiha_ qu'u_d
7. 	Wa hum ala_ ma_ yafalu_na bil muminina syuhu_d
8. 	Wa ma_ naqamu_ minhum ila_ ayuminu_ bil la_hi azizil hamid

11.	Inalazina a_manu_ wa amilusha_liha_ti lahum jana_tun tajri min tahtihal anha_r za_likal fauzul kabir
12.	Ina batsa rabika tasadid
13.	Inahu_ huwa yubdi u wa yu id
14.	Wa huwal gafu_rul wadu_d
15.	Zul arsyil majid
16.	Fa'a_lul lima_ yurid
17.	Hal ata_ka hadisul junu_d
18.	Firauna wa samu_d

.Topic qsAl-Bayyinah  " 98. Al Bayyinah"
